(Ki) mua (o te tangata).
(Tētahi hanga) kua whakahuatia, kua tohua rānei i mua, ka noho hei kaupapa mō te kōrero ka whai ake.
(Tō Te Waipounamu) He manu iti noho ngahere, noho ururua, he kōiraira mā kei runga ake i ngā ngutu o te toa, he pakohe te upoko, te kakī me ngā kaokao o te tinana, he pango ngā remu a runga, he mā a raro, he kōwhai te uma, he kōwhai mā te puku, he karu pango, he parauri pango ngā ngutu me ngā waewae, he kōwhai ngā raparapa. He iti iho te hanga o te uwha, he parauri ake a runga, he iti iho ngā wāhi kōwhai o raro. (Tō Te Ika-a-Māui) He tāhekeheke mā kei te upoko me ngā taha o te tinana, he huruhuru kiwikiwi whai tāingoingo mā kei ngā pāpāringa me te taha whakarunga o te uma, he mā te taha whakararo o te uma, te puku me te taha whakararo o te hūmaeko, he kōwhai parauri ngā waewae, he kōwhai ngā raparapa.
(Ētahi hanga) kua whakahuatia, kua tohua rānei i mua, ka noho hei kaupapa mō te kōrero ka whai ake.
A mua, kaua a muri.
A muri, tērā atu taha rānei.
A roto rawa o Papatūānuku, te wāhi o te whenua e tawhiti tonu ana i te mata.
A te tangata, o te tangata e tohua ana, nāna tūturu, nōna tūturu rānei.
A waenganui o te takurua.
A waenganui pū o te takurua.
A waenganui rawa o tētahi mea, te wāhi kei waenganui rawa o tētahi mea.
Ahakoa kāore tonu he take (i pērā ai).
Ahakoa te kore e āta whai kia pērā.
Arā noa atu (te wā ka taka).
E  maha ana, e tini ana (o ngā hanga moroiti).
E ai ki ngā kōrero tuku iho, he kararehe, he tipua, ko tōna hanga he whakamataku.
E angiangi ana, e pingohe ana, e kōpīpī ana rānei, me te aha, tērā ka kino noa, ka pakaru noa ki te kore e whāwhātia, e mahia i runga i te tūpato.
E apiapi ana te noho mai i te pēpēhitanga kia whāiti mai ki tētahi wāhi iti iho.
E aro nui atu ana, e whakarongo atu ana.
E aroha ana, e ngākau pai ana (ki te tangata).
E aroha nuitia ana.
E auau ana te puta, te mahia rānei.
E eke ana (tētahi āhuatanga) ki tētahi taumata teitei, e kaha ana, e rahi ana.
E haere ana mō tētahi wā roa.
E haere tonu ana mō ake tonu atu; kāore e mutu.
E haitutu ana, e mahana ana, (o ngā rangi).
E hakahaka ana te takoto mai (o te whenua).
E harikoa ana te wairua, me te pukukōrero anō.
E heke haere ana (tētahi mata), i te mea he teitei ake tētahi pito i tētahi.
E hia kē ina tatauria.
E hia kē nei ina tatauria, arā, he tino maha.
E hiahia ana ki tētahi mea, e hiakai ana rānei ki tētahi mea.
E hoihoi ana, e taikaha ana te reo.
E hono ana tēnei kupu i ētahi rerenga e rua, me te tohu ko te mea tuarua he momo whakamārama, he momo whakapuaki tuarua rānei i te mea tuatahi.
E honoa ana a waenganui (o ngā matimati o te waewae) ki te kiri.
E houhou ana ki te korokoro, kāore i reka.
E hua ana (ngā kai o te mahinga).
E huhua ana ōna wāhanga e hono tahi ana; ka roa tonu e wānangatia ana e mārama ai, e kitea ai te tikanga.
E hāngai ana, e tika ana, mō tētahi tangata, mō tētahi kaupapa, mō tētahi wā rānei.
E hāngai ana, e tōtika ana ki ngā whakaaro o te tangata.
E hāngai pū ana te taupatupatu (o ētahi mea e rua).
E hātea ana, e āhua mā ana te tae.
E hē ana te āhua, te hanga rānei (o te tinana), arā, kāore i rite ki te āhua, ki te hanga e tika ana.
E hōhonu ana (o te awa, o te moana, o tētahi atu takotoranga wai rānei).
E hōhonu ana, e hakahaka ana, e kaitara ana rānei (o te reo).
E hōhonu ana, e whāiti ana (o te ipu).
E hōhā ana, e whakatakariri ana rānei i te roa rawa e tatari ana ki tētahi mea, arā, kāore i manawanui.
E iti ake ana te tupu i tērā e tika ana (o te tangata, te kararehe rānei).
E iti ana ngā rawa, ngā moni, ngā aha atu e pai ai te noho.
E iti ana te kiko, e iti ana rānei te mōmona; e iti ana te mōmona me te tāroaroa anō.
E iti ana te tae o roto, kāore i uriuri, i mumura rānei.
E iti ana te tawhiti mai i tētahi taha ki tētahi (o tētahi hanga), ina whakaritea ki tōna roa.
E iti noa ana (o tētahi mea ora).
E iti noa ana te piki me te heke (o te tai), arā, kāore i pērā rawa te rerekētanga o te hōhonu i te tūnga mai, i te timunga rānei.
E kaha ana (te tangata) ki te kōrero mō ōna, mō āna, kia nui ai ia i waenga i ētahi atu.
E kaha ana ki te hora i te kai tino pai rawa atu, tino nui rawa atu.
E kaha ana ki te mahi.
E kaha ana te hononga (o tētahi ki tētahi atu).
E kaha ana te minamina tote.
E kaha ana te mingimingi, te kopakopa (o te makawe).
E kaha ana te mā.
E kaha ana te tuku aho, te whakaata aho rānei.
E kaha ana, e hiahia ana rānei ki te tākaro, ki te pārekareka, ki te whakangahau.
E kaha ana, e nui ana; e eke ana (tētahi āhuatanga) ki tētahi taumata teitei.
E kaha ana, e rahi ana.
E kaha ana, kua kaha kē atu rānei i te tuinga mai, i te urunga mai o tētahi atu hanga.
E kahurangi uriuri ana te tae.
E kaikā ana ki te rīriri, ki te whawhai me te whakatumatuma anō.
E kaingākautia ana, e noho taonga ana ki te tangata.
E kakama ana ki te neke, ki te mahi i tētahi mahi, he ringa rehe anō hoki.
E kanapa ana i te mea e whakaata ana, e whakaputa ana i te aho.
E kapi ana (tētahi mata) i tētahi tae hātea nei.
E kapi ana i te kōhao moroiti e uru atu ai te wai, te hau rānei.
E kapi katoa ana (te kanohi) i te moko.
E kapi katoa ana i te huruhuru.
E kapi katoa ana i te hāware, e rite ana rānei ki te hāware ki te whāwhā atu.
E kapi katoa ana i te rimurimu.
E kapi katoa ana i te tāekaeka poto, āhua tipirori nei.
E kapi katoa ana.
E kawea ana mō te katoa o ngā hāora o te wiki e rite ana (mō taua mahi, mō taua kaupapa rānei), kāore i harangotengote.
E kawea ana, e tū ana i te wā tonu e kawea ana, e tū ana tētahi atu mea.
E kikorangi teatea ana te tae.
E kimi riri ana, e rite ana rānei ki te riri, he toheriri, he kairiri.
E kitea ana tōna takenga mai, e tika ana kia āta arohia ake, e whai mana ana.
E kitea atu ana tōna whānui me tōna roa, e mōhiotia ana rānei he āhuatanga pērā ōna, engari kāore kau ōna hōhonutanga, ōna teitei rānei.
E kitea atu ana tōna whānui me tōna roa, tae atu anō ki tōna hōhonutanga, tōna teitei rānei, e mōhiotia ana rānei he āhuatanga pērā ōna.
E kitea nuitia ana, e puta ake ana i ia rā, i ia rā, kāore i tauhou.
E kiwikiwi mā ana te tae.
E kohu ana.
E kopa ana (te papa) i te wera o te rā, i te haukū rānei.
E kopa ana (te waewae) arā, kāore te kapu o te waewae e tau tika atu ki te whenua.
E kopa ana (tētahi wāhi o te tinana) arā, kāore i rite te tipu ki tērā e tika ana.
E kopa ana, e takawiri ana, kāore e rere tōtika ana.
E kore ai (te tangata, te aha atu) e whara, e pākia rānei e tētahi āhuatanga kino.
E kore e taea te tatau i te tino maha rawa atu.
E kore e taea te whakatau te uara, te wāriu, inā kē te puiaki, te noho taonga mai.
E kore e tino kitea i te kore e tino puta ake, whakamīharo ana, whakawehi ana.
E korekore ana te kai.
E koromeke ana, e awhi ana rānei ngā ringa me ngā waewae i te tinana.
E koropuku ana a runga, e kopa ana rānei (o te tuarā).
E koropungapunga ana, e kōpūtoitoi ana (o te rākau).
E kotiti ana, e hē ana te kawenga, te putanga rānei (o tētahi āhuatanga).
E kā ana, e kanapa ana.
E kākāriki teatea ana te tae.
E kī ana i te huahua, i te pukupuku.
E kī katoa ana i te kaka, i te weu, ko te kaka, ko te weu rānei te rite.
E kōataata ana, kāore i kauehu.
E kōpuku ana, e porotaka ana te pito.
E kōwhai teatea ana te tae, pērā i te kirīmi.
E kūngenge ana, arā, kāore i pāraharaha, i tautika (o te raranga, o te whatu).
E maha ana ngā aho, ngā wāhanga o roto.
E maha ana ngā kōruarua i te mata, ngā kōhao rānei o roto.
E maha ana ngā āputa, ngā mokotawhā (i tētahi mea).
E maha ana, e mātotoru ana ngā peka, me ngā rau.
E maha tonu ana ngā hanga koi i te mata.
E mahana ana, me te tatū o te ngākau i te pai.
E mahi ana kia māreparepa, kia karekare (te wai).
E mahi ana, e mahia ana rānei i runga i te aroha ki te tangata, ki te kaupapa rānei.
E makariri ana, e haukū ana, me te hāpiapia anō pea.
E makariri ana, e uru atu ana anō te hau ki roto (o te whare).
E mamae kore ana.
E manauri ana (o te kiko o te kūmara me te rīwai).
E manauri ana pērā i te kamorā.
E maramara rikiriki ana, me te puehu, me te kānga, te pata witi kua tukitukia.
E maroke ana, me te mōwhakiwhaki anō (o te papa, o te rākau).
E maroke ana; kua mārō, kua maroke i te roa e takoto ana i te rā, i tētahi wāhi wera rānei; kua wera i te ahi, kua tunua rānei kia kōtihetihe.
E mataku ana, e āmaimai ana, e whakamā ana rānei i mua i ētahi atu.
E matatau ana ki ētahi reo e rua; e rere tahi ana ngā reo e rua.
E mau pūmau ana, e kore e taea te neke.
E mauri tau ana, kua kore e tino wehi i te tangata, ka taea te whakatata atu (o te kararehe, o te manu).
E mingimingi ana, e kopakopa ana, e pūkorukoru ana rānei.
E mura pai ana, e pai ana te kā (o te ahi).
E mā ana te tae (o te makawe, o te huru manu, o te huru kararehe).
E mā ana, e pīata ana, e kanapa ana i te kore e rere o te paru i roto (o te wai).
E mākohakoha ana, kāore he wāhi taratara, he pukupuku, me te pīataata anō.
E mākū ana, e makariri ana.
E mākū ana, e tāpokopoko ana (o te whenua).
E mākūkū ana, e kurupetipeti ana.
E mākūkū ana, e takawai ana, e kōreporepo ana.
E māmā ana ki te whakapiko, e kore e whati.
E māmā ana te kitea atu o te tikanga (o te kōrero).
E māmā ana te rōnaki (o te tuanui), kāore i poupou.
E māmā ana te rōnaki o te tuanui, kāore i poupou.
E mārakerake ana, kāore he whakamarumaru.
E mārama ana te kitea atu, kāore he mea e whakararu ana i te tirohanga atu.
E mārama ana te titiro, te kite, te kitea.
E mārō ana (o te takere o te repo).
E mārō ana, e kaitara ana.
E mārō ana, e toro whakawaho ana.
E mārō ana, e whai ngoi ana, me uaua ka pakaru, ka whati, ka motu, ka whara rānei.
E mārō ana, kāore i ngahoro, i pakaru rikiriki noa (o te oneone).
E mātotoru ana, e kaha ana ki te ārai atu i te wai, i te aha atu rānei (o te papanga, o te kiri).
E mātotoru ana, e nui ana te kiko, e mōmona ana.
E mātotoru ana, e tuawhiti ana ngā rau me ngā tātā (o tētahi tipu) i te kī i te wai; e reka ana ki te kai, e ngohengohe ana, e waiwai ana;
E mōhio ana ki te tinihanga, ki te whakawai hoki.
E mōhio ana me pēhea te nukarau i tētahi atu e tutuki ai te whāinga, te hiahia.
E mōhiotia whānuitia ana, e kōrerotia ana puta noa.
E ngaro ana ētahi wāhi, e tupurangi ana, e hukihuki ana.
E ngaro ana, e hiahiatia ana (tētahi mea).
E ngau ana ki te arero, pēnei i te wai o te pūhā mata.
E ngau ana ki te arero, pērā i te rēmana.
E ngehe ana, e ngoikore ana.
E ngenge ana me te mamae anō.
E ngenge ana, e mamae ana te tinana, nā te nui rawa o te whakapau kaha.
E ngohe ana, e tārewa kau ana; kāore e mārō, e tū mārō rānei.
E ngohengohe ana, e pōareare ana, e māmā ana, e rite ana ki te pūkohu, ki te hautai rānei te hanga.
E ngohengohe ana, e tautau ana, e tāreparepa ana (o te kiko me te mōmona o te tinana tangata).
E ngohengohe ana; e ngāwari noa ana te kopenu.
E ngoikore ana ngā turi, ngā pona.
E ngoikore ana te tupu, (o te tipu, o te rākau) kāore i matomato.
E ngoikore ana, e ngenge ana, kua kore e tino kaha.
E ngoikore ana, e parure ana (o te tangata kua warea e te moe).
E ngākau hao ana, kāore e mutu te toro o te ringa ki te tango tonu māna.
E ngākau kōpīpī ana, e āhua mataku ana.
E ngāwari ana, e haukū ana (o te oneone).
E ngāwari ana, kāore e tere riri, ka whai whakaaro ki ētahi atu, me te ngākau whakaiti anō.
E noho ana hei mea nui rawa, e noho mātāmua mai ana.
E noho ana, e haere ana (te mea kotahi, ko ia anake), e kawea ana (e te mea kotahi, ko ia anake).
E noho kau ana, kāore he mea e whakakākahu ana, e whakapaipai ana i a ia.
E noho mai ana he momo hakihaki ki runga (i te kiri), ki roto rānei (i te waha, i te puku, i hea atu), he hakihaki kāore e tere mahu ake.
E noho mai ana he puku ki runga, ki te pito rānei.
E noho mai ana hei tūāpapa, hei wāhanga matua.
E noho mai ana i te taha o tētahi atu mea, e pā ana rānei ngā tapa ki tētahi atu mea.
E noho mai ana te kūwaha ki te taha.
E noho mai ana te āhua, he maramara rānei o tētahi hanga nō tua whakarere mai anō ki te kōhatu, ki te toka, kua whakakōhatutia.
E noho mākū ana (te whenua, te oneone) me te aha, kua huri ki te paru, ki te kene.
E noho mātāmua mai ana.
E noho tahi ana, e haere tahi ana (i runga i te maha e tohua ana i te wāhanga tuarua o te kupu), e kawea tahitia ana rānei (e te maha e tohua ana i te wāhanga tuarua o te kupu).
E noho tahi ana, e haere tahi ana (o ētahi mea e rua), e kawea tahitia ana (e ētahi mea e rua).
E noho tahi ana, e haere tahi ana (o ētahi mea maha), e kawea tahitia ana (e ētahi mea maha).
E noho tuarua mai ana, e tautoko ana i te hanga tuatahi, i te hanga mātāmua.
E noho tuwhera ana.
E noho wātea ana, kāore he aha o roto.
E noho wātea ana, kāore i raro i tētahi here.
E nui ana te aho, kāore i pōuri (o tētahi wāhi).
E nui ana te auahi, e kī katoa ana i te auahi.
E nui ana te hau takiwā o roto me te hauhau anō.
E nui ana te kiko o te tinana, he taumaha anō.
E nui ana te mana, e rongonui ana, he momo kāore e tino kitea.
E nui ana te pai.
E nui ana te wai kei runga (i te whenua), kua hōpua rānei te wai.
E nui ana te wai o roto.
E nui ana ōna hua.
E nui ana, e matomato ana te tipu o ngā mea katoa i reira (o te whenua, te oneone).
E nui tonu ana te whakapau kaha e tutuki ai (tētahi mahi).
E ohorere ana te mauri, e wehi ana, kāore e mōhio me aha.
E pai ana te rere (o ngā kupu o te waiata) ki te taringa.
E pai ana te tinana, te wairua, me te hinengaro, kāore e pāria ana e te mate.
E pai ana te wera, arā, kāore i pāwera, i pōkākā, kāore hoki i makariri.
E pai ana, e mārō ana te tupu o ngā io, o ngā uaua.
E pakari ana te tupu.
E paku haere ana te tinana, e ngoikore ana i te pāngia e te mate, i te kore kai, i te kore rānei e kai.
E paku rerekē ana te tae o ngā āpure me ngā tāekaeka (o tētahi mea), me te mea nei kua ukuparatia atu ngā tae.
E papatahi ana, me te whānui anō pea (o te ihu).
E parauri teatea ana te tae.
E parauri uriuri ana te tae.
E parori ana, kāore e hangarite ana.
E piko ana ngā turi.
E piko ana, e ānau ana, e pewa ana.
E piko whakawaho ana ngā waewae i ngā turi.
E piri tata ana, e pūmau ana te tautoko, te noho hei hoa (ki tētahi atu).
E pono ana, e tūturu ana, kāore e whakataruna ana.
E poroporo teatea ana te tae.
E porotaka ana a runga, tētahi atu wāhi rānei ōna, kāore he koinga, he tapa koi rānei.
E poto ana te tipu (o te taro).
E poupou ana te rōnaki (o te tuanui).
E puare tonu ana, kāore e tūtaki ana.
E pupuhi ana, e kōpuku ana, e kunekune ana (o te puku).
E puta ake ana, e tū ana rānei mō tētahi wā poto noa.
E puta tahi mai ana, me te mea nei rānei e puta tahi mai ana, i te ihu me te waha (o te reo kōrero, o te oro).
E pā ana ki ngā nekeneke, ki ngā mahi kāwanatanga e whakahaeretia ai tētahi whenua, tētahi rohe rānei, me ngā mahi a te hunga koirā tā rātou mahi.
E pā ana ki ngā tāngata o Ingarangi, ki ngā āhuatanga, ki te whenua o Ingarangi; ngā tāngata tonu o Ingarangi.
E pā ana ki ngā āhuatanga o te kawa whakamoe i te tāne me te wahine.
E pā ana ki te ao pakihi, ki te hoko mai me te hoko atu i ngā rawa, i ngā ratonga, e riro mai ai he moni.
E pā ana ki te hāhi Karaitiana whānui, e ai ki ngā kōrero kāore i mawehe i tētahi atu hāhi, mai i tōna tīmatanga; he pononga nō te hāhi Katorika.
E pā ana ki te mātai i te rangi, i ngā nekeneke o ngā whetū, o ngā aorangi, tae atu hoki ki ngā tohu o te rangi.
E pā ana ki te noho tahi a te tangata ki ētahi atu, ki te hapori, ki te iwi whānui rānei.
E pā ana ki te pokapū o te ngota me ōna āhuatanga, ki te pūngao rānei ka hua ake ina wehea te karihi o te ngota, ina honoa rānei ki te karihi o tētahi atu ngota.
E pā ana ki te tangata kotahi, ki a ia tonu, ki ana mahi, ki ana rawa.
E pā ana ki te āhua o tētahi reo - ōna kupu, ōna whakatakoto tika, tae atu ki ōna oro.
E pā ana ki te ōhanga.
E pā ana, e hāngai ana ki tētahi kaupapa kotahi, ki tētahi mea kotahi, kāore e whānui ana te aronga.
E pā kaha ana, e pā taikaha ana, e pā tino kino ana rānei.
E pā noa ana ki ngā āhuatanga matua, kaua ki ngā āhuatanga whāiti (o tētahi mea).
E pāhikahika ana i te noho mai o te tonatona, o te riwha, o tētahi momo tōrōkiri rānei ki te mata, kāore i māene.
E pāpaku ana (o te anga pāua me ērā atu mea).
E pāpaku ana (o te wai e hora ana i te taikoraha).
E pāpaku ana, e mimiti haere ana rānei (o te kōawa).
E pārekareka ana (te hā o te kai, o te aha atu) ki te arero.
E pārekareka ana (te hā o te kai, o te aha atu) ki te ihu.
E pātai ana i te āhua o tētahi mea, e kimi whakamārama ana.
E pātai ana kia tohua mai tētahi tangata, tētahi mea rānei e whakaritea ana ki te tangata.
E pātai ana kia tohua mai tētahi wāhi.
E pātai ana kia āta tohua, kia tautuhitia tētahi mea.
E pātai ana mō te wā e tū ai, e eke ai, e pā ai rānei tētahi āhuatanga.
E pātai ana mō te āhua, mō te whai take o tētahi āhuatanga.
E pātai ana mō tētahi mea - tōna āhua, tōna ora, tōna rahi, te āhua o te whakamahi, te aha atu, te aha atu.
E pēpēhia ana te wairua, e pōuri ana, e māharahara ana, ko te tinana rānei e pēpēhia ana e tētahi whakararu.
E pōruru ana te kāuru (o te rākau).
E pōturi ana te haere, te rere.
E pōuri ana (ngā kapua) tērā pea ka ua.
E pōuri ana (o te wai).
E pōuriuri ana, pērā i ngā kapua i te pānga mai o te āwhā, perā i te wai hōhonu rānei.
E pōwhīwhiwhi ana i te kore e herua, i te kore e āta tiakina (o ngā makawe, o te huruhuru).
E pūhihi ana, e rauangi ana pērā i ngā weu o te whītau.
E pūhore ana, kāore e whai hua ana (te haere ki te hī ika, ki te hao ika).
E pūhuki ana, kāore he kāniwha (o te matau).
E pūmau ana te maungārongo, e hora ana te rangimārie, kua tū te tatau pounamu.
E pūmā ana (o te makawe me te huruhuru kararehe).
E pūwhero ana te kiri, te kanohi rānei.
E rahi ana te hanga o ngā kongakonga (o te onepū, o te oneone, o tētahi atu mea pēnei rānei).
E rahi ana te hanga, e tino papai ana rānei (o te kai).
E rahi tonu ana, e pakari tonu ana te hanga (o te tinana); e porotaka ana, e mōmona ana (o te tinana).
E rangona ai te reo me ngā hiahia o te motu whānui, o te iwi whānui i roto i ngā whakahaere (o te kāwanatanga, o tētahi atu mana whakahaere rānei).
E rangona atu ana (e te taringa) engari kāore e mārama ana te rangona atu.
E rawe ana ki te ngākau, ki te karu, ki te taringa rānei.
E rehu ana, arā, kāore e mārama pū ana, e hāngai ana rānei (o te kōrero, o te tikanga).
E reka ana ki te taringa (o te waiata, o te reo waiata, o te tangi); he tangata e pēnei ana tana reo waiata.
E rere tahi ana me te ōrite pū o te ahunga, e kore rawa e tūtaki, e tawhiti kē atu rānei tētahi i tētahi.
E rere tonu ana te waiora i roto, arā, kāore anō i mate.
E rere whakapae ana, e rere hauroki ana rānei ki te kakano matua (o te rākau, o te papa), e kotiti ana rānei.
E rerekē ana i tērā e mōhiotia nuitia ana, e kitea nuitia ana, e whakaaetia nuitia ana.
E rerekē ana ngā tae i tēnā wāhi, i tēnā wāhi (o tētahi mea).
E rerekē ana ngā tae i tēnā āpure, i tēnā āpure.
E riko ana, e paruparu ana (o te tangata, te kākahu, te aha atu), e noho ana rānei i roto i te paru, i te riko.
E rite ana ki ngā huruhuru i te uma o te pūkeko te tae.
E rite ana ki te 'he rite ki'.
E rite ana ki te 'kaua e', ki te 'kaua rawa e' rānei.
E rite ana ki te hua maoa o te karaka te tae.
E rite ana ki te karaka me te parauri, te kōwhai rānei me te parauri kua ranua, e rite ana ki te waikura te tae.
E rite ana ki te kupu 'mō', ki te 'e pā ana ki' rānei.
E rite ana ki te oneone, ki te wahie rānei te tae.
E rite ana ki te toto hauora te tae.
E rite ana ki te waro, ki te pō mārama kore te tae.
E rite ana ki te whero kōmā te tae.
E rite ana, e eke ana ki tērā e hiahiatia ana, e whakaaetia ana, e manakohia ana.
E rite tonu ana te pāngia e te mate, kāore e tino ora ana.
E roa ana, kāore e haere tika atu ana (o te ara, o te haere).
E roha ana, e whānui ana te takahi (o te rākau).
E rua i te wā kotahi.
E rua ngā apa (o te kākahu).
E rua ngā mata koi, e rua ngā pito koi, e rua rānei ngā whakamahinga (o te taputapu, o te rākau whawhai).
E rua ngā tihi.
E rua rā i mua atu.
E rua whakaraunga te nui ake, e piri tahi ana rānei (ētahi mea e rua).
E rua, neke atu rānei ōna wāhanga motuhake kua hono tahi.
E rōnaki ana, e tere ana, e māmā ana te haere.
E tae atu ana, e tauawhi ana, e pā ana, e hāngai ana rānei ki te maha atu, ki te katoa rānei.
E taea ana (te maitai) te kukume kia oti mai ai he waea angiangi me te kore tonu e motu.
E taea ana (te maitai) te paopao, te pēpēhi kia rerekē te hanga me te kore tonu e whati, e pakaru rānei.
E tahuri ana ki te whakararu i tētahi atu, i runga i te wairua whakatoi, i te wairua ngahau.
E taikaha ana, e kairiri ana te āhua o te kawe (a te tangata, a te kararehe rānei) i a ia, tana āhua, tana mahi rānei.
E takahi ana i te ture, e taea ana te whiu i raro i te ture; he mahi e pēnei ana te āhua.
E takoto ana i te tuarā kia anga whakarunga te kanohi.
E takoto ana, e tupu haere ana me te piri tahi ki te whenua (o te tipu).
E takoto mai ana he haenga roroa, he wāhi hāpua roroa rānei (ki tētahi mata).
E takoto mai ana ki ōna anō koropewa.
E takoto mai ana ā-koropewa nei.
E takoto pai ana, e takoto tika ana, kua oti te whakatakoto kia tau rawa te āhua.
E takoto tahi mai ana ngā awa me ngā rangaranga roroa (ki tētahi mata pēnei i te rino, i te pepamārō rānei).
E takoto tahi mai ana ētahi tāhei ki runga.
E tapu ana, e pā ana ki ngā kōrero wānanga tapu o neherā.
E tapu tonu ana, kāore anō i rawekehia, kāore he para kino o roto.
E taratara ana, e kakawa ana, e hākirikiri ana (o te reo kōrero).
E taratara ana, e koikoi ana ētahi wāhi ōna.
E tata ana ki te pango te tae, e pōuri ana te tae.
E tata ana te eke o tētahi āhuatanga, engari kāore i eke rawa, kāore anō rānei kia eke rawa.
E tata ana te hemo.
E tata ana te tangi.
E tatū ana te noho, kāore he whawhai, he tutūnga puehu.
E tau ana te iri mai o ngā kākahu i te tinana, te kawe a te tangata i a ia, te hoahoa rānei o tētahi mea.
E tau ana te mauri, kāore e wehi ana.
E tau ana te ngākau me te wairua, e mahea ana ngā whakaaro, e māmā ana ngā io o te tinana.
E tau ana te wairua, kāore e rongo ana i te āwangawanga, i te mataku rānei.
E tau pai ana (tētahi horanga wai), kāore e ngarungaru ana i te hau.
E taumarumaru ana a raro (o te rākau), nā te mātotoru o te tipu o ōna rau.
E tautau ana, e koru ana rānei te iri mai.
E tautau kōrino ana (ngā makawe), e kapi katoa ana rānei (te upoko) i te makawe kōrino.
E tautika ana te takoto (o tētahi mata), kāore he piki, he heke, he puke, he mārua, kāore rānei i ānau.
E tawhiti ana (ētahi mea) tētahi i tētahi.
E tawhiti ana i ētahi atu; e wehe ana i ētahi atu.
E tawhiti ana mai i tētahi taha ki tētahi (o tētahi hanga).
E tawhiti ana te toro whakaroto atu (i te awa, i te moana, i te aha atu rānei) mai i te mata, mai i runga.
E tawhiti ana, kāore e taea atu.
E teatea ana, e keha ana te tae (o te kiri tangata).
E teitei ana (o te reo, o te oro) e tioro ai ngā taringa.
E tere ai, e wawe ai te tae atu (o te ara).
E tere ana te rere (o te wai).
E tere pukā ana, he hohoro ki te riri.
E tiakina ana i ngā āhuatanga kino e te wāhi ngaro.
E tika ana kia mihia, kia whakanuitia, he tohu rangatira.
E tika ana kia noho (te kōrero) ki waenga i ngā tāngata anake kua whakaritea kia mōhio.
E tika ana te toro whakarunga, e tū torotika ana, kāore i te paku tītaha.
E tika ana, e hāngai ana.
E tina ana, e pūmau ana.
E tino hara rawa atu ana, ko te mutunga kē mai o te hē.
E tino hia kai ana.
E tino kaha ana ki te kai me te kore e whakaaro ki ētahi atu.
E tino kaha ana te hiakai, te hiahia rānei ki tētahi momo kai.
E tino kaha ana te mā me te kōreko anō.
E tino kaha ana te rōnaki.
E tino kaha ana te tuku aho.
E tino kaha ana te tāwara.
E tino kaha ana te wera, kua hahana, kua whero (o te ahi, o te toka, o te maitai rānei).
E tino kakati ana te hā, tērā ka waiwai ngā karu, ka mamae, ka pāwera rānei te korokoro i te rongotanga.
E tino kino ana te mākū.
E tino kōpē ana i te mea kua āta penupenua.
E tino mahana ana, e taumaha ana, e whakahēmanawa ana (o te hau takiwā).
E tino matakawa ana ki te tangata, e whakamamae ana rānei i a ia (o te kōrero, te mahi rānei).
E tino mārama ana, e pīata ana, e pūataata ana.
E tino ngāwari ana, kua rite tonu rānei ki te wai.
E tino nui ana te hinu i roto, i runga rānei.
E tino nui ana te hoatu, te whakatakoto, te whakapau (i te moni, i te kai, i te aha atu), kāore he tirotiro ki te utu, ki te aha.
E tino ora ana, e tino puta ana te ihu, taha rawa nei.
E tino pai ana (o te aruhe).
E tino pai ana, e tino kaha ana rānei.
E tino pōuri ana, ka mutu kāore e taea e tētahi atu taua pōuritanga te whakamauru, te whakamahea ake.
E tino reka ana ki te arero.
E tino roa ana (te kōrero), me te wana kore anō.
E tino taea ana (e te tangata) ngā mahi, e ekea ana e ia ngā taumata, kei mua i ētahi atu e haere ana; he tangata e pēnei ana te āhua.
E tino tawhiti ana te hokinga ake ki waho (o te tai, i muri tonu mai i te Ōturu me te Whitireia).
E tino teitei ana, e tino poupou ana, e tū matika ana te mata (o te whenua).
E tino toro ana (ngā waewae, te tinana rānei).
E tino uaratia ana i te mea kua kore e tino kitea, e tino rangona; e tika ana kia āta tiakina, kia āta manaakitia.
E tino whai mana ana, e tika ana anō kia whakamihia, kia whakanuia (o te tangata).
E tino whai mana ana, e tika ana anō kia whakamihia, kia whakanuia.
E tino whai take ana, e tino whai tikanga ana; e whai mana ana, e noho mai ana ki tētahi taumata teitei.
E tino whāiti ana mai i tētahi mata ki tētahi, arā, kāore i mātotoru.
E tino āio ana, me te wai whakaata te rite.
E tino ōrite ana te āhua me te rahi o ngā wāhanga e noho tauaro ana ki tēnā taha, ki tēnā taha o tētahi rārangi, o tētahi papa, o tētahi pūwāhi rānei.
E titiro whakateihu ana tētahi o ngā karu, ngā karu e rua rānei.
E tohu ana e hono tata ana tētahi whakaaro, tētahi wāhi rānei ki te kaikōrero, te kaiwhakarongo, te tangata rānei e kōrerotia ana.
E tohu ana e whakapau kaha ana, e warea ana (te tangata) ki tētahi mahi.
E tohu ana e whāiti mai ana ki tērā e whakahuatia ana.
E tohu ana he hanga iti, he hanga hauarea rānei te mea ka tū i muri tonu i a ia.
E tohu ana he rerekē anō tētahi hanga i tērā e pōhēhētia ana, tētahi mahi rānei i tērā e pōhēhētia ana ka puta.
E tohu ana he tangata anō, he wāhi anō, he mea anō kei tua, e rerekē ana rānei i tērā i kōrerotia, e mōhiotia ana rānei.
E tohu ana he wā ka taka, he āhuatanga rānei ka pā, ā, hei reira rawa pā ai ko tētahi atu āhuatanga.
E tohu ana hei te ekenga rā anō o te āhuatanga ka whakahuatia i muri tonu mai, kātahi anō ka haere ko tētahi atu.
E tohu ana i hua mai i tētahi atu mārenatanga.
E tohu ana i ngā tāngata tokorua (o te tūkapi).
E tohu ana i ngā tāngata tokotoru, neke atu (o te tūkapi); e tohu ana i ngā tāngata tokorua, neke atu (o ētahi tūingoa mō te tangata).
E tohu ana i te ahunga ki tētahi wāhi e hono ana ki te kaikōrero, engari kāore ia i reira i te wā e kōrero ana ia.
E tohu ana i te ahunga o tētahi mahi, o tētahi āhuatanga ki te kaikōrero, ki te tangata matua rānei e kōrerotia ana.
E tohu ana i te ahunga o tētahi mahi, o tētahi āhuatanga ki wāhi kē, kaua ki te kaikōrero.
E tohu ana i te ahunga rua, i te ahunga tauaro (o te mahi kei te wāhanga tuarua o te kupu): rere atu, rere mai, mahi atu, mahi mai, whiu atu, whiu mai.
E tohu ana i te ekenga, i te haerenga o tētahi āhuatanga, ā, mā ngā kōrero karapoti e tohu mēnā kei te wāmua, kei te wātū, kei te wāheke, kāore noa iho rānei e herea ana ki tētahi wā whāiti.
E tohu ana i te hanga e pāpā atu ana, e taupatupatu atu ana tētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te hanga ko ia te pūtakenga o tētahi āhuatanga i pā, kua pā rānei.
E tohu ana i te hiahia o te tinana, o te ngākau rānei ki te mea, ki te mahi ka whakaaturia i muri tonu mai.
E tohu ana i te hua me puta, ka puta rānei.
E tohu ana i te kino, i te pānga rānei o tētahi āhuatanga kino.
E tohu ana i te maha tonu, i te huhua tonu.
E tohu ana i te mahi ka mahia e te mea ka whakaingoatia i mua ake, e tohu ana rānei i te wā e mahia ai te mahi ka whakaingoatia i mua ake.
E tohu ana i te mahi ka tutuki pai ki tētahi mea, i tētahi mea, ka pahure rānei i tētahi tangata.
E tohu ana i te mahi me tino mahi kia tutuki ai, kia tika ai tētahi atu āhuatanga.
E tohu ana i te matua, i te whaea, i te tipuna rānei o tētahi tamaiti, o tētahi tangata.
E tohu ana i te mea e taea ana te hoko ki tētahi moni, i te utu rānei o tētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te momo waka, i te ara, i te aha atu rānei e tae atu ai te tangata, te aha atu rānei ki tētahi wāhi.
E tohu ana i te momo whana hiko e kawea ana e te irahiko.
E tohu ana i te momo whana hiko e tauaro ana ki tērā e kawea ana e te irahiko.
E tohu ana i te mutunga o tētahi mea kua tū mō tētahi wā.
E tohu ana i te otinga o tētahi mahi, i te putanga ake rānei o tētahi āhuatanga.
E tohu ana i te reo nō Ingarangi taketake ake, kua kōrerotia ināianei i ngā whenua maha o te ao.
E tohu ana i te rere angiangi o tētahi hanga, arā, kāore he mea e whakapōrearea ana, e whakararu ana, e here ana rānei i te rere.
E tohu ana i te rere tahi, i te haere tahi, i te noho tahi o ētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te rerekē, i te tauhou (o te tangata, o te whenua).
E tohu ana i te rite tonu o te mahia o tētahi mahi.
E tohu ana i te roa e haere ana, e tū ana tētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te takanga o te wā.
E tohu ana i te take i mahia ai tētahi mahi, i te take rānei i puta ai tētahi āhuatanga.
E tohu ana i te tangata ko ia e pupuri ana, e pīkau ana rānei i tētahi mea i te wātū, i te wāheke rānei.
E tohu ana i te tangata koia e pupuri ana i tētahi mea i te wāmua, i te wātū rānei.
E tohu ana i te tangata kotahi, i te mea kotahi (o te tūkapi me ētahi atu hanga).
E tohu ana i te tangata nōna te whakaaro e whakaaturia ana.
E tohu ana i te tangata, i te aha atu rānei ka tau atu ki a ia ngā painga o tētahi hanga, i te tangata rānei me mahi e ia tētahi mahi ki taua mea.
E tohu ana i te tangata, i te aha atu rānei ka tau atu ki a ia ngā painga o tētahi mahi, o tētahi hanga rānei.
E tohu ana i te tangata, i te aha atu rānei ko ia te kaupapa, te aronga o tētahi kōrero, e pā ana ngā kōrero ki a ia.
E tohu ana i te tangata, i te hanga rānei ko ia kei te kawe i te mahi e whakaaturia ana i te wāhanga tuarua o te kupu.
E tohu ana i te tangata, i te hanga rānei ko ia te kaimahi i tētahi mahi i te wā kua hipa, ko ia rānei te pūtakenga o tētahi āhuatanga kua pā, i pā rānei.
E tohu ana i te tangata, i te hanga rānei ko ia te kaimahi i tētahi mahi ā te wā e heke mai ana, ko ia rānei te pūtakenga o tētahi āhuatanga ka pā ā te wā e heke mai ana.
E tohu ana i te tangata, i te hanga rānei ko ia te rangatira o tētahi mea, e noho tūturu ana rānei ki a ia tētahi mea o te rōpū 'a'.
E tohu ana i te tangata, i te hanga rānei ko ia te rangatira o tētahi mea, e noho tūturu ana rānei ki a ia tētahi mea o te rōpū 'o'.
E tohu ana i te tangata, te mea rānei (ahakoa kei te kīanga o mua ake e whakaingoatia ana) e pāngia ana e tētahi mahi, nāna rānei taua mahi i mahi.
E tohu ana i te taparau, ko te wāhanga tuarua o te kupu e whakaatu ana e hia rawa ngā tapa.
E tohu ana i te tino roa ki muri, i te tino tawhiti rānei.
E tohu ana i te uku.
E tohu ana i te whāinga mai o tētahi mahi, tētahi āhuatanga rānei, i muri tata mai i tētahi atu.
E tohu ana i te wā e mahia ai tētahi mahi, e tū ai tētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te wā e pā ai, i pā ai rānei tētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te wā i mahia ai tētahi mahi, i pā ai rānei tētahi āhuatanga.
E tohu ana i te wā i pā ai, e pā ai rānei tētahi āhuatanga.
E tohu ana i te wā tonu ka pā te āhuatanga e kōpaki ana i te kupu, i paku muri mai rānei, ka pā ko tērā atu āhuatanga ka whai i muri iho.
E tohu ana i te wā, te wāhi, te take, te ara rānei ka mahia tētahi mahi.
E tohu ana i te wāhi e noho ana tētahi mea i te wāmua; (i ngā rerenga whakakāhore) e tohu ana i te wāhi kāore e noho ana tētahi mea i te wātū, i te wāheke rānei.
E tohu ana i te wāhi e noho ana tētahi mea i te wātū, i te wāheke rānei.
E tohu ana i te wāhi e tika ana kia noho atu, kia takoto atu, kia kuhuna atu tētahi mea, tae atu ki ētahi atu āhuatanga e pēnei ana.
E tohu ana i te wāhi e tū ai tētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te wāhi, i te aronga e ahu atu ana tētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te wāhi, i te aronga e ahu mai ana tētahi mea.
E tohu ana i te wāhi, i te kāinga, i te iwi rānei i pūtakea mai ai te tangata; e tohu ana i te wāhi i pūtakea mai ai tētahi atu hanga.
E tohu ana i tētahi mea e whakahaeretia ana e tōna anō rangatira, hei tauira, ko te mahi, ko ngā mea e māmā ana ki te neke, te tamariki, te mokopuna, te tāne moe, te wahine moe, te pononga, te kōrero ā-waha, ngā mea i hangaia e te tangata, me te kai (engari kaua te wai māori e inumia ana me te rongoā). He pērā anō te tikanga o ngā kupu 'nā', 'tā', 'ā' me te 'mā', me ngā hononga o ēnei ki te '-ku', te '-u' me te '-na', hei tauira, 'nāku', 'tāu', 'māna', me te katoa o ngā pūriro o te rōpū-'a'.  Ko ērā atu o ngā pūriro e kīia ana he rōpū-'o'.
E tohu ana i tētahi mea koia e noho rangatira ana ki tētahi atu hanga, hei tauira, ko ngā mea, ngā tāngata rānei kei raro te mea e kōrerotia ana i tō rātou mana, ngā waka (tae atu ki te hōiho), ngā whakaaro me ngā kare ā-roto. Ko ētahi anō kei tēnei karangatanga, ko te wai māori, ngā wāhanga, ngā āhuatanga rānei o tētahi hanga (tae atu ki te tinana), ko te tuakana me te teina, me te kupu ka oti mai ina hurihia te tūmahi poro, te tūmahi oti rānei hei tūingoa. He pērā anō te tikanga o ngā kupu 'nō', 'tō', 'ō' me te 'mō', me ngā hononga o ēnei ki te '-ku', te '-u' me te '-na', hei tauira, 'nōku', 'tōu', 'mōna' me te katoa o ngā pūriro o te rōpū-'o'. Ko ērā atu o ngā pūriro e kīia ana he rōpū-'a'.
E tohu ana i tētahi mea kotahi nei e tata ana ki te kaikōrero.
E tohu ana i tētahi mea kotahi nei e tata ana ki te kaiwhakarongo.
E tohu ana i tētahi mea kotahi nei kāore e tata ana ki te kaikōrero, ki te kaiwhakarongo rānei.
E tohu ana i tētahi mea kua kōrerotia kētia.
E tohu ana i tētahi momo haurehu.
E tohu ana i tētahi momo whakatakoto i te kōrero e arotahitia ai te hanga i pā, ka pā rānei tētahi mahi ki a ia, kaua ko te kaimahi.
E tohu ana i tētahi peka mātauranga.
E tohu ana kei te ahu whakararo tētahi mea.
E tohu ana kei te ahu whakarunga tētahi mea.
E tohu ana kei te taha tonu o te kaiwhakarongo tētahi mea.
E tohu ana kei te wā e heke mai ana tū ai te mahi kei muri e whakaingoatia ana.
E tohu ana kei tētahi wāhi kē atu tētahi mea i te kaikōrero, i te kaiwhakarongo rānei.
E tohu ana kia eke rawa tētahi āhuatanga e whakaaturia ana i muri tonu mai, kua haere, kua eke, kua tūturu rānei ko tētahi atu āhuatanga e whakaaturia ana i te rerenga.
E tohu ana ko te kōrero i mua tata atu, koia te take i pā ai, me pā rānei te āhuatanga ka whai i muri mai.
E tohu ana ko te mea e whakahuatia ana i mua tonu i te kupu, e rerekē ana i ētahi atu, otirā he momo tāpiritanga anō hoki ki aua mea rā.
E tohu ana ko te mea e whakahuatia ana i mua tonu, i ngā taha e rua rānei o te kupu nei, he tāpiritanga ki te whakaaro kua whakahuatia i mua tata atu.
E tohu ana ko te mea ka whakaaturia i muri mai, koirā anake te mea ka mahia, kia mahia, e taea ana rānei te mahi.
E tohu ana ko te rerenga e whai mai ana, he momo whakamārama ki tō mua tata atu.
E tohu ana ko te wā tuatahi tēnei i puta ai, i pā ai te āhuatanga e kōrerotia ana.
E tohu ana ko tētahi mahi, tētahi haerenga, tētahi āhuatanga e ahu ana, e aro ana rānei ki tētahi wā, wāhi rānei e tawhiti ana i te kaikōrero.
E tohu ana kua kōrerotia katoatia, kua whakahuatia katoatia ngā mea e tika ana kia whakahuatia.
E tohu ana kua oti kē (tētahi mahi) i te wā ki muri, tērā pea i te wā roa tonu ki muri.
E tohu ana kua wareware noa iho te tangata, kua pōraruraru rānei ngā whakaaro.
E tohu ana kāore e taea ana he mahi i tua atu i tērā e whakahuatia ana.
E tohu ana kāore he mea i tua atu, ko ia tērā kei te tihi (o te āhuatanga kua whakahuatia i mua tonu i te kupu nei).
E tohu ana kāore he mea i tua atu, ko ia tērā kei te tihi (o te āhuatanga kua whakahuatia i muri tonu i te kupu nei).
E tohu ana kāore i puta he hua, kāore rānei e puta he hua i te mahi e whakaaturia ana.
E tohu ana kāore i pērā rawa te whai mana, te whai take, te nui, te kaha, te pai, te kino, te aha atu rānei.
E tohu ana kāore rawa (tētahi tangata) e mahi i tētahi mahi.
E tohu ana me tūpato te tangata i ana kōrero, i ana mahi rānei.
E tohu ana nā te kaikōrero, te kaituhi rānei te mea ka whakaingoatia i muri tonu mai, i mua tonu atu rānei, ā, nō te rōpū-'a' taua mea.
E tohu ana nā te kaiwhakarongo, te kaipānui rānei te mea ka whakaingoatia i muri tonu mai, i mua tonu atu rānei, ā, nō te rōpū-'a' taua mea.
E tohu ana nā tētahi tangata i tua atu i te kaikōrero/kaituhi me te kaiwhakarongo/kaipānui te mea ka whakaingoatia i muri tonu mai, i mua tonu atu rānei, ā, nō te rōpū-'a' taua mea.
E tohu ana nō taua wā tonu i puta ai, i pā ai te āhuatanga e kōrerotia ana.
E tohu ana nō te kaikōrero, te kaituhi rānei te mea ka whakaingoatia i muri tonu mai, i mua tonu atu rānei, ā, nō te rōpū-'o' taua mea.
E tohu ana nō te kaiwhakarongo, te kaipānui rānei te mea ka whakaingoatia i muri tonu mai, i mua tonu atu rānei, ā, nō te rōpū-'o' taua mea.
E tohu ana nō tētahi tangata i tua atu i te kaikōrero/kaituhi me te kaiwhakarongo/kaipānui te mea ka whakaingoatia i muri tonu mai, i mua tonu atu rānei, ā, nō te rōpū-'o' taua mea.
E tohu ana ā tōna wā eke ai tētahi āhuatanga, tērā pea rānei ka eke.
E tohunga ana, e rehe ana (ki tētahi mahi).
E toro ana ki te roa, ki te whānui ka taea, e kikī ana; e tū tika ana.
E toro mai ana ētahi wāhi taratara i te mata, i te tapa.
E torotika ana, e makiki ana (te makawe, te huruhuru).
E toru rā i mua atu.
E toto tonu ana, arā, kāore anō i maoa (o te kiko kua tunua).
E totohu whakaroto ana te mata.
E totohu whakaroto ana tētahi wāhi, arā he pāpaku ake i te mata karapoti i a ia.
E tuku aho atu ana ki roto e māmā noa ai te kitea atu o ngā mea kei roto, kei muri rānei.
E tuku āwhina ana e tutuki ai tētahi mahi, tā te tangata rānei e whai ana.
E tupu noa ake ana i te wāhi e tau atu ai te kākano, kāore i āta whakatōngia.
E tuwhera ana, e whānui ana, kāore e katia atu ana.
E tuwhera ana, e wātea ana, kāore he aha o roto hei whakararuraru.
E tākoru ana, e tautau noa ana, kāore e kikī ana (o te kākahu).
E tāmia ana, e puritia ana, e hunaia ana (te kare ā-roto, te aha atu rānei), kāore e āta whakapuakina ana.
E tītaha ana (te titiro ki te tangata i runga i te tūpato, i te kore e whakapono, i te kore e pai, i te riri, i te aha atu).
E tīwekaweka ana te āhua, te āhua o te mahi, te āhua o te haere, arā, kāore e ū ana ki te tauira kotahi.
E tōmua ana i te ata.
E tōrino ana te āhua o te tupu (o ngā makawe).
E tōtika ana te kakano (o te rākau), kāore i mingimingi, kāore ōna pūpeka.
E tōtika ana, e ū ana ki ōna anō tikanga kua tohua, kua whakatakotoria mō tētahi kaupapa.
E tū ana mai rā anō, kua roa e haere ana tētahi āhua.
E tū ana te ihu (o te tangata) ki ētahi atu i runga i te whakaaro arā noa atu tōna nui, tōna pai, tōna kaha, tōna aha atu.
E tū mārō ana i te tiketiketanga o te rangi (o te marama, o te rā, me ngā whetū).
E tū mārō ana, e kaha ana te piri tahi me te noho pūmau o ngā korakora o roto, kāore e rērere haere pērā i ngā korakora o te wai me te haurehu.
E tū poupou ana ki te rangi.
E tū pūmau ana ki tētahi wāhi, ki tētahi whakaaro, ki tētahi kaupapa rānei.
E tūpuhi ana, kāore i mōmona (o te ika).
E tūpuhi ana, kāore i ora (o te ika).
E tūtata nei (o te wā).
E tūturu ana, e pono ana, e pirihonga ana.
E tūturu ana, ehara i te kimikimi, i te rūkahu rānei.
E tūtū katoa ana, e rīrapa katoa ana (o te makawe).
E uaua ana ki te neke, ki te hiki, ki te whāwhā, i te nui, i te taumaha, i te rerekē rānei o te hanga.
E uaua ana ki te pupuri, ki te tū rānei ki runga, i te hinuhinu, i te mākū, i te kapi katoa rānei i tētahi hanga hāwareware.
E uaua ana ki te whakapiko, ki te tapahi, ki te wero, ki te wāhi; kāore i māmā te whakarerekē.
E uaua ana te haere, e uaua ana ki te pīkau, e whakamamae ana anō hoki.
E uaua ana te tiko i te mārō o ngā tiko.
E uaua tonu ana ki te hāpai ake, ki te neke, ki te pare atu rānei, kāore i māmā.
E waiporoporo uriuri ana te tae.
E waitohu ana tērā tonu pea ka pā he mate, he āhuatanga kino.
E waiwai ana (ngā whatu).
E waiwai ana (o ngā karu).
E waiwai ana te kiko (o te rīwai).
E warea ana (te tangata) ki a ia anō, ki tāna i pai ai, ki ngā painga ka hoki mai ki a ia, hei aha māna ētahi atu.
E warea ana (te wahine) ki te pūremu haere, ki te mate tāne haere.
E wehe ana kia rua ngā peka (o te rākau, o te aha atu).
E wehe ana tētahi i tētahi, kāore i herea tahitia, i raua rānei ki tētahi mea kia kotahi.
E wera ana, e kakati ana ki te arero.
E wera ana, me te āhua haukū anō (o te huarere).
E whai ana i te aronga kotahi, kāore e tahuri kē, kāore he piko.
E whai ana i te rere o te whenua papatahi.
E whai ana kia mahia tētahi mahi i runga i te kaikā, i te pōnānā.
E whai kōiraira ana i runga.
E whai kōrua ana a roto, kāore rānei he aha o roto.
E whai mai ana i ētahi katoa, kāore tētahi e whai i muri iho.
E whai mana ake ana tētahi o ngā mātua (o te tangata) i tētahi atu.
E whai matū ana, kāore e pāpaku; he painga, he māramatanga rānei kei roto mō te tangata, mō te kaupapa (o te whakaaro, te kōrero, te mahi rānei).
E whai niwha ana, e whai kātara ana.
E whai pūreke ana.
E whai tae ana, i tua atu i te pango i te mā.
E whai take ana, e pūmau ana i runga i ngā tikanga o te iwi, me te titiro a te nui tangata, e kore e turakina e wai rānei.
E whai take ana, i takea mai i ngā pūtake e mōhiotia ana he pono, e whakaarotia ana rānei he pono, he tōtika.
E whai tonu ana (te tangata) i tāna i pīrangi ai ahakoa pēhea, me te kore e aro ki ngā kino tērā ka puta ake.
E whakaae ana ki tētahi āhuatanga, kia mahia rānei tētahi mahi.
E whakaae noa ana ki tā ētahi atu, e whai noa ana i tā ētahi atu, e māmā noa ana te kawe i ngā whakaaro.
E whakaae noa ana ki tā ētahi atu, e whai noa ana i tā ētahi atu, kāore e whakahē mai, e whakararu mai.
E whakaaetia ana, e tukuna ana rānei i raro i te mana o tētahi whakahaere, o tētahi rōpū rānei.
E whakaahua ana i ngā karaka me ngā wati ka riro mā ngā ringa e rua e tohu te takanga o ngā hāora me ngā meneti.
E whakaata aho ana, e tuku aho ana rānei.
E whakaatu ana (te tangata) i tana tino pai ki tōna anō āhua, ki ngā mahi rānei ka taea e ia.
E whakaatu ana i eke tonu tā tētahi tangata i whakaaro ai ka eke, i hiahia ai, i whai ai rānei kia eke. Whakamahia ai hei whakaū, hei whakangahau i te kōrero.
E whakaatu ana i te pirihonga, i te aroha ki tētahi atu tangata.
E whakaatu ana i te taputapu, i te mea rānei koia kei te whakatutuki i tētahi mahi.
E whakaatu ana tērā tonu pea ka pā te āhuatanga e whakaingoatia ana i muri tata mai, ā, i tērā tonu ka pā ko tētahi atu āhuatanga.
E whakahau ana kia aro mai tētahi ki tāu e tohu atu ana.
E whakakaha ana i te rerekē o tētahi mea i tētahi atu.
E whakakoa ana, e whakapārekareka ana, e whakakatakata ana i tētahi atu.
E whakamā ana, e whīwhiwhi ana rānei ngā whakaaro, e pōkaikaha ana rānei.
E whakamāngeongeo ana i te ihu, e tihetihe ai, e hiahia tihetihe ai rānei te tangata.
E whakangenge ana i te wairua, i te ngākau, i te rite tonu, i te roa tonu rānei o te mahia o tētahi mahi, o te puta ake rānei o tētahi āhuatanga.
E whakangungua ana e ngā karakia o te kawa.
E whakaoho ana i te ihi, i te wehiwehi, i te whakamīharo.
E whakaohooho ana i te ngākau i te pai, i te ātaahua, i te rerekē rānei o tētahi mea.
E whakaputa ana i te oro kaha e tioro ai ngā taringa; he oro e pēnei ana te āhua.
E whakaputa ana, e tohu ana i te pōuri, i te mamae, i te kōhau o te ngākau, aroha ana ki te whakarongo atu.
E whakaputa kino ana i te riri e mamae ai tētahi atu ā-kiko, ā-hinengaro, ā-wairua rānei, e takakinotia ai rānei tētahi mea.
E whakararu ana i ētahi atu kia riri tahi, kia hē rānei te mahi tahi, te noho tahi.
E whakaroaroa ana i muri.
E whakataki ana i tētahi whakaaro e whakatakoto wero ana ki te kaiwhakarongo.
E whakataki ana i ētahi āhuatanga ka pā, tētahi i muri i tētahi.
E whakatatū ana i te tinana, i te noho, kāore e whakamamae ana i te tinana.
E whakatūpato ana ka pā he raruraru ki te whāia tonuhia tētahi mahi, tētahi āhuatanga, ki te kore rānei te tangata e whai ki te ārai atu i taua raruraru.
E whakaū ana i te pakupaku, i te hauarea rānei o tētahi mea.
E whakaū ana i te pono o tētahi āhuatanga.
E whāiti ana (o te koki); e iti ake ana i te 90° te rahi (o te koki).
E whāiti haere ana tētahi mea tae noa ki tōna tihi, ki tōna pito rānei, e koi ai te hanga.
E whānui ana mai i tētahi mata ki tētahi, ina whakaritea ki te roa, ina whakaritea rānei ki ētahi atu hanga; te whānui mai i tētahi mata ki tētahi.
E whānui ana me te pararaki anō (o te puoto).
E whānui ana ngā āputa, ngā mokotawhā o roto (o tētahi mea).
E whānui ana, e pāpaku ana (o te ipu).
E whānui ana, e pāpaku ana (o tētahi mea pērā i te waka).
E āhua mātao ana, kāore i tino mahana (o te hau, o te hau takiwā, o te tinana rānei).
E āhua mātao ana, kāore i tino mahana, kāore i wera.
E āhua pāpango ana, e whai tae ana me uaua ka taea te horoi atu, te muku atu.
E āhua pōuri ake ana, e āhua mātao ake ana nā te mea e āraihia atu ana ngā hihi o te rā e tētahi mea.
E āhua pōuri ana (tētahi wāhi), i te mea kua āraia atu ngā hihi o te rā.
E āhua pōuri tonu ana (o te rangi).
E āhua pūataata ana.
E āhua rite ana (tētahi hanga) ki (tētahi atu mea).
E āhua tautau ana ngā paerunga, he hūmārie, he ngāwari te āhua (o ngā karu).
E āhua tawhiti ana te tupu tētahi i tētahi, kāore i mātotoru.
E āhua tuku ana i te aho ki roto, ki tērā taha rānei, engari kāore i pūataata rawa.
E āhua tāwhi ana i te kōrero, e āhua tapepa ana rānei te kōrero.
E āhua tāwhitiwhiti ana te noho tētahi i tētahi, ko tēnā ki tōna wāhi, ko tēnā ki tōna.
E ānau haere ana, e huri haere ana, huri katoa i tētahi pūtahi, me te rahi haere anō pea.
E āta piki ana, e āta heke ana, pērā i te hone moana āio.
E ātaahua ana ki te titiro atu, e noho ana hei kai mā te mata.
E ū ana (te ahunga o te huringa) ki tērā ka whāia e ngā ringa o te karaka.
E ū ana ki te pono, e ū ana rānei ki ngā pūtake e mōhiotia ana, e whakaarotia ana rānei he pono.
E ū tonu ana ki tētahi mahi uaua, ki tētahi mahi mōrearea me te kore e mataku, ahakoa rānei te mataku; e manawanui ana, e manawa kai tūtae ana.
He ahi e whakahaeretia ai ngā mahi hei whakakore atu i te tapu.
He ahi hei tunu i te manu tuatahi ka patua e tētahi hunga patu manu, hei kai mā tō rātou tohunga ina mutu ana karakia whakarata i a Tāne, ina hikina te tapu i te taupuni me te ngahere kei reira rātou. I te wā e haere ai ngā karakia, ka whiua atu he rau huka ki te ahi.
He ahi i tapu ai nā te mea i āta hikaia (arā, kāore i tīkina atu tōna mura i tētahi atu ahi) e rite ai ngā karakia, ngā tikanga mō te tūpāpaku.
He ahi ka tahuna e te tohunga o te taua ina tata atu ki te pā o te hoariri, ka karakia kia kino ai te rangi, kia noho mākūware ai te hoariri, kia kore e tūpato.
He ahi ka tahuna me te haere anō o ētahi karakia hei kaupare i te aituā, hei whakamate rānei i te tangata.
He ahi tapu e tunua ai te manawa o te hoariri kua mate kia taiatea ai, ka pāhunu ai ana hoa whawhai.
He ahi tino tapu he maha noa atu ngā take i tahuna ai, tae atu ki ngā karakia whakarata i a Tāne ina patua te manu, ina tangohia rānei ētahi hanga i te ngahere.
He aho e herea ai, e mau pai ai te kākahu ki te tinana, e iri mai ai rānei te patu ki te kawititanga o te ringa.
He aho hei here i te kete.
He aho hei hōtiki i tētahi mea.
He aho hei takai i te kiko o tētahi mea (pērā i te toki) ki te kakau.
He aho ka herea kia āhua porohita mai te hanga, kia mahuhu anō te pona, ina kumea, kua kikī haere.
He aho ka kitea mō tētahi wā poto noa iho. (E tino hāngai ana ki te aho ka whakaataria.)
He aho kaha e rewha ai, e kōrekoreko ai ngā karu.
He aho kanapa ka hiko i te rangi i te marangai; arā tana hoa puta ngātahi, ko te whatitiri.
He aho kua oti te miro, hei whenu mō te whatu kākahu.
He aho maitai angiangi, he tāwariwari te nuinga, he maha anō ngā whakamahinga.
He aho pūioio, he mā te tae, e tūhono ana i ngā uaua ki te kōiwi.
He aho rangitahi ka herea ki ngā kaho whakapae o te tuanui i te hanganga o te whare.
He aho roa ka mahia ki ngā weu o ētahi tipu pērā i te muka, ki tētahi atu hanga rānei, hei tuitui, hei whatu i tētahi mea.
He aho, he kirihou he rapa rānei a waho, kei roto ētahi waea hei kawe i te hiko.
He ahunga ka whāia - taha tinana, taha hinengaro, taha mahi rānei, e tutuki ai tētahi mea.
He ahunga oneone i whakatōkia ai te kūmara tuatahi me te mea whakamutunga, ko ngā hua ka whakamahia mō ētahi karakia.
He aitanga pepeke noho rāpoi ka haukori ake i ngā rā mahana, he roroa ngā waewae me ngā weri, he parauri, he kahotea te tuarā, ka kitea ngā rua o ngā punua i ngā tahataha oneuku.
He aituā i ngā mahi raranga, i ngā mahi whatu ka hua ake i te poto rawa o tētahi aho, e tohu ana ka mate te kairaranga, tana tāne rānei.
He aituā ka puta ake ina takahia ngā tapu e pā ana ki te riri, ki te pakanga; he kupu whakarite mō ēnei aituā.
He aituā ka pā i te hapa o te whiu i te tao.
He aituā ka pā i te kore e whakahaere i te whāngai hau.
He aituā ka pā ki te waka, ki te kupenga nā te kore e whakaaro ki te tango i ngā ika katoa i mau i te rā o mua atu.
He aituā ko te wai te pūtakenga mai.
He aituā, he tohu kino mēnā e aro whakatetonga ana te whare, e huri ana rānei te tuarā o te tangata ki tētahi atu.
He aka hei here i te toki ki te kakau.
He aka pango piki rākau, he rau pinerua tapa pūngarungaru, he kōratarata, he whānui tonu, he niho kei te kāmata, he hua whero pūhui roa te tupu.
He aka pango piki rākau.
He aka piki ki te kāuru o te rākau, he mati toru, he kōratarata ngā rau, he kōwhai, he ririki, he kakara ngā pua tipu runga tātā roa, he kākano rere.
He aka piki ki te kāuru o te rākau, he rau hohoko tātā roa te tupu, he manawa roa te hanga, he pua māwhero nunui kapu te hanga.
He aka piki ki te kāuru o te rākau, he rau mati toru kōratarata, he pua mā tātā te tupu, he kākano rere.
He aka piki ki te kāuru o te rākau, he rau mati toru, he kārikiuri, he kōratarata, he pua kākāriki, he kōwhai, he kakara, he tātā te tupu, he kākano rere.
He aka piki ki te kāuru o te rākau.
He aka piki ki te kāuru te rākau, he rau hohoko tātā roa te tupu, he manawa te hanga, he pua mā nunui kapu te hanga.
He aka piki rākau e 3, e 5 rānei ngā mati o ngā rau, he whāiti, he roa ngā mati, he niho pūhuki kei ngā tapa, he tara matau te hanga kei muri i ngā kakau o ngā rau me ngā rārā, he pua mā kakara pūhui roa te tupu, he kōwhai karaka ngā hua.
He aka piki rākau e 3, e 5 rānei ngā mati o ngā rau.
He aka piki rākau, e toru ki te rima ngā mati o ngā rau, he whānui, he poto ngā mati, he niho pūhuki kei ngā tapa, he tara matau te hanga kei muri o ngā kakau o ngā rau me ngā rārā, he mā, he kakara ngā pua pūhui roa te tupu, he kōwhai karaka ngā hua.
He aka piki rākau, he rau hohoko kōratarata, he tōihi kei te aka, he pua mā poi taratara te hanga, he hua karaka kei ngā aka wahine, he whero ngā kākano me te puru.
He aka piki rākau, he rau kāwitiwiti tōrino te tupu mai i te aka, he pua tuawhiti mā, he hua kākāriki ure te hanga.
He aka piki rākau.
He aka piri rākau ka noho aka tonu, he rau pinerua ririki tōpuku te hanga, he whero ngā pua poi taratara te hanga.
He aka piri rākau ka noho aka tonu, he rau pinerua, he pua whero poi taratara te hanga.
He aka piri rākau ka noho aka tonu.
He aka piri rākau, he rau pinerua te tupu, he kōtingotingo kei te angamate, he huruhuru kei ngā wana, he pua mā ririki ōna, he poi taratara te hanga.
He aka piri rākau, he whāiti, he tōpuku ngā rau pinerua te tupu, he mā ngā pua poi taratara te hanga.
He aka piri rākau.
He aka toro nuku, he hohoko ngā rau tātā roa te tupu, he manawa iti te hanga, he māwhero ngā pua kapu te hanga.
He aka toro nuku.
He aka tāwhiwhi rākau, he rau kārikiuri tao te hanga, he parauri ngā rau i te ohinga, he pua mā kakara pōī te tupu.
He aka tāwhiwhi rākau, he rau kārikiuri, he pua mā kakara pōī te tupu.
He aka tāwhiwhi rākau.
He amaia e taka ana i te marama, he tohu mate.
He amotai moana roa.
He ana e haria ai ngā poroiwi o te tūpāpaku ina horo katoa ngā kiko pirau.
He anga ka hangaia ki te rākau hei whakairinga mō te ika, mō te aha atu.
He anga ka mahia ki te harakeke hei whakamaroke īnanga me ētahi atu kai.
He anga ka mahia ki te rākau hei whakaapaapa atu i ngā paihere aruhe.
He anga maitai ka pūhia mai i te pū, he rango te hanga, he koi tētahi pito.
He anga maitai rango te hanga, he koi tētahi pito, ka purua ki te paura me te matā, hei pupuhi mai i te pū.
He anga mā ka tere i te kare o tai hōhonu, he kōmiro te hanga, 12-15 henemita te tupu, he pōngarengare e rere ana i ngā kaokao me te kōpako, ko te anga nei te putunga hua o te uwha ngū.
He anga māmā nei te hanga kua uhia ki te raupō, te pepa, te aha atu rānei, he tapatoru te āhua, ka tukua kia rere i te hau ki tētahi aho roa.
He anga mātaitai hei tapahi huruhuru.
He anga papatahi ka hangaia ki ētahi rawa ka mānu i te wai, he mea here ngātahi hei kawe i te tangata, i ngā utanga rānei mā runga i te wai.
He anga porotaka ka kitea e piri ana ki te korokoro me te puku o te paikea.
He anga pāua pāpaku.
He anga rākau poutū e iri ai te kākahu e whatua ana.
He anga whai kōrewa ka whakamaua ki te taha o te waka, kia kore ai te waka e tahuri.
He anuhe kua nohopuku, kua kōpaki i a ia, i te mea e huri ana hei pūrerehua; te whare tonu e kōpaki ana i a ia.
He ao tuarangi e amio ana i tētahi whetū, he mea hanga ki te toka, ki te konganuku, ki te haurehu rānei.
He ao tuarangi he pororapa tana ara amio i te rā, he hukapapa, he puehu te karihi, kia tata ki te rā kua whai hiku.
He ara i waenganui i ētahi toka, i ētahi tāhuna rānei, e takoto ana, e rere ana te wai.
He ara ka keria i raro i te whenua e haere ai te tereina, te waka, te aha atu.
He ara wai karekare ka mahue ki muri i te waka haere moana.
He ara, he tikanga rānei ka whakatakotoria e tētahi rōpū hei ārahi i āna mahi.
He arearenga i te whenua, i tētahi hanga, i tētahi mata rānei.
He aroha tino nui, tino hōhonu.
He aruhe kua hē te tunu.
He aruhe kua oti te whakaapaapa, te whakapū.
He aruhe kua rite hei hari i tētehi haerenga.
He aruhe kāore i pai i te mea he nui te tākaka, me te aha  kāore e whati noa.
He aruhe kāore i tino pai i te nui o te tākaka me te iti o te renga.
He aruhe pai, he iti te kaka.
He aruhe tino pai.
He aruhe waitau, kāore anō i rite hei kai.
He atamira i te roro o te whare, i te marae rānei hei nohoanga mō te rangatira.
He atarau rehurehu e taiāwhio ana i te marama; he āniwaniwa rehurehu kōmā ngā tae ka kitea i te pō.
He atua kawe māuiui ki te tangata.
He au i te wai, i te hau, ka hurihuri tonu ki roto i a ia anō, e puta ai he āwhiowhio.
He aupuru hei tautoko i te upoko o te tangata i a ia e takoto ana, e moe ana.
He aupuru rau raupō ka herea ki runga o ngā purupuru o te rauawa o te waka.
He awa kore wai, kua maroke i te whāinga o te awa he ara kē.
He awa rere tāhapa i te wahapū.
He awa whakarara ka rere i waenga i ngā rārangi pākati i te whakairo.
He haenga i te takere o te waka e tuturu kino mai ai te wai.
He haenga iti ka mahia ki tētahi mata, ki tētahi taitapa.
He haenga nui, he haenga hōhonu i te mata o te whenua, o te aha atu rānei.
He haenga roroa, he wāhi hāpua roroa rānei i tētahi mata.
He haenga, he kōihi i te mata o tētahi mea.
He haenga, he matiti e rere ana i te whenua.
He haenga, he tapahanga, he wāhi rānei e totohu whakaroto ana i tētahi mata, i tētahi tapa rānei.
He haka e tirohia ai ngā tohu o roto; ka hakaina i te taenga mai o te ope tūārangi, o te taua wāhine, o te taua muru rānei, i mua rānei o te whawhai.
He haka hei whakatau i te manuhiri ki te tangihanga.
He haka mō te wā e toa ai te tangata.
He hana whero i te rangi.
He hanga ahutoru hangarite, e ono ōna mata tapawhā ōrite.
He hanga angiangi ka mahia ki ngā kaka o te rākau me ētahi atu mea, hei papa tuhituhi, hei takai, hei pēke, hei aha atu rānei.
He hanga e ihi ai, e wehi ai, e koropiko ai rānei te tangata.
He hanga e iri mai ana i te rangi ka amio i tētahi atu hanga rahi ake.
He hanga e māuiui ai, e mate ai rānei tētahi mea ora ki te uru atu te hanga nei ki tana tinana.
He hanga e raua atu ai he reta, he pepa, he aha atu hei tuku ki tangata kē, hei tiaki noa rānei i ētahi mea kia kore ai e marara noa.
He hanga e rite ana ki ngā matihao o mua o te kōura, o te pāpaka.
He hanga e rite ana ki te huamanu ki te titiro atu, arā, he āhua rite ki te porohita kua kūmea ngā pito e rua, engari e hema ana, e āhua whāiti ana tētahi o ngā pito.
He hanga e rite ana ki te porohita kua kūmea ngā pito e rua kia porohita roa.
He hanga e whai haere ana i te tapa o tētahi mea, e karapoti ana, e taiapa ana i taua mea.
He hanga e whā ngā waewae hei hīkoitanga mōna, he hanga whāngote i ana kūao.
He hanga hauarea noa, he hanga iti noa.
He hanga hei harakuku, hei tapahi rānei i tētahi mea.
He hanga hei hono i ētahi mea e rua, ka hurihuri tētahi me te mau tonu o tētahi, kia kore ai te mea e hurihuri rā e mau, e whīwhiwhi rānei.
He hanga hei hopu ika ka mahia ki te kōiwi, ki te rākau, ki te maitai, ki te aha atu, he pito koi whai kāniwha tōna.
He hanga hei karatiti i ētahi mea pērā i te papa, ka hangaia ki te maitai, he koi tētahi pito, he upoko kei tētahi.
He hanga hei rau atu i ngā momo mea katoa, ka rangā ki te harakeke, he kīwei tō te nuinga hei kawe haere ki te ringa.
He hanga hei rau atu, hei kōpaki i tētahi mea, pērā i te naihi, i te hoari.
He hanga hei tuhi ki te papa tuhituhi, he mea mahi mai ki tētahi hanga e rite ana ki te pākeho.
He hanga hei uhi i ngā waewae mai i ngā matimati ki ngā rekereke, ko te tikanga ka kuhuna ki waho atu i ngā tōkena.
He hanga hei uhi i te māhunga.
He hanga hei wehe mai i ngā wāhanga tūmārō o tētahi wai, hei wehe mai i ngā pōrukuruku o tētahi puehu, hei penupenu rānei i te kai.
He hanga hei ārai atu i te hau.
He hanga i te taiapa e uru atu ai, e puta mai ai te tangata, te kararehe, ka taea te whakatuwheratia, te kati.
He hanga i te tinana ka waihanga i tētahi momo matū whāiti kia rukea atu, kia kawea atu rānei ki te wāhi o te tinana e hiahiatia ai.
He hanga iti ka pēhia hei whakakā, hei whakaweto i tētahi mea, hei whakahaere rānei i tētahi mahi.
He hanga iti, he pāpaku, ka rangā ki te harakeke hei takotoranga kai maoa.
He hanga ka kainga, ka pania, ka werohia, ka kuhuna rānei ki te tinana, he mahi rānei ka mahia hei whakaora i te mate, hei kaupare atu rānei i te mate; he mahi e ora ai tētahi raruraru.
He hanga ka kuhuna ki te kōhao kia kikī tonu, kia kore ai tētahi mea pērā i te wai e puta, e uru atu rānei.
He hanga ka mahia ki te kirikiri, ki te onepū, me tētahi paura kua mahia ki te pākeho me te uku, ka pokepokea ki te wai, me te kōhatu te mārō ina totoka.
He hanga ka mahia ki te kōata, ki te kirihou, ki te aha atu, he whānui ake te tinana i te kakī whāiti, he hanga hei pupuri wai.
He hanga ka mau ki te ringa, he pūkoro motuhake anō ōna mō ia mati, kuhuna ai hei whakamahana, hei ārai i te kino, hei whakapaipai noa rānei.
He hanga ka nekenekehia e te ringa i runga i tētahi mata papatahi kia neke ai te pehu i te mata o te rorohiko, he wāhi anō ka pēpēhia e taea ai ētahi āhuatanga o te rorohiko te mahi.
He hanga ka purua, ka takaia rānei ki te waha kia noho ngū ai te tangata.
He hanga ka tere noa, ka māturuturu, ka taea rānei te riringi.
He hanga ka whakakī i tētahi āputa.
He hanga ka whakamahia e te matatuhi hei tohu mō tētahi mea kua whānakotia, ā, e whai ana kia whakahokia mai taua mea mā te karakia.
He hanga ka whakamaua ki te kakī o te kararehe hei whakaita, hei whakamatua i a ia.
He hanga ka whakatūria, ka whakanōhia rānei ki raro, ki muri rānei i tētahi atu mea, kia noho rewa tonu taua mea, kia kore ai rānei e hinga.
He hanga ka whakaurua atu, ka whakamaua rānei ki te  tomokanga, ki te taupoki, ki te aha atu kia kore ai e taea te huaki; ka mahi kia ita, kia noho haumaru (tētahi mea) i tēnei hanga.
He hanga koi e rite ana ki te ngira e puta ake ana i tētahi mea pērā i te ika, i te kararehe, i te tipu rānei.
He hanga koi, he makiki, ka tipu i te tātā, i hea atu rānei o ētahi tipu pūtaratara pērā i te tūmatakuru, i te ongaonga, i te kōtimana.
He hanga koropuku ka tupu tika mai i te kakau, i te pito rānei o te kakau (o te tipu), ka huri hei pua, hei putiputi, hei rau, hei pihi hou rānei.
He hanga kāore e hou atu te wai ki roto, he kaha, he tāwariwari, he pīngore, ka mahia ki te tarawai o tētahi rākau ka tipu i ngā whenua pārūrū.
He hanga kōata ka whakamaua atu ki te rama hiko, koia te mea ka tuku aho mai ina whakakāngia te rama.
He hanga kōmāmā pēnei i te paretua ka kuhuna ki raro i te utanga, kia kore ai te kiri e pahore.
He hanga kōpae, kāore ōna koko; te ara amio i tētahi pū e ōrite ana te tawhiti huri katoa i taua pū; ka tuhi i tēnei hanga hei tohu i tētahi mea.
He hanga maha e tū matatira mai ana, e noho matatira mai ana.
He hanga maitai he tapaono, he tapawhā te hanga ka whakawiria atu ki te pine hei whakamau atu i tētahi hanga.
He hanga maitai iti ka hurihia kia mau ai tētahi mea ki tētahi atu, he kōmiro e rere ana i te tinana, he koi te pito ngau, he upoko whai haenga kei tērā atu pito.
He hanga maruwehi, he hanga whakamataku he kaha  motuhake anō tōna, ko tōna whakatinanatanga ko te tangata, ko te rākau, ko te toka, ko te aha atu.
He hanga mata whānui ka whiuwhiua e te ringa kia hauhau ai te tangata.
He hanga motuhake pēnei i te whetū, i te aorangi, e iri mai ana i te rangi, i tuarangi, i te ao tukupū.
He hanga māmā, he hanga e kī ana i te hau ka whakamaua ki te tapa whakarunga o te kupenga kia kore ai e totohu.
He hanga mārō he whero, he mā, he māwhero te tae, ka hua ake i ngā wheua o ētahi momo ika tino ririki, nā wai ā, ka tupu hei toka, hei pūkawa.
He hanga mārō iti ka tupu ake i te kiri, he huaketo te pūtakenga mai.
He hanga mārō ka mahia ki te rākau, ki te maitai, ki te aha atu, hei whakairinga mō tētahi mea, hei tautoko i tētahi mea, māna rānei e tū tika ai, e kaha ai tētahi mea.
He hanga mārō ka tū takirua mai i te tumuaki o te nanekoti, o te kau me ētahi atu kararehe, he ānau, he āhua koi anō te nuinga.
He hanga mārō, he mōwhakiwhaki anō, he pūataata, he whakatīaho rānei te nuinga, whakamahia ai hei hanga matapihi, hei hanga ipu.
He hanga ngohe, he hinuhinu anō, kei ngā arearenga o te wheua.
He hanga ngāwari ka horaina ki te papa, he taputapu whai hanga ngāwari rānei hei takotoranga, hei wāhi moe.
He hanga noho ki roto i te oneone, he tinana roa tōna, kāore ōna poroiwi, kāore ōna waewae, he kaha ia ki te wāwāhi oneone, ki te tuku atu anō i ngā painga ki te oneone.
He hanga nā te hoariri kua hinga, ka whakamahia i roto i ngā karakia hei kaupare atu i te kimi utu a taua hoariri.
He hanga nō roto tonu i te toka, e karia ake ana hei hoko, pērā i te kōura, i te waro rānei; he hanga nō roto tonu i te whenua kei a ia tōna ake āhuatanga matū, he hanga tioata anō tōna; he hanga pērā i te tote, i te wai, ka mātua hiahiatia e ora ai ngā mea oreore.
He hanga ora ahakoa te maha o ngā waewae, o ngā parirau, o te aha atu (hāunga anō te tangata).
He hanga ora e toru ngā wāhanga o te tinana, ko te pane, te tārāuma me te puku, e ono ngā waewae, tērā anō pea he pakihau, he pūhihi anō ōna.
He hanga ora whai parirau, whai huruhuru, he whai tuaiwi, ka whakaputa hua e puta ai he uri; ētahi atu hanga ora whai parirau nui, pērā i te pekapeka, te kīkītara, te rangataua, te pūrerehua.
He hanga papatahi e hora ana ki tētahi mata, e takoto ana rānei i waenganui i ētahi mea e rua.
He hanga papatahi ka rangā ki te harakeke, ki te aha atu, hei uhi ki te papa, ki hea atu rānei, hei moenga, hei nohoanga, hei aha atu.
He hanga papatahi ka tipu mai i te kiri o te manu, he tātā piako āhua mārō kei waenganui, he weu e rere ana i ngā taha e rua.
He hanga papatipu whakaata aho, e noho raupapa ana, e ōrite tahi ana anō hoki te hanga o ōna wāhanga whakaroto mano tini.
He hanga pararaki, he pāraharaha, he porowhita te hanga o te nuinga, he taputapu hei pupuri kai.
He hanga paraumu pērā i te maramara tipu, te hamuti kararehe, te aha atu, kua popo, kua hanehane, ka whakamahia hei whakahaumako i te oneone.
He hanga porohita, he papatahi, he angiangi, ko te nuinga he pakupaku anō.
He hanga porotaka ka whiua, ka whanaia, ka patua rānei i ngā tākaro, i ngā mahi hākinakina.
He hanga pupuri kai ka mahia ki te kiri o te tōtara, o ētahi atu rākau rānei.
He hanga pupuri pūngao ka kuhuna ki te mīhini whakapau hiko, nō reira mai te hiko e kā ai, e haruru ai te mīhini.
He hanga pākākā ka puta i te mata o te rino, o te maitai i te pānga tonuhia e te wai, e te haukū.
He hanga pēnei i te kākahu, i te papanga rānei ka uhia ki tētahi mea.
He hanga pērā i te kōhatu, i te rākau, me ētahi atu mea, ka noho hei taunga mō te mana atua e tiaki ana i te hau o te tangata, o te whenua, o te ngahere, o te kāinga, o te aha atu; te mana atua ka whakanohoia mai ki te kōhatu, ki te rākau, ki te aha atu, ko taua mana atua te kaitiaki o te tangata, o te whenua, o te aha atu, he tapu.
He hanga pērā i te oneone e kino ai tētahi mea; he oneone e takoto pūngorungoru noa ana i te whenua.
He hanga pērā i te pito whenua, i te whenua, i te whare, he wāhanga whāiti rānei o tētahi mea nui ake.
He hanga pērā i te rino ka kukume i ētahi atu konganuku, aha atu rānei, kia piri tahi ki a ia.
He hanga rere poutū e puta atu ai te auahi o te ahi ki te takiwā.
He hanga rerekē, he taonga kāore i tino kitea, he mea mīharo.
He hanga rite ki te kakī mō runga i te tahā, i hangaia ki te rākau, i āta whakairohia a waho, he moani a roto, i waruwaruhia kia noho pai mai ai ki te waha o te tahā. I mahia he kōhao i te tapa whakararo o ētahi kia pai ai te tui atu ki ngā kōhao kua mahia mai ki te tapa whakarunga o te tahā.
He hanga rite ki te kōrehu ka rewa ake ki te rangi, ka tāiri mai rānei ki te rangi ina wera tētahi mea.
He hanga rite ki te pātaka iti kei runga pou, hei pupuri taonga pērā i te rākau whawhai, i te kākahu, i te taputapu, i te aha atu, tae atu hoki ki te kōiwi tūpāpaku.
He hanga roa ka mahia ki te maitai, he rau rapa tōna, ka piua ānautia e te hiko ki te ūkui i te ua, i te aha noa iho ka tau ki te matapihi o mua o te waka.
He hanga roa ka mahia ki te wūru, ki te hiraka, ki te aha atu rānei, ka mau ki te kakī hei whakamahana, hei whakapaipai rānei.
He hanga roa tonu, he mātotoru tonu, he tino kaha, ka hangā ki te rākau ki te maitai rānei, hei tautoko i ngā wāhanga taumaha o te whare.
He hanga roa, he papatahi, he rahirahi, he mātotoru rānei,  ka kania mai i te rākau.
He hanga roa, he whāiti ka mahia ki te rākau, ki te maitai, ki te kirihou rānei, kua tāia ki ōna anō waeine, he torotika ngā tapa, whakamahia ai hei ine i te roa, hei tuhi rārangi tōtika rānei.
He hanga roa, he whāiti, he angiangi, he mea hanga ki te kirihou, ki te pepa, ki te papanga, ki te maitai, ki te aha atu, whakamahia ai mō ngā mahi huhua. Hei tauira, hei whakapiri, hei paihere, hei whakamau, hei ine, tae atu ki te hopu, ki te whakaatu i te āhua me te oro.
He hanga roa, he whāiti, he rite te hanga o te nuinga ki te rango engari he ipuipu a roto, ko tāna he kawe i te wai, i te hau, i te aha atu.
He hanga roroa rite ki te pūhihi ka tiaia ki te huruhuru manu, hei whakarākei i te tauihu o te waka taua.
He hanga roroa rite ki te pūhihi ka tiaia ki te huruhuru manu.
He hanga tangata weriweri te āhua i roto i ngā mahi whakairo.
He hanga taumaha (pērā i te kōhatu, i te maitai) e mau ana ki te taura, ki tētahi atu mea rānei i runga i te waka, ka tukua ki te takere o te wai kia kore ai te waka e nuku.
He hanga taumaha ka utaina ki te riu o te waka hei whakamatua i te waka.
He hanga tino iti.
He hanga tino rerekē, he hanga tauhou.
He hanga tuawhiti rite ki te tarakina ka tipu mai i te kauae o te ika.
He hanga wairua e whakaponotia ana e ētahi he kaiāwhina, he karere nā Ihowā, he tangata whai parirau tōna hanga.
