He hau taurangi ka pupuhi mai i te tonga-mā-rāwhiti.
He hau tino kaha te pupuhi, otirā he hau taurangi.
He hau tino kaha te pupuhi.
He hau tino kino ka ohorere te pā mai mō tētahi wā poto.
He hau tino kino te āwhiowhio.
He hau tino kino, he āwhā tino kino rānei ka ohorere te pā mai mō tētahi wā poto.
He hau tino ngāwari, kāore noa e kaha te pupuhi.
He hau tino tere te āmiomio.
He hau tonga ka kawe mai i te paki.
He hau tonga ko te ua te hoa haere.
He hau whenua ka pupuhi mai i te raki.
He haupū tio nui whakaharahara e tino pōturi ana te heke haere (i ngā maunga), te toro whakawaho rānei (i ngā kōpakatanga o te ao).
He haurehu kākāriki-kōwhai te tae, he kanekane ki te ihu, he tāoke. (Tohu pūtaiao: Cl)
He haurehu nohopuku tino māmā, he mura kore, he tae kore, he kakara kore. (Tohu pūtaiao: He)
He haurehu nohopuku, he tae kore, he kakara kore, ka noho rikiriki mai ki te kōhauhau o Papatūānuku. Nāna i whero ai ngā rama o ngā pānui hoko me ērā atu rama whero o te tāone. (Tohu pūtaiao: Ne)
He haurehu tae kore, kakara kore ka mura noa, ina hono ki te hāora ka hua ake ko te wai. (Tohu pūtaiao: H)
He haurehu tae kore, kakara kore kei te hau takiwā, e ora ai te kararehe me te tipu. (Tohu pūtaiao: O)
He haurehu tae kore, kakara kore, koia te nuinga o te hau takiwā o Papatūānuku. (Tohu pūtaiao: N)
He haurehu, he kōwhai teatea te tae, he kanekane ki te ihu, he āhuatanga tāoke ōna. (Tohu pūtaiao: F)
He hei kakī ka tāraia ki te pounamu, ki te wheua rānei, e tohu ana i te kikiri tangata.
He hekenga poto (i tētahi hiwi).
He here hei whakamau i te pīkaunga ki te tuarā.
He here kua miroa ki te muka, ki tētahi atu hanga rānei, he rahi ake i te miro engari kāore i rite ki te taura te mātotoru.
He here āhua rite ki te pūreke ka oti mai ina kuhuna tētahi pito o te taura, o te aho, o tētahi hanga pērā rānei, ki roto atu i tētahi atu wāhanga ōna kua oti te whakakoropewa, me te kukume kia kikī.
He hiahia tino nui ki tētahi mea.
He hikinga wairua, he hikinga manawa i te rongotanga i te āhuareka, i te pārekareka.
He hiku kōura kua whakamarokengia.
He hoahoa ka hangaia hei tautuhi i tētahi whakahaere, i ngā taonga, i ngā ratonga rānei e hokona ana e tētahi kamupene.
He hoahoa whakarākei mō te tukutuku, mō te kōwhaiwhai, mō te raranga mō te aha, mō te aha.
He hoe hei rūnā i te poti, i te waka rānei.
He hoe tuarua hei rūnā i te waka.
He hoenga waka kakama, he pāpaku, he poto te kumenga.
He hokinga whakamuri i te whawhai ki te akiaki i ngā toa ki te whawhai anō.
He hononga ka hua ake i te moe, i te mārena a tētahi tokorua.
He horanga moana nui tonu e tawhiti ana i te whenua.
He horanga taonga ka āta whakaritea hei mātakitaki mā te marea.
He horanga wai i te moana tata ki uta, he pai mō te tuku kupenga.
He horanga wai māori nui e karapotia ana e te whenua.
He horanga whenua nui e tipuria ana e te rākau nui me ētahi atu tipu.
He horanga whenua tino nui, he papatahi, he āhua papatahi rānei, he māmā noa te rōnaki.
He hua iti whai kākano (pērā i ērā ka kainga e te manu).
He hua ka tipu ki te rākau, he kākano, he karihi rānei kei te pū, ko te wāhi kikokiko e horopaki ana i ēnei ka kainga.
He hua kei reira e puritia ana ngā kākano o ētahi rākau, ētahi tipu rānei, kia pakari kua kōwhā ki te tuku i ngā kākano.
He hua āhua porotaka he kākāriki, he waiporoporo, he pango rānei te peha, ka puhipuhi te tipu mai i te aka, ka kainga, ka mahia rānei hei inu.
He huaki ohorere (o te taua).
He huarahi ka whakatūria ki runga ake i te awa, i te whārua, i te huarahi, ki hea atu rānei, e taea ai aua mea te whakawhiti.
He huarahi tūmatanui e noho rārangi mai ana he whare i ngā taha, he tau tō ia whare.
He huarahi āwhiowhio, arā, kāore e haere tōtika.
He huarākau kawa, ka kōwhai ina maoa; te rākau e tipu ai te hua nei.
He huarākau kiri maheni, he whero, he kākāriki rānei, he mārō, he mā te kiko.
He huarākau kāore anō i pakari, i maoa.
He huarākau roa piko te hanga, he kākāriki te kiri mata, he kōwhai te kiri maoa, he kōwhai teatea te kiko ngohe.
He huarākau tōpuku he kākano kotahi kei roto, he kōwhai, he mā rānei te kiko reka, he hanga rite ki te kerehunga kei te kiri; te rākau e tipu ai te huarākau nei.
He huawhenua he karaka, he kākāriki, he kiwikiwi rānei te kiri ina pakari, he karaka te kiko, kei te pukahu i waenganui ngā kākano; te tipu toro nuku e tupu mai ai te paukena.
He huawhenua he kākāriki ngā rau.
He huawhenua ka hua mai i tētahi tipu teitei tonu, kotahi, e rua rānei ngā puku ka tupu mai i te tipu kotahi, he hanga rite ki te pātītī hiraka e kōpaki ana i ngā kai o roto, he rau kei waho atu i tērā, ka noho rārangi mai ngā pata kōwhai ki te puku; he māra, he wāhanga rānei o tētahi māra kua whakatipuria ki tēnei huawhenua.
He huawhenua ka tipu mai i tētahi tipu toro nuku, he pororapa, he kākāriki, he pāhiwihiwi te kiri, kia pakari kua tino mārō, kua karaka a waho, a roto; he māra, he wāhanga rānei o tētahi māra kua whakatipuria ki te kamokamo anahe.
He huawhenua kōekoeko te tupu i raro i te whenua, he karaka te tae, he kai.
He huawhenua kōroaroa kōiheihe nei te tupu, he pūkanohi ōna, ka hua mai i raro i te whenua, he māwhero, he waiporoporo, he kahotea rānei te kiri, he kahotea, he kaho rānei te kiko, he huawhenua māngaro ina tunua; he māra, he wāhanga rānei o te māra kua onokia ki te kūmara.
He huawhenua nunui ngā raupaka, he roa ngā tātā, kainga ai ko ngā rau me te hua tōpuku ka tupu i raro i te whenua, he tino kai ki ngā iwi huri i Te Moana-nui-a-Kiwa, he kai māngaro.
He huawhenua porotaka, he maha ōna paparanga, ki te kainga matatia he kakati ki te waha.
He huawhenua tōpuku te hanga, he poto, he mātotoru te kakau, he mātotoru anō ngā rau kākāriki, waiporoporo rānei e kōpaki ana i ngā rau hou i te pū.
He huawhenua tōpuku whai pūkanohi ka hua mai i raro i te whenua, he parauri, he māwhero, he keretewha rānei te kiri, he motuhanga te kiko ina tunua; he māra, he wāhanga rānei o tētahi māra kua whakatipuria ki te rīwai anahe.
He huawhenua āhua hīmoemoe ka whakatipuria hei kai, he mōhinuhinu te kiri, he whero te nuinga ina maoa.
He hue i tapahia i te puku tonu hei mahi oko.
He hue kua whakatangatatia.
He hue pakari kua oti te karu te tango ake, whakamahia nuitia ai hei kawe wai.
He huhu, tētahi atu torongū rānei i te wā e huri ana hei tūngoungou.
He hui e āta whakawhiwhia ai ngā ākonga o tētahi whare mātauranga ki ā rātou tohu mātauranga.
He hui ka whakatūria hei whakatau i te tamaiti rangatira kātahi tonu ka whānau mai.
He hui whakamana, whakanui i te mārenatanga a tētahi tokorua.
He huihuinga e whakahaeretia ai ngā āhuatanga, ngā tikanga hei tangi, hei poroporoaki i te tūpāpaku.
He huihuinga ko tōna kaupapa nui he kanikani, he ngahau tahi ki ētahi atu, me te rere anō o te waiata, o te puoro i te taha.
He huinga ika e haere tahi ana.
He huinga ingoa tāngata, tau, aha atu rānei ka āta whakatakotoria kia whai mai tētahi i tētahi, kia raupapa anō pea te takoto mai.
He huinga kaka māeneene.
He huinga kararehe, tipu rānei e āhua ōrite ana te hanga, e taea ana te whakaputa uri tahi; koia te wehenga matua o raro rawa o te pūnaha tātai whakapapa o te ao pūtaiao; tētahi wehenga iti o tētahi huinga pēnei e ōrite tonu ana te hanga, he mea āta whakatipu pea e te tangata kia pērā.
He huinga korakora motuhake i pūtakea mai i te whenua, ko te maha atu i raweketia anō hoki e te ringa tangata.
He huinga kupu e kawe ana i tētahi whakaaro, e tū ana hei wāhanga motuhake o te rerenga.
He huinga kupu tū motuhake, e kawe ana i te whakaaro, i te pātai, i te whakahau, i te aha atu.
He huinga mano tini, ahakoa tāngata, ahakoa kararehe, ahakoa pepeke, aha atu rānei.
He huinga manu e noho tahi ana, e rere tahi ana, he huinga kararehe rānei e noho tahi ana.
He huinga matū kāore e kōputaputa ana, he kaha tonu te piri tahi o ngā matū o roto.
He huinga mea e piri tata ana.
He huinga mōhiti maitai kua hono tahi e oti mai ai he taputapu tāwariwari roa hei here, hei whakamau, hei tō haere i tētahi mea, e oti mai ai rānei he taonga whakapaipai tinana.
He huinga pata wai moroiti mano tini ka iri mai ki te hau takiwā, ka pātata tonu ki te mata o te whenua te iri mai.
He huinga pepeke mano tini e  rere tahi ana.
He huinga pōkurukuru, he kōpuku.
He huinga pūtau kōpae te hanga ka tipu i te kōpū o te whaea, o te whāereere, hei hono i ana toto ki ō te kukune, e whakawhitihia ai te hāora, te kai, me ngā para.
He huinga rākau e tū tahi ana, e tū motuhake mai ana i ētahi atu.
He huinga rākau o te momo kotahi e tū tahi ana.
He huinga rākau, pātītī, aha atu e piri tahi ana, e tupu tahi ana.
He huinga rārangi, he wāhanga nō tētahi waiata.
He huinga tikanga kua āta whakatakotoria, kua āta whakaraupapatia kia oti pai ai tētahi mahi; te tōpūtanga o ngā wāhanga o tētahi mea, mā te noho tōpū rawa, mā te mahi tahi rawa e tika ai te haere, te tū mai rānei o taua mea.
He huinga tikanga, he huinga kōrero ka hangaia, ka hāpaitia e tētahi mana tōrangapū hei ārahi, hei whakataki i ngā mahi a te iwi whānui; tētahi o ēnei tikanga, o ēnei kōrero.
He huinga toa whawhai.
He huinga tohutohu rorohiko ka tīkina atu hei whakatutuki i tētahi mahi ki te rorohiko.
He huinga tuna e rere tahi ana.
He huinga tāngata e hono tahi ana, e mahi tahi ana i raro i tētahi kaupapa.
He huinga tāngata e noho ana ki te wāhi kotahi, e whai ngātahi ana rānei i ētahi tikanga.
He huinga tāngata e tautoko ana i tētahi tangata whai mana.
He huinga tāngata e whai ana i ngā tikanga o tētahi wehenga o te whakapono Karaitiana.
He huinga tāngata e whai tahi ana i te huarahi kotahi ki tētahi wāhi.
He huinga tāngata he herenga toto, he herenga whakapapa ō rātou ki a rātou anō, he wāhanga rātou nō tētahi hapū, nō tētahi iwi.
He huinga tāngata huhua, he huinga manu, pepeke, aha atu rānei e huhua ana.
He huinga tāngata ka taka ki raro i te karangatanga kotahi.
He huinga tāngata ka whakakotahi i runga i tētahi kaupapa.
He huinga tāngata tino tokomaha.
He huinga tāngata whaimana ka whakakotahi i runga i tētahi kaupapa.
He huinga tōtā ka kitea e te karu, e rere ana i te rangi.
He huinga whetū e noho tauira mai ana i te rangi, kua tapaina te tauira ki tētahi ingoa.
He huinga whetū e tū tahi ana, e tū motuhake mai ana i ētahi atu.
He huinga whetū toiroa e āhua karapoti ana i te whetū e kīia nei ko Taumatakuku.
He huinga whānau, he huinga hapū, ka heke mai ō rātou kāwai whakapapa i te tupuna kotahi.
He hurihanga, he piko rānei i te taiapa.
He huru poto, he makiki, ka tipu i te kiri o te kararehe, i te kanohi rānei o te tāne.
He huruhuru kotahi o te manu tuatahi ka mau i te hunga patu manu, ka whakamahia i roto i ngā karakia kia nui atu te manu ka mau.
He huruhuru mai i te parirau o te toroa.
He huruhuru manu whero ka mahia hei tope, hei whakakai, hei whakarākei rānei.
He huruwhenua e 4 mita te roa o ngā rau taumaha, he pū te tupu, he uriuri, he mōhinuhinu ngā tawheraiti, he kai tōna akakōare.
He huruwhenua e 4 mita te roa o ngā rau taumaha.
He huruwhenua nunui toro nuku, he niho ririki kei ngā tawheraiti, he unahi mangaeka whai pokapū pāpango e rere ana i ngā tuaka, he māwhero ngā rau hou, kei ngā rau kōpiri ngā tihenga atua.
He huruwhenua nunui toro nuku.
He huruwhenua piki rākau, he tātā pūioio kōmiro whakarunga ōna, he pūngarungaru he roroa ngā rau, he kākāriki kitakita a runga, he kānapanapa te angamate.
He huruwhenua piki rākau.
He huruwhenua pū te tipu i ngā kōawaawa haukū o te ngahere, ka tipu ake i te akakōare whai unahi pāpango, he  roa tonu ngā tētē kākāriki, he pango parauri te pito whakararo o ngā kakau, ka kitea he punua huruwhenua e tipu ana i ngā rau.
He huruwhenua pū te tipu i ngā kōawaawa haukū o te ngahere.
He huruwhenua pū te tupu, he parauri ngā tātā, he karera, he roroa ngā rau, he pūkanikani, he tōpuku, he roroa ngā tawheraiti, e rua ngā rārangi tihenga atua e noho tata ana ki te tuaka o ngā tawheraiti. I ngā rā o mua i koropaepaehia te hāngi ki ngā rau o te huruwhenua nei kia kakara ai ngā kai. I tunua anō ngā pītau hei kai. I wakuwakua ngā pakiaka ka tāpi ki te kiri hei rongoā i te whēwhē.
He huruwhenua pū te tupu, he rau tūtika roroa ōna, he pāpango, he tōpuku, he kōratarata ngā tawheraiti, kei ngā tapa o ēnei ngā tihenga atua.
He huruwhenua pū te tupu, he ōriwa, he roa ngā rau, he tautau, he tūtika ngā rau whakapā parauri, he tōpuku ngā tawheraiti. I ngaungaua te huruwhenua nei hei rongoā i ngā mamae o te waha me te arero.
He huruwhenua pū te tupu.
He huruwhenua rākau te hanga, 10 mita te tupu, he toenga tuaka e rere ana i te kahiwi, he mā ngā tuaka me te taha whakararo o ngā rau. I ngā rā o mua he mea tāpi te iho o te huruwhenua nei ki te kiri hei rongoā i te kōpukupuku.
He huruwhenua rākau te hanga, e 2 mita te tupu, he kahiwi takoto i ōna wā, he kākāriki kōwhai ngā rau torutoru noa nei, he huruhuru parauri roa kei ngā tātā i te takahi, kia pakari haere, kua huruhuru kore.
He huruwhenua rākau te hanga, e 20 mita te tupu, he pororapa, he papatahi ngā nawe i te kahiwi pango, he pango, he mātotoru ngā tuaka o ngā rau. I tunua te iho o te huruwhenua nei i te hāngī hei kai, i tunua anō, i tāpia matatia rānei hei rongoā i ētahi mate i te kiri pērā i te whēwhē, i te kaiākiri. I tīkina anō ngā pakiaka i te takahi o te huruwhenua nei hei koropaepae i te putunga kai.
He huruwhenua rākau te hanga, e 6 mita te tupu, he mātotoru, he ura, he pukahu te kōhiwi, he whāiti, he kaitara ngā rau runga tātā poto, mātotoru ana te tautau o ngā rau maroke i raro mai i te kāuru. I tapahia te kahiwi o te huruwhenua nei hei koropaepae i te whare, i te putunga kai rānei.
He huruwhenua rākau te hanga, e 7 mita te tupu, he rau kaitara huapae te tupu, he toenga tuaka ka mahue ki te kahiwi, he tupu ā-uru tēnei huruwhenua.
He huruwhenua rākau te hanga, e 7 mita te tupu.
He huruwhenua rākau te hanga, e 8 mita te tupu, he rau māeneene roa huapae te tupu i te kahiwi parauri, ka mau tonu ngā tuaka o ngā rau maroke ki raro mai i te kāuru. I tunua te iho o te huruwhenua nei hei kai.
He huruwhenua rākau te hanga.
He huruwhenua toro nuku pū te tupu, he rau karera i te ohinga, kia pakari kua kārikiuri, e kapi katoa ana ngā rau i te tihenga atua. I ngā rā o mua i tunua ngā pītau hei kai.
He huruwhenua toro nuku pū te tupu.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, e 2 mita te tupu, he kaitara ngā rau, he tātā kōkōwai, he huru hāuratea kei ngā tētē. He kai matua ngā akaaka o te huruwhenua nei i ngā rā o mua.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, he kōratarata, he whakatīaho, he tākihi te hanga o ngā rau, he pūngarungaru ngā tapa.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, he rau tautau tātā roa, he kārikiuri, he kōratarata, kei ngā rau pūtokitoki ngā tihenga atua.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, toro rākau rānei, he rau kākāriki kitakita, he karera rānei, he rau angiangi, he whakatīaho, he huruhuru kore.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, toro rākau rānei, he rau ōriwa, he angiangi, he whakatīaho.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, toro rākau rānei, he ririki ngā rau, he tawheraiti tōpuku tō te mea toro nuku, he tawheraiti koikoi roa tō te mea toro rākau.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, toro rākau rānei.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, toro rākau, he tātā kāwekaweka ōna, he rau kakau roa, he whāiti ngā tawheraiti. He huruwhenua tēnei i whakamahia hei whakakakara i ngā makawe, i te tinana, i te whare, i pūpūhia anō hei tāhei ki te kakī.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, toro rākau.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, toro toka, toro rākau rānei, he tātā tuawhiti kāwekaweka, he rau kakau roa, he kōratarata, he whānui, he pokopoko, ka kitea ngā tihenga atua parauri e puku mai ana i waenga i ngā tapa me te tuaka o ngā rau. I tunua ngā tētē o te huruwhenua nei hei kai.
He huruwhenua toro nuku, toro toka, toro rākau rānei.
He huruwhenua toro nuku.
He huruwhenua whai kahiwi poto 1 mita te tupu, he kāwitiwiti ngā rau whakatīaho i ngā pito e rua, tūtū ai ngā tawheraiti i ngā tuaka iti.
He huruwhenua whai kahiwi poto 1 mita te tupu.
He huruwhenua whai kahiwi poto ina pakari, he pāpango, he whakatīaho ngā rau, he papatahi te noho mai o ngā tawheraiti i ngā tuaka iti.
He huruwhenua, he rākau te hanga.
He hāhi, tētahi atu whakahaere rānei he atua tōna, he apataki tōna e koropiko ana ki a ia.
He hākari hei whakanui i te moe a ētahi rangatira.
He hākari ka hora i te moenga, i te taumautanga rānei o tētahi tokorua.
He hākinakina e patua ai e ētahi kaitākaro e rua tētahi pōro ngohengohe iti ki te rākete, kia tika atu ai ki ngā pakitara o tētahi papa tākaro kei rō whare.
He hākinakina e rere ai te tangata i runga wai, me te tū ki tētahi papa whai kōmaru, ko te kōmaru anō te urungi.
He hākinakina e tākaro ai ētahi tīma e rua, tekau mā tahi kei ia tīma, he porowhita te pōro, ko te whāinga ia kia piro rātou mā te whana, mā te tuki rānei i te pōro ki te upoko, kia uru atu ai ki roto i te kupenga piro a te hoariri. Kotahi anō te tangata e whakaaetia ana kia pā ana ringa ki te pōro, ko te kaitiaki kupenga piro tērā.
He hākinakina e tākaro ai ētahi tīma e rua, tokoiwa kei ia tīma, e whā ngā pūrei kei te ara oma tapawhā te hanga; e piro ai te kaipatu me patu te pōro kia taea ai e ia te huri i tēnā, i tēnā pūrei me te kore e mau, e raru rānei i te hoariri.

He ika tai pāraharaha e 25-50 henemita te tipu, he kākāriki uriuri a runga, he āhua kōwhai a raro, ko ōna karu iti kei te taha matau o te upoko, ka takoto i tōna taha mauī. Ko ngā pakihawa ka rere huri noa i te tinana porohema, he pakupaku ngā unahi.
He ika tai pāraharaha e 35-50 henemita te tipu, he kiwikiwi, he āhua kākāriki, he parauri a runga, he whakanako uriuri anō kei runga.
He ika tai tuatete e 60 henemita te tupu, e tata ana te urutira me ngā paihau ki te hiku, he kākāriki, he kiwikiwi, he parauri rānei a runga, he mā a raro, kia wehi te ika nei kua whakatetere i a ia.
He ika tai tuatete e 60 henemita te tupu.
He ika tai, he nui te māhunga me te tinana porohita, e toru ngā manawa, he ngohengohe te āhua, e waru ngā kawekawe whai pata hei pupuri, hei piri. Ka eke ki te 1.5 mita te horahanga o ngā kawekawe.
He ika tōpuku te hanga, e pōtaea ana te tinana e te anga, he whakapaipai e rere ana i te anga, ko te upoko, te timu me ngā pakihau anake ka kōture mai i te anga.
He ika wai māori 10 henemita te tipu, he kiwikiwi, he pango rānei, he tāingoingo kei te tuarā me ngā kaokao, he tāwakawaka kei ngā pāpāringa me ngā paihau, he tāhekeheke horotea kei te pū o ngā pakipaki.
He ika wai māori 10 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori 10-12 henemita te tipu, he kiwikiwi, he kiwikiwi parauri rānei, e whā ngā tāhekeheke kei te tinana, me te mea nei kua pania a raro me ngā paihau ki te karaka, he pakohe ngā poto.
He ika wai māori 10-12 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori 120 henemita te tipu, he kahurangi, he ōriwa rānei a runga, he hiriwa mā ngā kaokao me te puku, he ōriwa te urutira me te hiku, me te mea nei kua pania ngā kaokao me te uhi pihapiha ki te whero, he iraira kei runga, kei te urutira me te hiku.
He ika wai māori 140 henemita te tipu, he hiriwa, he ōriwa parauri te tuarā, he iraira manauri kei te tuarā, te urutira, ngā uhi pihapiha me ngā kaokao, he iraira whero anō kei ngā kaokao.
He ika wai māori 15-20 henemita te tupu, he parauri ōriwa te tinana me te rere anō o ōna tāingoingo kiwikiwi pango, he karaka te urutira me te paihau o te tou, he ira pango kei runga ake i ngā pakipaki.
He ika wai māori 15-24 henemita te tipu, he ika pango, he pūmā a raro, he tāingoingo ōriwa kei ngā pāpāringa, he pāpango ngā tāingoingo i te tinana, he iraira kōura e rere ana i ngā kaokao.
He ika wai māori 15-24 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori 16-18 henemita te tipu, he kākāriki ki te ōriwa parauri te tinana me te rere anō o ōna tāingoingo kākāriki parauri, he iraira pango kei runga ake i ngā pakipaki, he manauri ngā paihau katoa.
He ika wai māori 16-18 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori e 20 henemita te tipu, he hāurauri ōriwa te tuarā me ngā kaokao, he tāhekeheke horotea anō kei te tinana, he hiriwa ōriwa a raro, he kōtingotingo pango kei runga ake i ngā pakipaki.
He ika wai māori e 20 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori e 20-25 henemita te tipu, he tōpuku, he pāraharaha te hanga, he pango ōriwa a runga, he pūmā a raro, he iraira horotea, he ura rānei kei runga, he iraira manauri kei raro.
He ika wai māori e 20-25 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori e 30-40 henemita te tipu, he hāurauri ki te ōriwa te upoko, te tuarā me ngā kaokao, me te rere anō o ōna tāingoingo kōura, he hiriwa ōriwa a raro, he iraira kōura kei te pū o ngā paihau.
He ika wai māori e 30-40 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori e 30-45 henemita te tipu, he kiwikiwi ōriwa, he ura rānei te tuarā, he hiriwa, he kororā rānei ngā kaokao, he hiriwa, he kōura rānei a raro, he hoata ngā paihau katoa.
He ika wai māori e 30-45 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori e 45-75 henemita te tupu, he rite ki te tuna te hanga, he pukepoto a runga, he hiriwa a raro, he pongāihu kotahi kei te tumuaki, e whitu ngā puta pihapiha kei ngā kaokao, he waha momimomi porowhita tōna.
He ika wai māori e 45-75 henemita te tupu.
He ika wai māori e 8 henemita te tupu, he rauwhero, he kiwikiwi parauri rānei te tinana, he tāhekeheke kei te upoko, he tāingoingo kei te tinana, he tāwakawaka kei ngā paihau.
He ika wai māori e 8 henemita te tupu.
He ika wai māori e 8-10 henemita te tipu, he kātoretore, he ōriwa te tuarā me te rere anō o ōna kōtingotingo kākāriki kiwikiwi, he ōriwa ngā kaokao, he hiriwa a raro, he hoata ngā paihau katoa.
He ika wai māori e 8-10 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori e 9-10 henemita te tipu.
He ika wai māori e 9-10 henemita te tupu, he ika kātoretore, he ōriwa te tuarā, me te mea nei kua pania ngā kaokao ki te waiporoporo, he hiriwa a raro, katoa ngā paihau he hoata.
He ika wai māori e 9-10 henemita te tupu.
He ika wai māori noho paru 10 henemita te tipu, he kiwikiwi parauri te tuarā me ngā kaokao, he manauri, he kākāriki parauri ngā tāingoingo, he kiwikiwi, he kahotea a raro, he parauri ngā paihau whai iraira i te pū.
He ika wai māori noho paru 10 henemita te tipu.
He ika whāngote e 2 mita te tipu, i ōna wā anō ka ū mai ki uta, he ihu koi tōna, he pākākā ngā huruhuru, me uaua ka kitea ngā taringa, he pakikau kei ngā kaokao me te timu.
He ika whāngote e 2 mita te tipu.
He ika whāngote nui whai huruhuru hāura pango, e 3 mita neke atu te tipu o ngā toa, 1.8 mita te tipu o ngā uwha, he iti ngā taringa, he pakikau kei ngā kaokao me te timu, he tau ki te rērere wai engari he pakihawa ki uta.
He ika whāngote nui whai huruhuru hāura pango.
He ika, he aha rānei ka tāpaea ki tētahi atua hei whakarata i a ia.
He ingoa (nō te tangata) e kaha ana te whakahuahuatia, i tua atu i tōna ingoa tūturu.
He ingoa karakia e mau ai te tohunga i tētahi maro i kīia he maro huka.
He ingoa karakia.
He ingoa kārangaranga mō te tangata.
He ingoa mō te hīnaki, te māhanga hopu manu me te kupenga ka waiho kia roa tonu ki te mahi i tāna mahi.
He ingoa mō te tino tāne, te tāne toa rānei o tētahi kōrero, tērā anō ka noho hei ingoa mōna.
He ingoa mō te tino wahine, te wahine toa rānei o tētahi kōrero, tērā anō ka noho hei ingoa mōna.
He ingoa mō te tūwhenua ina mate rawa, ina riro rawa ngā matimati.
He ingoa mō tētahi hahau ki te tokotoko.
He ingoa unahiroa.
He ingoa whetū.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā hanga ora ka tupu i te oneone pērā i te rākau, i te otaota, i te huruwhenua, i te pūkohu,  he rau, he tātā, he pakiaka ō te nuinga.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā ika tai tino nui, he niho ō ētahi, he pāhau ō ētahi, he tāpihapiha kei te upoko, kei te ua rānei, he whakapae te hiku, he pakihau ōna, he ika whāngote i ana kūao.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā ika tai tino nui.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā kahu ka mahia ki te kiri kurī.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā kahu tāniko.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā kākahu tūturu papai o te Māori ka uhia ki ngā pakihiwi, he poto ētahi, he roroa ētahi.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā mea ora anuanu nei te āhua, pērā i te mokomoko, te mangō, te whai, tae atu ki ngā pepeke me ngā pūngāwerewere.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā mea ora ka whai pua atua, kāore ōna rau, ōna tātā, ōna pakiaka, kāore rānei he kanokāriki o roto. Ko ētahi e mōhio nuitia ana ko te hōpurupuru me te harore tūturu.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā momo harakeke tino pai katoa mō te mahi muka, he harakeke ka taea te hāro ki te matikara.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā momo kākahu tūturu o te Māori ka uhia ki ngā pakihiwi, he kākahu waho, he poto ētahi, he roa ētahi.
He ingoa whānui mō ngā uwhi tinana ka whakamaua e te tangata.
He ingoa whānui mō te manu māori rongonui i te ao, he manu rerekore, he roa ngā ngutu, kei te pito o ngā ngutu ngā pongāihu, he taratara ngā huruhuru, he mātotoru ngā waewae, he manu haere pō.
He ingoa whānui mō te manu māori rongonui o te ao, he roa ngā ngutu.
He ingoa whānui mō te tātai mau rākau; he tātai mau rākau e puritia ai te rākau ki te paemanu, he tātai karo.
He ingoa whānui mō tētahi aitanga pepeke tino moroiti, he tini kei te kāhui kotahi, e rua, e toru rānei ō rātou hope whāiti, he whatīanga kei ngā pūhihi, e whā ngā parirau o ngā mea rere.
He ingoa whānui mō tētahi aitanga pepeke tino moroiti.
He ingoa whānui mō tētahi whānau manu tai, he whāiti iho te tinana o te nuinga i tō te karoro, te tarāpunga rānei, he hiku tokomanga ō ētahi.
He ingoa whānui mō tētahi whānau ngārara, he roa ngā tinana, he hiku roa anō ō rātou, e whā ō rātou waewae, he unahi e rere ana i te kiri, he tara anō ō ētahi.
He ingoa whānui mō tētahi whānau ngārara.
He ingoa whānui mō ērā o ngā iti a Tangaroa haere wai tai, wai māori, he tinana roroa, he kiri hāwareware, kāore ō rātou pakihawa, e hono ana te urutira me te pakihau o te tou i te taharapa.
He ingoa whānui mō ērā o ngā ngārara he roa te tinana me te hiku, he poto ngā waewae e whā, he kamo neke ōna, he unahi kei te tinana, he taratara rānei te kiri.
He ingoa whānui mō ētahi karakia e pā ana ki ngā tikanga mahi ika, mahi manu, me ētahi atu mahi pērā.
He ingoa whānui mō ētahi karakia maha tonu.
He inu e haurangi ai te tangata, ko te moītanga te pūtakenga mai.
He inu parauri ka mahia mai i ngā kākano o tētahi rākau pārūrū ka tunua, ka kauorotia kia nehu te āhua; te nehu e mahia ai te inu nei.
He inu reka ka mahia ki te wai, ki te huka, ki te huarākau anō pea, he huarākau anō te tāwara o te nuinga.
He io harakeke kuratea kōwhai hei whakaniko i ētahi momo kahu; he kākahu kua whakanikoa pēneitia.
He ipu hei kōhua kai, ka whakakīia ki te wai, ka kuhuna he kōhatu wera ki roto.
He ipu hei maka atu i ngā para kia kore ai e putu haere.
He ipu hei mimi mā te tangata, ka noho mai ki te rūma moe; he hanga pēnei mā te kōhungahunga.
He ipu hei pupuri wai, he kakau kei tētahi taha, he ngutu kei te niao hei riringi atu i te wai.
He ipu hei whakawera wai ki te tō, ki te hiko rānei.
He ipu i hangā ki tētahi wāhanga o te tahā.
He ipu i mahia ki te rimurapa, ki te kiri tōtara rānei, hei pupuri tītī kōtutu.
He ipu kōata he roa, he whāiti anō te tinana, he koropuku te tou, whakamahia ai i roto i ngā whakamātauranga taiwhanga pūtaiao.
He ipu maitai porotaka hei tao, hei whakamahana kai, hei tao rānei i te aha noa iho.
He ipu pararaha hei pupuri mea, hei tao kai rānei, he paparite te tou.
He ipu pararaha hei tunu kai ki roto.
He ipu porotaka āhua nui tonu ka hangā ki te rākau, ki te maitai rānei, ka puku mai a waenganui o ngā taha, he putunga kai, he putunga inu, he putunga aha atu rānei.
He ipu porowhita whai puritanga tiriwhana, hei kawe wai, aha atu rānei.
He ipu whānui te waha mō te wai, mō te kai, mō te aha atu, i ngā rā o mua i mahia ki te hue, i ēnei rā ka mahia ki te rākau, ki te karāhe, ki te uku, ki te aha atu.
He ipu, he papatahi te takere me ngā taha, he taupoki tōna, he tapawhā te hanga o te nuinga.
He iti nā Tangaroa haere tai, haere wai māori, he pihapiha, he pakikau, he unahi ō te nuinga.
He iwi pūrākau nahonaho, he kiritea, i ōna wā ka kitea i runga tūporo tipua e kautere ana i te waipuke, me te waiata haere anō.
He iwi pūrākau, he wairua tangata ka rere ā-tira i te takiwā, he iwi ka kitea e te matakite, e te matatuhi anahe.
He iwi tauhou, he iwi nō whenua kē atu, nō tāwāhi.
He iwi wairua, he iwi kēhua.
He kaha nō roto tonu i te tangata, nō te wairua, nō te hinengaro o te tangata.
He kaha whai mana.
He kahawai kua tata te pakari.
He kahawai kōpīpī, arā, kāore anō i pakari.
He kahiwi rākau kua waimanutia, kia mānu ai i te mata o te wai, e haere ai ka hoea ki te hoe.
He kahokaho takoto huapae i runga i ngā heke o te whare hei takotoranga mō ngā apa rauwhare.
He kahu e āhua rite ana ki te mangaeka, engari he poto ngā hukahuka.
He kahu harakeke ka mahia hei pare i te ua.

He kahu kaitara ka mahia ki te harakeke.

He kahu kiri kurī pango, he mea tuitui atu ngā ngaku kiri ki te kaupapa.
He kahu kiri kurī pango.
He kahu kiri kurī, he mea haehae te kiri kurī kia roroa ngā wāhanga whāiti, ka tuitui ai.

He kahu kua whakarākeitia ki ngā kihukihu he mā, he pango te tae.

He kahu kurī i whakamahia anō i te pakanga.

He kahu kōkau hei pare i te ua.

He kahu kōkau.

He kai arā noa atu ōna momo, he tino iti te nuinga, he mārō ētahi, he ngohengohe ētahi, ka nui te huka o roto.
He kai hei hari i tētahi haerenga.

He kai i te wāhi tapu, he takahanga tapu.

He kai ka mahia ki te miraka kua tepe, kua wehea mai i te waikuruwhatu.

He kai ka taona mō te tohi, hei kai mā ngā tāne anake.

He kai kopenu.

He kai mā te ohu, mā te rōpū mahi.

He kai reka ka whakamahia whānuitia hei whakareka i ētahi atu kai.
He kai reka, he ngohe, ka mahia ki te puehu parāoa, te hēki, te huka, te pata, te aha atu, te aha atu ka ranua, ka tunua ki te umu.
He kai tapu e pā ana ki te huamata, ki te tūātanga tamariki, ki te mate, ki te hahu, ki te aha atu.
He kai tapu hei kai mā ngā ariki o te kāwai mātāmua anahe.
He kai tapu ka tunua i te hahunga o te kōiwi, i te whānautanga tamariki, i ētahi atu wā hoki.
He kai tapu ka tāpaea ki tētahi atua.
He kai tapu mā te tohunga, mā te ariki, mā te tangata e noho tapu ana.
He kai, he kawenga hei hari i tētahi haerenga.
He kaiako whai mana i roto i tētahi kura wānanga.
He kaihoe, he kaimahi rānei o runga i tētahi waka.
He kaikōrero kakama te hinengaro, he mōhio anō ki te whakatakoto i te kupu kia ngahau tonu.
He kaimahi i runga i tētahi kaipuke, kei raro mai i te āpiha.
He kaimahi ka hika, ka tiaki hoki i te ahi tapu o te umu tapu.
He kaipuke kāore he pūkaha, he rā tōna, he roa, he teitei ngā niao, he hōhonu te riu.
He kaipuke pakanga, he taumaha, he nui, he kaha, he maha ngā hanga pērā i te pū repo kei runga; he kaipuke kua utaina ki ētahi hanga hei āwhina i te pakanga.
He kaiwhakaako i te whare wānanga.
He kaka harakeke kua oti te hāro, e rite ana mō te whatu, mō te whiri rānei.

He kanae iti.

He kanga e tohu ana i te kino, i te riri o te tangata ki tētahi atu, ki tētahi tūāhua rānei. (I takea mai i te whakaaro kia kōhuatia te upoko o te tangata.)
He kanoi poutū i te mahi whatu kākahu ka rere ki runga ki raro, ki runga ki raro i ngā aho.
He kapua angiangi, he teitei te iri iho ki te rangi, he mā te tae, he āhua rite ki te huruhuru manu, ki te whiore hōiho rānei ki te titiro atu. Tērā tonu ka kitea i te rangi i ngā rā paki.
He kapua e rere kōpurepure ana i te rangi.

He kapua pōuri kua pupuke mai i te rangi.
He kapua pōuri.
He kapua rite ki te haupū hune te āhua, he papatahi a raro, he pāpaku te iri iho ki te rangi, kitea ai i ngā rangi paki. He mā kitakita te nuinga, he ngangahu anō te hua.

He kapua tāekaeka roroa te hanga.
He kapua, he kohu rānei e whakakapi ana i te rangi, e rite katoa ana te āhua mai i tētahi pito ki tētahi.
He karakia e hikina ai te tapu e pā ana ki te hunga ora me te tūpāpaku, ki ngā mahi tā moko me ngā tāngata i whai wāhi atu, ki te ika tuatahi ka mau i te tamatāne.

He karakia whakatō kūmara.

He karamea kāore anō i pakari noa.
He karanga ki te whakatītina i ngā kaihoe.
He karanga tīorooro kia aro atu ai tētahi ki te kaikaranga; ka whakaputa i tēnei momo karanga.
He karanga, he pōhiri ki te manuhiri, ki te hoa, ki te whanaunga kia whakatata mai, kia uru mai.
He karangatanga angawaho, he noho moana, he noho awa te nuinga, ko ētahi e mōhio nuitia ana ko te kōura, ko te pāpaka, ko te kōuraura, ko te pāpapa.
He karangatanga tāngata nui tonu he āhuatanga ō rātou e motuhake ai, e rerekē ai rātou i ētahi atu huinga tāngata nui o te ao, pērā i te tae o te kiri, i tō rātou reo mātāmua, i ō rātou whenua tuku iho, i ā rātou kōrero tuku iho, i ā rātou tikanga tuku iho.
He kararehe iti he pūhina ngā huruhuru, 11-13 henimita tana roa mai i te upoko ki te hope, 12-15 henimita te roa o te whiore, e whā ōna waewae, i mauria mai ai e ngā tūpuna Māori i Hawaiki.
He kararehe iti, he kai kiko, he ngerungeru ngā huruhuru, e kaha ana te whakamōkaitia e te tangata.
He kararehe kai i ngā momo mea katoa, kiko mai, otaota mai (o te kararehe).
He kararehe kai kiko, kāore e kai otaota.
He kararehe kai otaota, kāore e kai kiko.
He kararehe kaiota, he huruhuru roa kei te ua me te whiore, he kararehe tēnei kua whakaratangia e te tangata hei hoa mahi mōna, hei eke rānei māna.
He kararehe kaiota, he uri nō te hōiho engari he pakupaku ake, he roroa ngā taringa, i ētahi whenua he tino kararehe tēnei hei pīkau i ngā hanga a te tangata.
He kararehe noho ngahere, noho wao, he parauri kiwikiwi ngā huruhuru ngerungeru, he nunui ngā karu, ka taea e ia tana whiore roa te takai ki te rākau, he kararehe haere pō.
He kararehe pūhina ngā huruhuru.
He kararehe pūhuruhuru 16-22 henimita te roa, e whā ōna waewae, noho ai i te whare, i te rākau, i mauria mai ki Aotearoa e te Pākehā.
He kararehe rata, he manu rata ka noho hei hoa mō te tangata; he tamaiti, he tangata rānei ka whakapuhingia, ka poporetia e tētahi atu.
He kararehe whai tuaiwi, he pūkahukahu ōna, he kiri unahi tiotio, he anga rānei tōna, ka whānau ngā uri i roto i tētahi hua kahu.
He kararehe whāngai i āna punua ki te waiū.
He kararehe whāngote e whā ngā waewae, he auau, he ngawī te waha, ko te nuinga ka noho mōkai, ka noho hoa mahi rānei mō te tangata.
He kararehe whāngote kai otaota, he mātotoru te wūru i te tinana, ka whakatipuria ā-rāhui nei e te tangata mō ngā wūru me ngā mīti; te kikokiko o te kararehe nei ka tunua hei kai.
He kararehe whāngote kai otaota, he whai pihi, he whai whiore poto, he pāhau anō tō te nuinga, he uri tata nō te hipi.
He kararehe whāngote tino kaitā, he kiwikiwi he hākorukoru te kiri, he ihu roa tōna, he rahi, he tīreparepa ōna taringa.
He kararehe whāngote tukituki whenua, he kaikiota, he huruhuru tūrukiruki kei te tinana, he papatahi te toi o te ihu, whakangaua ai, whakatupuria ai e te tangata hei kai; te kiko o te kararehe nei ka kainga hei mīti.
He kararehe, arā he whāngote apu whenua ki te mahi rua hei kāinga mōna, he roa ngā taringa, he roa ake ngā waewae o muri i ō mua, he mutumutu, he mā te whiore.
He kararehe, he aha atu e hono ana ki tētahi atu i te mea nō tētahi karangatanga kotahi.
He kararehe, he manu, he aha atu rānei ka puritia e te tangata hei hoa mōna.

He karere ka āta tukuna atu i tētahi rorohiko ki tētahi atu; te ara e tukuna ai tēnei momo karere.
He karetai iti.

He kiri rākau, he rauwhare rānei hei uhi i te tūpāpaku kua whakatakotoria ki runga kaupapa i tētahi rākau.
He kiri torongū kua pau katoa a roto i te āwhato te kai, he toenga tātā āwhato kei tētahi pito ōna.
He kirimana ōkawa i waenga i ētahi iwi mana motuhake, i ētahi whenua mana motuhake rānei.
He kite ā-wairua i ngā āhuatanga kāore anō kia pā mai.
He koha ka hoatu hei whakamihi i te tangata nāna tētahi koha mai ki a koe.
He koha nā te wahine ki tana tāne ina moe, ina mārena rāua.
He kohinga kupu ka whakahuatia (me te haere tahi anō pea o ētahi atu tikanga) i runga i te whakapono, i te tūmanako rānei ka whakamanatia mai, ka arohaina mai e te taha wairua, e te wāhi ngaro rānei.
He kohinga papatono ka whāngaihia atu ki te rorohiko e taea ai e te rorohiko te whakatutuki ētahi mahi e hiahiatia ana.
He kohinga weu kotahi, he weu kotahi rānei e whiria ai he au, he taura rānei.
He kohinga whārangi pepa whai tuhinga, whai tānga, kua tuia, kua whakapiria rānei tētahi o ngā tapa, kua uhia anō ki tōna uhi.
He kohinga, nō te momo kotahi, nō te karangatanga kotahi rānei ngā mea o roto.
He kohu mātotoru ka tau ki runga ki te whenua.
He koi (o te takere o te waka).
He koki, he ānau rānei i tētahi mea roa pēnei i te huarahi, i te awa, i te paipa, i te aha atu.
He kongakonga toka e taea ana e te tangata te neke, te hiki, te whiuwhiu, te aha atu rānei.
He konganuku aukume, he hiriwa kiwikiwi te tae, he mārō, he kaha, he kōngohe, whakamahia nuitia ai hei hanga taputapu. (Tohu pūtaiao: Fe)
He konganuku he mā-kahurangi, he mā-hiriwa rānei te tae, koia tētahi o ngā mea e hangaia ai te kuratea, ka whakamahia anō hei kiri tiaki i te rino me te maitai kia kore ai e waikura. (Tohu pūtaiao: Zn)
He konganuku hiriwa mā, he kaha, he tino māmā, he kōngohe, he papare tāna i te waikura.  (Tohu pūtaiao: Al)
He konganuku ka kaingākautia nuitia, he kiwikiwi mā, he mōhinuhinu te āhua, he tino kōngohe, whakamahia nuitia ai hei hanga taonga whakapaipai, hei hanga kahurangi, aha atu, aha atu; he tae rite ki te konganuku nei te āhua. (Tohu pūtaiao: Ag)
He konganuku ka kaingākautia nuitia, he kōwhai te tae, he tino kōngohe, ka taea anō te paopao kia angiangi tonu, whakamahia nuitia ai hei hanga taonga whakapaipai, hei hanga kahurangi, aha atu, aha atu, he momo moni anō; he tae rite ki te konganuku nei te āhua. (Tohu pūtaiao: Au)
He konganuku kōngohe, he māngohe, koia te ranunga o te konukura me te konutea.
He konganuku māmā, he kōngohe, he kōmā hiriwa te tae. (Tohu pūtaiao: Mg)
He konganuku ngohe, he mā-hiriwa te tae, ka tino kitea i te tote. (Tohu pūtaiao: Na)
He konganuku taumaha he kiwikiwi kahurangi te tae, he kōngohe, he māngohe, he āhuatanga tāoke tōna. (Tohu pūtaiao: Pb)
He konganuku whero, he ngongohe, he pai hei kawe i te hiko, i te mahana. (Tohu pūtaiao: Cu)
He konganuku, he ngohe, he kiwikiwi-mā te tae, ko te pākeho tētahi o ōna pūtakenga mai. (Tohu pūtaiao: Ca)
He konganuku, he ranunga konganuku rānei ka whakamahia hei hanga taputapu.
He korakora tino iti e amio ana i te karihi o te ngota, he whana tōraro tōna.
He korakora tino iti kei te karihi o te ngota, he whana tōrunga tōna he rite ki te kaha o te whana tōraro o te irahiko.
He korakora tino iti kei te karihi o te ngota, kāore kau ōna whana hiko.
He koropiko harakeke kei waenganui i te rākau ka whiua i ngā karakia o te niu.
He korowhititanga i te pakihiwi, he tohu kino.

He kou, he puku pērā i te hanga kei te reke o te huata, o te mere.
He kuaka kua roa ngā rā ki te ao, kua tūnohunohu.

He kupenga hanga kete roa nei te āhua mō te hopu tuna.

He kupenga hanga rite ki te kete te āhua mō te piharau.
He kupenga hei koko mai i te kahawai i te wai.

He kupenga iti hei hao ā-ringa i te ika.
He kupenga iti ka kuhuna ki te waha o te hīnaki kia kore ai ngā tuna e puta.
He kupenga iti kei runga atu te raumata i te mōwhiti, ka kumea tētahi aho i konei kia kopi ai te waha.
He kupenga iti mō te hao ika wai māori.
He kupenga iti mō te hao īnanga.

He kupenga ka puritia ki te ringa hei hao kōkiri me ētahi atu ika.
He kupenga ka puritia ki te ringa hei te hao ika.
He kupenga ka puritia ki te ringa.
He kupenga ka whakamauria ki ētahi pou kua poua atu ki te au o te tai.
He kupenga kua tuia ki te koropewa mō te hao tarakihi.
He kupenga kua whakamaua atu ki te koropewa hei hopu kōura, īnanga, me ētahi atu ika ririki.
He kupenga mō te hao kōkopu ka puritia ki te ringa.
He kupenga mō te hao kōuraura.
He kupenga mō te tuna.
He kupenga rahi mō te hao ika i te moana.
He kupenga rahi tonu, 10 mārō te roa, he iti iho i te kaharoa.
He kupenga tapawhā ka mōunutia ki te tuangi, ki te pāpaka, ki ētahi atu mea rānei hei hopu manu moana.
He kupenga tino nui i āta hangaia tuatahitia tēnā me tēnā wāhanga, kātahi ka honoa katoatia kia kupenga kotahi.
He kupenga tino nui rite ki te hīnaki te hanga, ka tukua ki ngā awa e paria ana e te tai.
He kupenga waha nui e hono ana ki te hīnaki hei ārahi i ngā tuna ki te waha.
He kupenga whai kakau roa hei kawe mai i te ika pērā i te kahawai ki uta.
He kupu e kaha whakakāhore ana i tētahi kōrero kua puta, e āhua rite ana ki te 'kore rawa'.
He kupu e pā ana ki te ingoa tapu ka tapaina ki te tamaiti a te ariki, na, ka tapu rā pea taua kupu i te whakamahinga o taua kupu hei ingoa mō taua tamaiti.
He kupu e pātai ana mō te maha o ētahi mea.
He kupu e pātai ana pēhea te tawhiti.

He kupu e tohu ana i te tamaiti e aroha nuitia ana.
He kupu e tohu ana i te tangata e aroha nuitia ana.
He kupu e tohu ana i te tau, tatau nei.
He kupu e tohu ana i te taupatupatu o te āhuatanga whai i muri mai ki tētahi atu kei mua e rere ana.
He kupu e tohu ana i te urunga mai, i te tāpiritanga mai o tētahi atu mea ki roto i te whakaaro kua takoto i mua atu.
He kupu e tohu ana i te āhua taupatupatu o te whakaaro whai i muri tonu mai i a ia, ki tētahi atu kei mua, kei muri rānei e rere ana.
He kupu e tohu ana i te āhua taupatupatu o te āhuatanga whai i muri mai ki tētahi atu kei mua e rere ana.
He kupu e tohu ana i tētahi wāhi e tata ana ki te kaiwhakarongo, i tētahi wāhi rānei kāore e tino tata ana ki te kaikōrero.
He kupu e tohu ana i tētahi wāhi kāore e tata ana ki te kaikōrero, ki te kaiwhakarongo rānei.
He kupu e tohu ana i tētahi wāhi, i tētahi āhuatanga e tata ana ki te kaikōrero, i tētahi mea rānei kātahi tonu ka whakahuatia ake.
He kupu e tohu ana mā te kaikōrero te mea, te mahi, te aha atu e kōrerotia ana.
He kupu e tohu ana mā te kaiwhakarongo te mea, te mahi, te aha atu e kōrerotia ana.

He kupu e tohu ana nā te kaiwhakarongo te mea, te mahi, te aha atu e kōrerotia ana.

He kupu e tohu ana nō te kaikōrero te mea e kōrerotia ana.
He kupu e tohu ana nō te kaiwhakarongo te mea e kōrerotia ana.
He kupu e tohu ana nō tētahi tangata i tua atu i te kaikōrero me te kaiwhakarongo te mea e kōrerotia ana.
He kupu e tono ana kia āta aro mai te kaiwhakarongo ki tētahi mea e tata ana, e hono ana rānei ki te kaikōrero.
He kupu e whakaatu ana i te whakahē, i te whakakāhore i te wā kua hipa. Ka mātua whai iho ko te kupu 'i'.
He kupu e whakaatu ana me mahi tētahi mahi i taua wā tonu. Ka tū i muri i te kīanga kei reira taua mahi e whakaingoatia ana.
He kupu e whakahau ana i te tangata kia tatari mō tētahi wā.
He kupu e whakahau ana i te tangata kia whakamutu i tētahi mahi.
He kupu e whakakāhore ana i ētahi whakatakoto.
He kupu hei hono i ētahi kōrero e rua, e tohu ana ko te mea tuarua ka whai mai i te mea tuatahi, ka haere tahi rānei ki te mea tuatahi.
He kupu hei mihi i te tangata ahakoa tāne, ahakoa wahine.
He kupu hei whakahau i te ope taua kia rere ki te taupoki i te hoariri.
He kupu iti ka tū i mua i te tūingoa, i te tūkapi, i te tūwāhi, i te tūwā, me te whakaatu i tētahi hononga ki tētahi atu, ki ētahi atu kupu i te rerenga.
He kupu iti ka tū i mua, i muri rānei i te tūmahi, ka whakaatu i ētahi āhuatanga e pā ana ki taua mahi, pērā i te wā i tū ai, mehemea rānei he mahi auau, he mahi e tika ana kia mahia, kia kaua rānei e mahia.
He kupu ka haere tahi me te 'wāwā' e tohu ana ki hea noa, ki hea noa.
He kupu ka haere tahi me te 'wīwī' e tohu ana ki hea noa, ki hea noa.
He kupu ka hono i ētahi kōrero e rua.
He kupu ka hono i ētahi kōwhiringa e taea ana.
He kupu ka huaina i ngā mōteatea, i te mutunga o ētahi rārangi kōrero. Kāore ōna whakamārama tūturu, heoi anō pea tāna he whakaū i te tangi o te ngākau, he whai kia huatau te kupu.
He kupu ka mahi tahi ki ngā pūmahi wāheke, tae atu ki ētahi atu pūmahi, ki te kawe i te whakakāhoretanga.
He kupu ka noho hei wāhanga tuatahi o te ingoa o tētahi iwi, o tētahi hapū rānei e tohu ana he uri rātou nō te tupuna e tū ana i muri o tēnei kupu.
He kupu ka noho hei wāhanga tuatahi o te ingoa o tētahi rōpū e tohu ana he huihuinga tāngata rātou i whakakotahitia i runga i tētahi kaupapa, i tētahi āhuatanga rānei i pā ki a rātou.
He kupu ka noho i muri i tētahi rerenga me te huri i taua kōrero hei pātai, e akiaki ana i te kaiwhakarongo kia whakaae mai ki tā te kaikōrero i kī ai.
He kupu ka noho mai ki mua i te ingoa tangata, te ingoa wāhi me ngā tūkapi 'mea' me 'wai', ina tū ēnei hei tāhū mō tētahi rerenga, ina whakarārangitia rānei ēnei; ki mua i te ingoa tangata me te tūkapi (hāunga anō te 'ahau' me te 'awau') i muri i ngā pūtūmua 'i', 'ki', 'hei', 'kei'.
He kupu ka puta i te tangata e whakamārama ana i tētahi āhuatanga e whakapono ana ia ka eke ā tōna wā; ka whakaputa i tēnei tūmomo kupu.
He kupu ka rere i te waha o te tangata, e whakaatu ana i tana ohorere, i tana mīharo rānei ki tētahi tūāhua, e haukoti ana rānei i te kōrero a tētahi atu.
He kupu ka tae ake ki te taringa e whakaatu ana i tētahi āhuatanga kua pā.
He kupu ka tohu i tētahi mahi, i te pānga rānei o tētahi āhuatanga.
He kupu ka tāpiria ki mua i te ingoa o te tangata, ka whakamahia rānei hei whakakapi i tana ingoa, hei tohu i tētahi taumata kua ekea e ia.
He kupu ka tū hei pātai, ka whakataki rānei i te pātai.
He kupu ka tū hei whakakapi mō te tūingoa, e tohu ana i tētahi mea, i tētahi tangata rānei kua whakahuatia kētia, e mōhiotia ana rānei.
He kupu ka tū i mua i te tūmahi, e āhua whakahau ana, e whakahau tonu ana rānei i te tangata kia mahi i tētahi mahi, e tohu ana e tika ana kia mahia taua mahi.
He kupu ka tū i mua i tētahi atu kupu e tohu ana he whanaunga te tangata ka whakahuatia i muri mai.
He kupu ka tū i mua tonu i te tūingoa, ka whakawhāiti i te aronga o taua tūingoa.
He kupu ka tū i muri i te tūingoa, i te tūmahi rānei, ka whakawhāiti i tōna aronga.
He kupu ka tū i muri tonu i te tūmahi, e whakaahua ana i taua mahi, he huinga kupu rānei e whakaahua ana i taua mahi.
He kupu ka whakaahua i te tūingoa.
He kupu ka whakahuatia kia aro mai te tangata e kōrero atu ana koe.
He kupu ka whakaingoa, ka tohu i tētahi mea.
He kupu ka whakakāhore i te kōrero.
He kupu ka whakataki i tētahi kōrero hou e tautoko ana, e whakaū ana i te whakaaro kātahi tonu nei ka takoto atu.
He kupu ka whakataki i tētahi kōrero hou, e tohu ana he āhuatanga kei taua kōrero e āhua rite ana ki te whakaaro kātahi tonu nei ka takoto atu.
He kupu ka whiua e tētahi ki te tangata tonu e kōrero atu ana ia, hei tohu kua tau atu ki runga i taua tangata tētahi āhuatanga kino e tika ana kia tau atu ki a ia, arā, nāna tonu i kimi tana mate.
He kupu ka whiua hei tohu kua tau atu ki runga i tētahi tangata he āhuatanga kino e tika ana kia tau atu ki a ia, arā, nāna tonu i kimi tana mate.
He kupu ka whiua ki te whakaiti, ki te whakahāwea i te tangata.
He kupu karakia ka whakahuatia tahitia me ētahi atu kupu pēnei i te tauira, i te atua, i te tohunga, i te kete, me ētahi atu.

He kupu mō te kākā kua kore e eke ki te rangi, i te mea kua mōmona rawa.

He kupu tū motuhake e pātai ana kei hea ake tētahi mea kātahi tonu ka tohua, ka kōrerotia rānei e tētahi atu.

He kupu tū motuhake e whakaatu ana i te mīharo, i te ohorere.
He kupu tū motuhake e whakaatu ana i te ohorere, i te mīharo, i te whakahē me ētahi atu kaupapa.
He kupu tū motuhake e whakaatu ana i te ohorere, i te mīharo, i te āwangawanga, me ētahi atu āhuatanga pēnei.
He kupu tū motuhake e whakaatu ana i te ohorere, i te mīharo.
He kupu tū motuhake e whakaatu ana i te ohorere, i te whakahē, i te whakatakariri, i te aha atu. He wā anō ka whai mai ko te kupu 'hoki'.
He kupu tū motuhake e whakaatu ana i te ohorere; he wā anō e kawe ana anō hoki i tētahi whakaaro pērā i te hōhā, i te whakahē, i te whakatakariri o te kaikōrero - ki tētahi atu, ki a ia tonu rānei.

He kupu tū motuhake e whakautu ana i te pātai, i tētahi atu momo kōrero rānei, e whakaatu ana i te ohorere, i te kore whakapono anō pea o te kaikōrero.
He kupu wetereo e tohu ana i te wā kei te heke mai.

He kupu whakakaha ka piri ki ngā kupu mō te maroke (hei tohu i te tino kino o te maroke).
He kupu whakakaha ka piri ki te kupu 'maroke' (hei tohu i te tino kaha o te maroke).
He kupu whakakaha ka piri ki te kupu 'mārama'.
He kupu whakakaha ka whai mai i te kupu 'tini' me ētahi atu kupu mō te maha, tae atu ki ētahi atu kupu ruarua nei.
He kupu whakakaha ka whai mai i te kupu 'tini' me ētahi atu kupu mō te maha.
He kupu whakakaha, ka kaha te whai mai i te kupu 'taumaha'.
He kupu whakakāhore i ngā momo kōrero maha, tae atu ki ērā e tīmata ana ki te pūmau me te pūmahi. Ka kaha te whai mai o tētahi pūmuri pērā i te 'kau', i te 'rawa', i te 'anō', i te 'atu', i te 'ake' rānei.
He kupu whakakāhore, whakamahia ai hei whakakāhore i ngā momo whakahau katoa. Ko te 'e', ko te 'hei' rānei te pūmahi ka tohu i te tūmahi, te tūāhua rānei ka whai i muri mai.
He kupu whakamihi ki te kuia, ki te koroua rānei.
He kupu whakamihi ki te kōtiro.
He kupu whakamihi ki te tāne taipakeke, ki te tāne whai mana rānei.
He kupu whakamihi ki te tāne taipakeke; he kupu whakamihi ki te koroua.
He kupu whakamihi ki te wahine; he kupu whakamihi ki te kuia; he kupu whakamihi ki te wahine kua whai tamariki.
He kupu whakamihi ki te wahine; he kupu whakamihi ki te wahine kua whai tamariki.
He kupu whakarite ka uhia ki runga i te tangata rongonui i tōna matenga, hei whakanui i a ia.
He kupu whakarite mō te aruhe.
He kupu whakarite mō te hē, mō te hapa ina whakahuahua i te karakia.
He kupu whakarite mō te kai.
He kupu whakarite mō te ngākau māia i uhia e te tohunga ki runga i te toa i ngā karakia waitaua o mua i te pakanga.
He kupu whakarite mō te pā whawhai.
He kupu whakarite mō te rangatira tino nui.
He kupu whakarite mō te rangatira.
He kupu whakarite mō te tangata kāore e āta tau, kāore e tau te noho.
He kupu whakarite mō te tangata pukumahi.
He kupu whakarite mō te toa māia.
He kupu whakarite mō te toa whawhai.
He kupu whakarite mō te tōtara me ērā atu rākau nunui o te ngahere ka waimanutia hei waka; te waka tonu ka oti mai.
He kupu whakarite mō te ua kōehuehu.
He kupu whakarite mō te waka, ka rangona i roto i ngā mōteatea.
He kupu whakarite mō te whenua nui tonu, hāunga te moana.
He kupu whakataki i te whakaaro e whakapuakina ana e te tangata, e tohu ana nō wai ake taua whakaaro.
He kupu whakataki i te whakamihinga, i te whakahēnga rānei (o te mea ka whakahuatia i muri mai).
He kupu whakataki pātai e kimi ana nō tēhea wā i pā ai tētahi āhuatanga.
He kupu whakatangata i te hau.
He kupu whakautu e whakaatu ana i te whakaae.
He kupu whakautu e whakaatu ana i te whakaae. Mēnā e whakautu ana i te pātai whakakāhore, e whakaū ana i te whakaaro whakakāhore o roto.
He kupu whakautu i te pātai whakakāhore, e whakaū ana i te whakaaro ka takoto ki taua pātai.
He kupu whānui mō ngā mea ka āta hangaia hei kawe i te tāngata, i te utanga, i te aha atu, ka haere i te moana, i te whenua, i te rangi rānei.
He kupu whānui mō te taonga tākaro.
He kupu ā-tuhi, ā-waha rānei e whakaputa whānui ana i tētahi kōrero.
He kura e haere ai te ākonga ki te whai i ngā mātauranga mō te whakaako, kia puta ai hei kaiako.
He kura e kawe ana i ngā akoranga o te kura tuarua, ko te reo Māori te reo whakaako, e haere ai ngā ākonga o ngā kura kaupapa, o ngā akomanga rumaki rānei.
He kura mō ngā taiohi tekau mā rua ki te tekau mā waru tau te pakeke.
He kura mō ngā tamariki mai i te rima ki te tekau mā rua tau te pakeke, ko te reo Māori te reo whakaako, he Māori anō ngā tikanga whakahaere.
He kuru, he mea hanga ki te kōhatu.
He kāeo e paku tonu ana.
He kāhu e ohi tonu ana, e hāurauri tonu ana te nuinga atu o ngā huruhuru.
He kāhu kua koroua, kua hina ngā huruhuru.
He kāhu pīrere.
He kāhui atua tāne tino tapu kei Tikitiki-o-Rangi.
He kāhui atua wāhine tino tapu kei Tikitiki-o-rangi.
He kāhui kererū.
He kāhui manu.
He kāhui waka ka rere tahi, ka hoe tahi.
He kāhui whetū rangatira, ko Takurua te whetū kōratarata o roto, koia anō te whetū tino kōratarata e kitea ana i te rangi.
He kāinga ka uaua te tomokia, te whakaekea i te mea e karapotia ana e te maioro, e te tūwatawata, e te aha atu hei ārai atu i te hoariri.
He kākahu e rite ana ki te maro, he pango te tae.
He kākahu e āhua rite ana ki te piupiu, he mea hāngungu ētahi wāhanga o ia mātātara harakeke, ko ētahi wāhanga ka waiho kia rūmene noa.
He kākahu harakeke kaitara ka heke iho i te hope ki ngā turi.
He kākahu harakeke, he makiki, he mangungu te āhua o te whatu, ka tāpekatia ki te tinana hei whakangungu rākau.
He kākahu he mea āta hoahoa kia whakamaua tahitia ōna wāhanga e rua, neke atu, pēnei i te koti me te tarau, i te koti me te panekoti.
He kākahu iti mō ngā pakihiwi.
He kākahu ka heke iho i te hope ki ngā rekereke, e rua ngā wāhanga motuhake, tētahi mō tēnā waewae, tētahi mō tēnā.
He kākahu ka heke iho i te hope ki ngā turi.
He kākahu ka heke iho i te hope ki te takiwā ki ngā pona,  e rua ngā wāhanga motuhake, tētahi mō tēnā waewae, tētahi mō tēnā.
He kākahu ka mahia ki ngā rau harakeke kāore i hāroa.
He kākahu ka mahia ki te harakeke, he whānui tonu te hope, he harakeke memenge ka whatua ki te hope ka waiho kia tautau iho.
He kākahu ka mauria e te tohunga i a ia e whakahua ana i te maro huka.
He kākahu ka takaia ki te ringa hei whakapuru rākau whawhai.
He kākahu ka whatua ki te whītau, ka pania ki te hōrū.
He kākahu kaitara hei ārai atu i te ua, ka whatua ki te harakeke, kaua ki te muka.
He kākahu kua taretare, kua kino te āhua nā te roa e whakamahia ana.
He kākahu mō te taha whakarunga o te tinana ka whatua mai i ngā hanga pēnei i te wūru.
He kākahu mō te wahine ka heke iho i te hope ki ngā turi.
He kākahu mō te wahine, mō te kōtiro ka tautau iho i te hope ki ngā waewae.
He kākahu ringa roa, kei ngā pona, kei ngā rekereke rānei te roa, ka mau ki waho atu o ngā kākahu katoa ina haere i te makariri, i te ua.
He kākahu rite ki te korowai, engari kāore he hukahuka.
He kākahu tangi e tohu ana i te mamae, i te pōuri, i te aroha ki tētahi kua mate.
He kākahu whawhai pītongatonga hei kaupare atu i ngā weronga mai a te tao, a te aha atu ki te uma.
He kākahu āhua rite ki te piupiu, engari he roa ake.
He kākahu, he papanga rānei kua taretare, kua kino te āhua nā te roa e whakamahia ana.
He kākano porotaka iti, he kākāriki te tae, ka tupu i roto i te pākākano, he huawhenua; te tipu nō reira mai te kai nei.
He kākā ka hopukia hei mōkai mō te rangi kotahi.
He kākā ka ākona ki te karehā kia pai ai te onga i ētahi atu kākā.
He kākā mā; he kupu whakarite anō mō te taonga kāore e tino kitea.
He kānga pakari kua waiho ki te wai kia pirau haere, he kai.
He kāpara kua whakataerangitia ki te tarawai hei pani ki te kiri kua haehaea ki te uhi tā moko.
He kāri mārō ka mahia ki te pepa tupenu.
He kāwai tangata, he whānau rānei kāore he uri e ora ana, kua mate oti atu.
He kāwai whakapapa heke iho i te taha tāne.
He kāwai whakapapa heke iho i te taha wahine.
He kāwai whakapapa ka heke tōtika mai i tētahi tupuna.
He kēmu e makaia ai ētahi rākau poto tētahi ki tētahi, me te waiata i tētahi waiata.
He kēmu e noho ai tētahi tangata ki tētahi pito o te papa rākau, he tumu anō kei waenganui hei toko, he tangata anō i tētahi pito, ka heke, ka piki.
He kēmu e tākaro ai ētahi tamariki e rua neke atu, ko tā te tamaiti tuatahi he pupuri i ana ringa ki mua i tana tinana kapu ki te kapu, ko tā te tuarua he miri i te angamate o ana ringa ki ngā kapu o ōna, kātahi ka taki haere i ana kupu. Nā wai ā, kua werohia atu e te tamaiti tuarua tana kōnui ki ngā ringa e kapu mai rā, ā, ko te whāinga ia kia mau te kōnui o tētahi ki ngā kapu o te ringa o tētahi.
He kēmu e tōia ai tētahi rau i roto i te ringa meke, me te pātai anō kua tae te pito o te rau ki hea.
He kēmu e whiua ai te teka mai i tētahi tangata ki tētahi atu.
He kēmu, he taonga tākaro rānei ka tāraia hei whakamātau, hei wero i te hinengaro o te tangata ka riro māna e whāwhā, e whakaoti.
He kōawa iti e rere atu ana ki tētahi awa nui tonu.
He kōawa ka whati mai i te awa matua me te ahu ki wāhi kē.
He kōhao e purua atu ai te puru hiko hei hono atu i te taputapu hiko ki te puna hiko.
He kōhatu iti, he porotaka, he matā nā te Māori i te pakanga o te tau 1865.
He kōhatu ka purua atu ki te kōpua i te taha whakararo o te kaharoa kia noho tonu ai tērā pito ki raro i te wai.
He kōhatu kiripaka pūwhero i whakamahia i ngā karakia o te whare wānanga.
He kōhatu kiwikiwi uri i keria nuitia i ngā rā o nehe i Whakatū, i Te Waipounamu.
He kōhatu kua haupūngia.
He kōhatu mārō whai takawai, he māene he kiwikiwi te āhua, kia pātukia ki te rino ka puta he kora.
He kōhatu mō te kōtaha.
He kōhatu pango.
He kōhatu porohita ka whakamahia hei kuoro i te kōkōwai.
He kōhatu puia i whakamahia hei tao kai.
He kōhatu pāpango mārō hei hanga taputapu.
He kōhatu ririki, he kōhatu rānei kua wāhia kia pakaru rikiriki.
He kōhatu taumaha ka whakamaua ki te aho hī ika kia totohu ai.
He kōhatu, tētahi atu mea rānei ka whakamahia hei wāhi mō te karakia whakaū.
He kōheru e kōpīpī tonu ana.
He kōhine, he wahine i heke mai i te kāwai ariki, i te kāwai rangatira.
He kōiraira tino iti, he wāhanga tino iti rānei (o tētahi mea).
He kōiwi mō te kaui ika.
He kōiwi nō te waha o te kewa.
He kōiwi pango nō te kewa.
He kōiwi tapu kei te pito o te iwi tuaroa ki te kakī, e tohu ana i te mana o te tangata.
He kōiwi, he kōhatu rānei he mōhiti te hanga, ka whakamaua ki te waewae o te mōkai manu kia kore ai te waewae e motu i te here.
He kōkiri ngātahi i te hoariri i te wā kotahi.
He kōmaru i hangā motuhaketia mō te waka taua.
He kōpaki kirihou papatahi iti, he tēpa autō kei roto hei hopu, hei whakatangi oro.
He kōpaki kirihou papatahi, he tēpa autō kei roto hei hopu, hei whakatangi oro, hei hopu, hei whakaatu āhua.
He kōpaki, he pouaka rānei e mau mai ana ngā kōrero mō tētahi kaupapa, mō tētahi tangata rānei, he mea āta whakarārangi i te taha o ētahi atu, e māmā ai te tiki atu ina hiahiatia.
He kōpata wai tai ririki ka rere ki te hau takiwā i te ākinga a te hau.
He kōpua i tētahi awa, he hōhonu, he kāniwhaniwha.
He kōpūtea e kōpīpī tonu ana.
He kōrero e rere haere ana i waenganui i ētahi, engari kāore pea i te pono.
He kōrero e whakaahua ana i ngā unahiroa.
He kōrero e whakaahua ana i te mīharo, i te ahurei o tētahi mea.
He kōrero e whakaatu ana i te koa o te tangata, i te pai o tana wairua.
He kōrero e whakaatu ana i te pono, i te tika o tētahi āhuatanga, ki tā te kaikōrero titiro.
He kōrero e whakaatu ana i te whanowhanoā o te tangata,  i te hē o tana wairua.
He kōrero hei ārahi i te tangata, e kī atu ana me aha ia, me pēhea ia.
He kōrero ka hariharia e te tangata, ehara pea i te kōrero pai, i te kōrero pono rānei.
He kōrero ka puta i te tangata e whakaatu ana i tana whai kia mātua tutuki tētahi āhuatanga, ahakoa te aha.
He kōrero ka tuhia, ka tukuna anō ki te tangata māna ngā kōrero o roto.
He kōrero ka tāpaea ki te aroaro o te tangata e whewhera ana i ētahi āhuatanga i tirohia, e whakaatu ana i ētahi mea i kitea.
He kōrero ka tāpaea ā-waha ki tētahi huihuinga hei whakaako, hei tohutohu i a rātou.
He kōrero ka tāraia e te hinengaro, kāore ōna mana, kāore ōna kiko.
He kōrero ka āta tukua, ka āta waiho rānei mā tētahi atu.
He kōrero kiko kore, tikanga kore.
He kōrero kino ka puta whānui mō te mahi hē a te tangata, ahakoa kāore e pono ana.
He kōrero kāore i pono.
He kōrero mō ngā rangi makariri o te takurua.
He kōrero mō tētahi mahi e whakaarotia ana he tino kino, e riri ai te iwi, te marea.
He kōrero pono, he kōrero paki rānei ka hopukia ki te kāmera e waihangatia ai he āhua nekeneke hei whakaatu ki te pātū, ki te pouaka whakaata rānei.
He kōrero poroporoaki ki te tangata e noho mai ana i tawhiti.
He kōrero poroporoaki nā te tangata e wehe atu ana ki te tangata e noho tonu ana.
He kōrero pāngarau e whakaatu ana i te ōrite o ētahi rahinga e rua, ā, me te noho mai o te tohu '=' ki waenganui.
He kōrero tuku iho nō te ao o nehe e mōhio whānuitia ana, he kōrero atua, he kōrero e whakaahua ana i te pūtakenga mai o ngā momo mea katoa ki te ao.
He kōrero tuku iho, he iti te kupu, he hōhonu te whakaaro, he tohutohu, he kaupapa pono anō ōna; ka mea hei whakataukī, ka kuhu atu rānei ki te whakataukī.
He kōrero whaitake nō nā tata nei i pā ai, kātahi anō rānei ka puta whānui.
He kōrero whakakino, whakaiti i tētahi atu.
He kōrero whakarite mō te wā, mō te whānau rānei e pōuri ana, e noho pani ana i te matenga o tētahi tangata; te wāhi e takoto ai te tūpāpaku.
He kōrero whakataki pātai e kimi ana nō tēhea wā i pā ai tētahi āhuatanga.
He kōrero, he aha atu e whakatūturu ana i te pono o tētahi whakapae.
He kōrero, he kī taurangi rānei kāore i whakatinanatia, kāore i whakatutukihia.
He kōrero, he mātauranga e pā ana ki tētahi kaupapa, ki tētahi āhuatanga kua pā, ka tukua, ka kitea rānei.
He kōrero, he pātai hei whakamātau, hei wero, i te hinengaro o te tangata ka riro māna e kimi te tikanga, te taunga o te kōrero, te whakautu tika rānei.
He kōrero, he tohutohu whakamutunga nā te tangata i mua i tōna matenga.
He kōrero, he tuhinga e whakaatu ana i ngā mahi i mahia, i pā rānei, i te āhua rānei o tētahi mea i tētahi wā kua hipa.
He kōrero, he whakaahua, he taputapu, he aha atu kua waihangatia, kua whakaemitia rānei hei āwhina, hei tautoko i te whāinga o te mātauranga.
He kōrua ka karia i te whenua hei takotoranga mō te tūpāpaku.
He kōtiro kāore anō i moe tāne.
He kōtiro kāore anō kia rere te awa o te atua, kāore anō kia taea e te tāne, e kiritapu tonu ana; he tangata kāore anō kia aitia.
He kōura e pīpī tonu ana.
He kōura nō nā noa nei i ngahoro ai te pāpapa.
He kōwhao i te pū whakatangitangi.
He kōwhaowhao ka rere iho i te kōanga, i te wā e pua ana te kōwhai.
He kōwhiuwhiu hei patu, hei papare rango i te tūpāpaku.
He kūmara iti.
He kūmara ka waruwarua, ka whakamaroketia ki te rā, ka tunua kia maoa, ka whakamaroke anō ai ki te rā.
He kūmara ka whakamahia i te tamaahu.
He kūmara kua pirau.
He kūmara kua waruwaruhia.
He kūmara penupenu.
He kūmara rahi, he pāpango te kiko.
He kūmara, he rīwai, ka mahue ki te whenua i muri i te hauhaketanga.
He maha ngā whakatakotoranga kei reira te kupu nei e piri tahi ana ki tētahi atu punga. Anei e whai ake nei ētahi: i muri i te tūāhua, i te tūmahi oti, e tohu ana i te tino eke o tētahi āhuatanga ki tētahi taumata.
He maha, he rahi hoki (o te kai).
He mahere huna, he tikanga huna.
He mahere ka whakaritea kia eke ai tētahi whāinga roa.
He mahi auroa ka āta whakaritea kia kawea e te tangata i tētahi whare mahi, i hea ake rānei, tērā e utua anō ai ia mō taua mahi.
He mahi e takahi ana i te tapu, i te tika, i te ture rānei.
He mahi ka kawea i roto i ngā pūtau o ngā mea ora e wāwāhia ai ngā huka, e puta ai he pūngao hei whakamahi mā te tinana.
He mahi ka mahia, he taonga he aha atu rānei ka tukua, e ea ai tētahi āhuatanga kino pērā i te patunga o te tangata kia mate.
He mahi ka āta whakatakotoria kia kitea ai te mātau, te mōhio o te tangata ki tētahi kaupapa, tōna pai rānei ki te mahi i tētahi mahi.
He mahi ngahau, he whakataetae te nuinga, kei te pai me te kaha o te kori o te tinana, kei te kakama anō pea o te hinengaro, te toanga.
He mahi ngahau, kei te kakama o te hinengaro, kei te waimarie, kei te kori anō pea o te tinana te toanga.
He mahi pūtaiao ka āta whāia hei kimi i te whakautu ki tētahi pātai pūtaiao, hei tautoko, hei turaki i tētahi whakapae, hei whakaū rānei i tētahi mea e mōhiotia ana kei te pono; ka mahi i tētahi mahi pēnei.
He mahi toi e honoa ai ētahi reo tangata, ētahi reo taonga whakatangitangi, e honoa ai ngā mea e rua rānei, ki te whakapuaki i tā te wairua, i tā te ngākau, i tā ngā kare ā-roto i hiahia whakaputa ai.
He mahi tuatahi, he mahi tōmua kia whakatikaina, kia whakapaipaitia ake ā tōna wā; tētahi o ngā āhua maha o tētahi mea i tāraia, i hangaia.
He mahi whakangahau, he mahi whakawehiwehi, he mahi whakaihiihi, e tū mai ai te tangata, tētahi kapa rānei ki te whakaputa i ō rātou whakaaro ki tētahi kaupapa. Ka haere ngā ringa, ka pūkana ngā karu, ka whātero te arero, ka horu te waha, ka takahi anō te waewae, ki te whakatinana i ngā kupu e whakapuakina rā.
He mahi, he kaupapa rānei e tūmanako ana te tangata, te rōpū rānei ka tutuki i a ia, mā roto tonu i āna whakapaunga kaha.
He maitai kōrahirahi, he koi tētahi pito, he pane kei tētahi, hei karatiti i te papanga, i te pepa, i te aha atu; tētahi atu hanga roa he karatiti tāna mahi.
He maka whakararo ka makā ki te rau o te taiaha mai i te popotahi.
He makatiti roa hei wāwāhi rākau.
He makawe hina ka tipu i te upoko o te tangata kāore anō i koroheketia, i kuiatia rānei.
He makawe kotahi, he huruhuru kotahi; he whenu angiangi kotahi nei, nō te tipu, nō te papanga rānei.
He makawe kua tārekoreko, kua pūmā.
He mamae e ngau kino ana.
He mamae i te puku.
He mamae ka pā ki te tinana.
He mana ka tukua e te ture ki te tangata nāna ake tētahi mahi, ki tētahi atu rānei kua tohua e ia, e motuhake mai ai ki a ia te tārua i tāna i hanga ai, i tito ai, i tuhi ai mō ētahi tau nei.
He mana ka tukua ki te tangata, ki te rōpū rānei, kia riro māna e whakatau, e whakahaere ētahi āhuatanga kua tohua.
He mana wairua whāioio tuauriuri nō te wāhi ngaro, kei reira te ora, kei reira te mate.
He manaakitanga, he painga ka tūpono te pā.
He manga rākau kua maroke, kua mate.
