He manu rahi noho pātītī taranui.
He manu rahi noho wairepo, noho awa, noho kōawa, noho waikeri, he tuarā pango tōna, he pukepoto ngā kaokao me te uma, he whero te rae, ngā ngutu me ngā wae, he mā te tou.
He manu rahi noho wairepo, noho awa, noho kōawa, noho waikeri.
He manu rere ahiahi noho ana, noho rua rākau rānei, kia tau ki te rākau ka iri iho ko te upoko ki raro, ko ngā maikuku o ngā waewae o muri kei te mau ki te peka.
He manu rere kore haere moana, he tāekaeka pango kei ngā huru kōwhai i te upoko, he tāhei kōwhai kei te murikōkai, he kōwhai ngā karu, he pukepoto a runga, he mā a raro.
He manu rere kore haere moana.
He manu rere kore noho tahatika, ki te taipū, te taha repo, te mōheuheu, te ngahere me ētahi atu wāhi, i te taha uru me te raki o Te Waipounamu, he parauri pango whai tāekaeka pākākā ngā huruhuru o runga, he kōkōwai a raro, he huruhuru kiwikiwi kei te korokoro, he tāhei whero kei te uma, he karu whero, he kōkōwai ngā waewae āhua roa tonu.
He manu rere pō e whā ngā parihau whānui, he parauri, he hātea rānei ngā tae o te nuinga, kia whakangā kua pāraharaha ngā parihau; arā tana whanaunga tata ko te pūrerehua mumura rere awatea.
He manu rerekore haere moana, he upoko pango, he pukepoto a runga, he mā a raro, he tāhei kōwhai e rere ana i runga ake i ngā karu.
He manu rerekore haere moana.
He manu rerekore noho ki te ākau, te taipū, te taha o te wairepo, te pātītī taranui, ki hea noa atu, he hāurauri, he parauri, he kahotea rānei ngā huruhuru, e kapi katoa ana aua huruhuru i te tāekaeka pango, he karu whero, he ura ngā ngutu me ngā waewae āhua roa tonu.
He manu rerekore noho ki te ākau, te taipū, te taha o te wairepo, te pātītī, ki hea noa atu.
He manu tai nui tonu ka kitea i ngā tahatika, i ngā awa me ngā roto, atu i tana upoko pango he manu mā, he ngutu whero nui tonu ōna.
He manu tai taumaha tonu, he hāurauri ngā huruhuru, he manauri ngā parirau, he tāhei mā kei ngā parirau, he pango ngā ngutu, ngā karu me ngā waewae.
He manu tai taumaha tonu.
He manu tai āhua nui tonu, he mā te nuinga atu o ngā huruhuru, he upoko kōwhai, he pango ngā hikutau, ka tiripou iho ki te wai ki te hopu ika māna.
He manu tai āhua nui tonu.
He manu tai, he kiwikiwi, he pango te upoko, te rae me te ua, kia whakaipoipo he pango katoa, he huru mā kei raro iho i ngā karu pango, he kiwikiwi te nuinga o ngā huruhuru, he mā ngā papa, he karaka ngā ngutu.
He manu tai, he mā a runga, he mā a raro, he pango te toi o ngā parirau kiwikiwi, he ngutu whero, he wae huirapa whero, he karu whero.
He manu tai, he mā te nuinga o ngā huruhuru atu i ngā mea pango i te tuarā me ngā parirau, he ngutu kōwhai, he wae kōwhai, he karu pango ōna.
He manu tai, he mā te upoko, te kakī, te hūmaeko me te puku, he kiwikiwi ngā pakihiwi me ētahi o huruhuru i ngā parirau, he huruhuru pango anō kei ngā parirau, he ngutu pango, he waewae pango, he pango anō ngā huirapa.
He manu tai, he mā, he māwhero ngā huruhuru, he huruhuru pango e rere ana i te pī o ngā ngutu ki muri o ngā karu, he karu parauri, he tino roa ngā hūmaeko whero.
He manu tai, he mā, he pango te rae, he pango te pito o ngā ngutu, kia whakaipoipo he kōwhai ngā ngutu, he mā katoa te rae, he kiwikiwi te tinana a runga, he mā a raro, he pango te tumuaki me te ua, he tāhei pango kei mua o ngā karu engari kāore e tae rawa ki ngā ngutu, he tokomanga te hūmaeko, he karaka ngā waewae.
He manu tai, he pango te tumuaki me te ua, he mā te rae, he kiwikiwi a runga, he mā a raro, he mā, he roa, he tokomanga te hūmaeko, he pango ngā karu, he pango ngā ngutu, he mā te pito, he pango, he karaka rānei ngā waewae.
He manu tai.
He manu taumaha tāwhai tai, he hāurauri te upoko me ngā parirau, he pakohe te uma, he kiwikiwi a raro me te tuarā, he ānau mā kei te karu, he kororā ngā waewae.
He manu taumaha tāwhai tai, he ngutu māwhero mātotoru, he kanohi mā, he parauri te tumuaki me te ua, he mā a raro, he tāingo kei te uma, he hāurauri ngā parirau, he ōrangitea ngā waewae.
He manu taumaha tāwhai tai.
He manu tino taumaha tāwhai tai, he ngutu māwhero mātotoru, he mā ngā huruhuru atu i ngā parirau pango parauri, he ōrangitea ngā waewae.
He manu tino taumaha tāwhai tai.
He manu tukutuku tapatoru te hanga, kia turua ki te rangi ko te tara kei runga, i mahia te anga ki te kākaho, ka uhia ki te raupō, he pua toetoe kotahi kei te tara, e toru ka tautau iho i te tapa whakararo, ko te aho ka herea ki te tohe kei waenganui o te anga.
He manu tukutuku tapawhā e kapi katoa ana i te whā raupō. Kāore ōna pākau engari he mea pūtoi ngā pito e rua ki te huruhuru manu.
He manu tāwhai tai, he kiwikiwi pango te tumuaki, he kiwikiwi parauri te kakī me ngā taha o te kakī, tae atu ki te tuarā, he hāurauri, he pakohe, he parauri pango ngā parirau, he mā te rae, te korokoro, te uma me te puku, he tāhei mā kei runga ake i ngā karu, he parauri pango a raro iho o ngā karu, he kiwikiwi ngā taha o te uma, he karu hāurauri, he ngutu pango, he waewae pango.
He manu tāwhai tai, he kororā a runga, he mā a raro, he ngutu kahurangi whānui tonu, he mā ngā tukemata, te kauae me te korokoro, he ōrangitea ngā waewae, he kahotea ngā huirapa.
He manu tāwhai tai, he kororā a runga, he mā a raro, he pango, he kahurangi ngā parirau, he poto ngā ngutu, he karu parauri, he waewae kahurangi, he kiwikiwi ngā huirapa.
He manu tāwhai tai, he kororā ngā huruhuru, he mā a raro i ngā parirau pango, e rite ana te whānui o ngā ngutu pakohe ki te whānui o te upoko, he ōrangitea ngā waewae, he kahotea ngā huirapa.
He manu tāwhai tai, he mā te korokoro, te uma me te puku, he kiwikiwi parauri te upoko, he pango, he parauri ngā parirau, he mā a raro iho, he karu parauri, he ngutu kiwikiwi, he pango a runga.
He manu tāwhai tai, he mā te rae me ngā tukemata, he kiwikiwi te tumuaki, te ua, me ngā pakihiwi, he pango parauri te hope, he pango ngā parirau, he mā a raro, he ngutu pango, he waewae kikorangi, he kōwhai ngā huirapa.
He manu tāwhai tai, he pango ngā huruhuru, he kiwikiwi te kauae me te korokoro, he karu parauri, he ngutu pango, he huirapa, he pango ngā waewae.
He manu tāwhai tai, he pango parauri ngā huruhuru o runga, he pango ngā parirau me ngā hūmaeko, he kiwikiwi a raro o ngā parirau, he karu parauri, he ngutu pakohe, he huirapa, he pakohe ngā waewae.
He manu tāwhai tai, he pango parauri, he kiwikiwi parauri a raro, he kiwikiwi a raro i ngā parirau, he karu hāurauri, he ngutu pakohe, he parauri pango, he poroporo ngā waewae, he poroporo anō ngā huirapa.
He manu tāwhai tai.
He manu wai māori kunekune te hanga.
He manu wai māori tetere te hanga, he pango te tumuaki me te ua, he hāurauri a runga, he mā a raro, he kōkōwai te korokoro me te uma, he karu kōwhai.
He manu wai māori, he huru pākā kōrito, he hāurauri te tumuaki me te ua, he kanohi kahotea whai tāwakawaka hāurauri, he korokoro kahotea, he karu kōkōwai, he pango te pito o ngā ngutu kiwikiwi, he kōwhai kākāriki ngā waewae huirapa.
He manu wai māori, he mā katoa ngā huruhuru, he pango te rae me ngā pāpāringa, he kōwhai ngā karu, he ngutu papa roa tōna, he pango ngā waewae.
He manu wai māori, he mā ngā huruhuru, he kōwhai ngā karu, he ngutu kōwhai roa tonu tōna, he pango ngā waewae.
He manu wai māori, wai tai, he manu nui tonu, he pango a runga, he mā a raro, he karu kahurangi.
He manu wai māori, wai tai, he manu āhua nui tonu, he pango ngā huruhuru me te pare, he kōwhai te pī o ngā ngutu, he mā ngā pāpāringa me te kauae.
He manu wai māori, wai tai, he manu āhua nui tonu.
He manu wai māori, wai tai, he pango ngā huruhuru o runga, he mā, he mā pango rānei ō raro, he kōwhai te kanohi me ngā ngutu, he pango ngā waewae.
He manu wai māori, wai tai, he pango ngā huruhuru, he kahurangi te korokoro, he kororā, he kahurangi ngā ngutu, he karu kākāriki.
He manu wai māori, wai tai.
He manu wai māori.
He manu wai pāpaku kōrahirahi nei, he pango a runga, he mā a raro, he tāhei pango kei te kakī, he ngutu pango roa ōna, he waewae whero tino roa.
He manu wai tai, he pango te upoko, te pare, te ua, te kakī me te tuarā, he parauri kiwikiwi ngā parirau, he tāwakawaka mā ka heke i te karu ki te kakī, he kanohi kākāriki, he wae karaka.
He manu wai tai, he pango te upoko, te pare, te ua, te kakī me te tuarā.
He manu āhua nui tonu noho maunga, he karera ngā huruhuru, he huru whero kei ngā kēkē me te tou.
He manu āhua nui tonu noho maunga.
He manu, he aha atu rānei ka hopukina e te tangata hei kai; whakamahia nuitia ai hei whakaahua i ēnei hanga ka kōtutua.
He manu, he ngārara, tētahi atu mea pēnei rānei kua mau i te tore kai huruhuru i mua i tana taua tuatahi.
He manu.
He manuhiri ka tangi tahi ki tētahi hunga kua murua.
He maramara iti o tētahi mea, he angiangi, he papatahi anō; he hukarere e pēnei ana te āhua.
He maramara iti wera ka puhaina mai i tētahi mea e kā ana, ka takoto mai rānei ina tata poko te ahi, ka puta ake rānei ina hikaia ētahi mea mārō e rua.
He maramara ka pakaru mai ina paopaohia he toka, whakamahia ai hei taputapu tapahi, hei hāro, hei tārai rānei i ētahi atu taputapu ki te toka.
He maramara kiri mate nō te kiri angaanga kei ngā makawe o te tangata.
He maramara maroke tino moroiti rawa atu (o te oneone, o te aha atu).
He maramara mōkitokito.
He maramara pātītī hei horoi i te tou o te tūpāpaku.
He maramara pēnei i te puehu ka tukuna e te wāhanga toa o te pua; ina hono ki te kano o te uwha, kua puta he kākano hou.
He maramara rākau hei puru i te kōwhao i te waka.
He maramara rākau ka kuhuna atu ki raro i ngā takā e here ana i te kiko o tētahi mea pērā i te toki ki tōna kakau.
He maramara rākau ka whakatakotoria ki te papa, kātahi ka hikaia atu ki tētahi atu maramara rākau koi kia puta ai he ahi.
He maramara rākau, he maramara waro rānei e kā tonu ana i te ahi.
He maro mō te kōhine, he pūtoi whītau noa.
He maro mō te wahine ka mahia ki te kuta.
He mata ka heke haere, ka piki haere rānei, i te mea ko tētahi pito he teitei ake i tētahi.
He mata kōata kua peitahia a muri ki tētahi hanga kia whakaaria tūturuhia te āhua o te mea kei mua i a ia.
He mata papatahi, he mata tautika.
He mata tokatoka tū poupou, tū tiketike mai.
He matakahi iti hei kuhu atu ki te rākau e wāwāhia ana.
He matakahi nui ka hangā ki te taikākā, ka titia atu i muri iho i te haenga o te rākau ki te pipi.
He matata hōhonu ka pakaru ake i ngā mea pēnei i te toka, i te papa whenua.
He matau hopu ika ka hangā ki te pāua, he matau kāore e mōunutia.
He matau rahi i mahia mai ki te rākau, he kāniwha wheua i te pito hei hī mangā.
He mate ai.
He mate e kakā ai, e mamae ai ngā pona, tae atu ki ngā uaua me ngā iohere.
He mate e kakā ai, e pupuhi ai te ate, e kirikā ai, e kiri kōwhai ai, e ngoikore anō ai te tangata, i te pokenga o te ate e te mahi a te huaketo.
He mate e kore ai e taea e te tinana te whakataki te rahi o te huka i ngā toto.
He mate e kukuti ai, e mamae ai ngā uaua o tētahi wāhanga o te tinana.
He mate e mamae ai, e papī ai, e mangeo ai rānei te kiri.
He mate e māuiui ai te tangata, e mangeo ai rānei tana kiri ina kai, ina rongo, ina whakapā atu rānei ia ki tētahi mea e pai noa iho ana ki te nuinga.
He mate e māuiui ai te tangata, e mangeo ai rānei tana kiri ina kai, ina rongo, ina whakapā atu rānei ki tētahi mea.
He mate e tohua ana e te ngau kino o te puku, he kakā, he pupuhi rānei nō te kōpiro, he mau rānei nō te hau ki reira.
He mate hā e tohungia ana e te ngāngā, tērā tonu ko te mate pāwera tōna pūtakenga mai.
He mate ka ahu mai i te mākutu, i te whakaaro kino, i te takahi i te tapu.
He mate ka rere ki te mātinitini.
He mate ka rere ki te tangata, ki te aha atu ina pā atu, ina pātata atu rānei ia ki tētahi e pāngia ana e taua mate.
He mate ka rere, ka horapa ki te mātinitini i tētahi wā motuhake, me te hemo anō o te tokomaha i taua mate.
He mate kino e kakā ai ngā kiriuhi o te ua me te roro i te pokenga e tētahi momo huakita, e tētahi momo huaketo rānei.
He mate kino e kakā ai ngā pūkahukahu, e uaua ai te whakahā, ko te huaketo, te huakita, tētahi matū rānei te takenga mai.
He mate kino e rea ai ētahi pūtau kino i te tinana, e tipu ai he puku.
He mate kōpiro e kaha ai, e tino waiwai ai te tiko.
He mate nakunaku kai e pāwera katoa ai te pūkai me te uma i te waikawa e pupū ake ana i te puku.
He mate ohorere e hē ai te mahi a te manawa i te mea kua puru tētahi o ngā iaia kawe toto ki a ia.
He mate rere e puta ai he harehare ki ngā ū o te kau. Ka rere anō te mate nei ki te tangata, he āhua rite ki te koroputaputa, engari kāore i pērā rawa te kino.
He mate rere e āhua kirikā ai te tamariki (me te pakeke anō i ētahi wā), e harehare ai te kiri, me te tino mangeo anō.
He mate rere he huaketo te takenga mai, e pupuhi ai, e mamae ai ngā repe hūare, e kirikā anō ai te tinana. Ka pāngia nuitia ko te tamariki.
He mate rere he huaketo te takenga mai, ka kirikā te tinana, ka ānini te māhunga, ka mamae ngā uaua, ka hūpē te ihu, me te wharowharo anō.
He mate rere ka hua ake i te urutomo mai a tētahi momo huakita i te tinana, mā roto i tētahi tūnga, e kikī ai, e hukihuki ai ngā uaua.
He mate rere ka nui te pā ki te tamariki, ko tōna tohu ko te maremare tonu me te tekekō anō ina whakahā.
He mate rere ka pā ki te ihu me te korokoro, ko te mātihetihe, te rere kino o te hūpē me te maremare ētahi o ōna tino tohu.
He mate rere ka pā ki te kiri, ki te kiriwai o ngā ara whakaroto o te tinana, ki ngā ioio, me ētahi atu wāhi o te tinana e poapoa ai, e pukupuku ai te kiri, ā, tērā anō pea ka mate rawa, ka riro rawa ngā matimati.
He mate rere kino e kirikā ai te tangata, e pakaru mai ai he harehare pirau. Kia makere ngā pāpaka tērā kua noho he nawe ki te kiri.
He mate rere kino e tipu ai he kōpuku ki ngā pūkahukahu, i ōna wā anō ka toro ki ngā kōiwi, ki ngā tākihi me ētahi atu wāhi o te tinana. Tērā ka mate rawa te tangata i te mate nei, ki te kore e rongoātia.
He mate rere kino ka hua ake i te huaketo ko tāna mahi, he patu i ngā pūtau mā o te toto, e kore ai e taea e te tinana te mate te kaupare atu.
He mate rere āhua kino tonu e kirikā ai, e maremare ai te tangata, e mamae ai ngā karu, e kapi ai te kiri i te tiwha whero. I ētahi wā koia te mātārere o ētahi atu mate kino. Ka kotahi wiki neke atu e ngau ana te mate nei, ā, ka pāria nuitia ko te hunga tamariki.
He mate rere āhua rite ki te karawaka, e kirikā ai te tangata, e mamae ai te korokoro, e puta ai he tiwha whero ki te kiri. Tērā pea ka tino hē te hanga o te pēpē ka whānau mai ki te wahine i pāria e te mate nei i a ia e hapū ana.
He matū e hāpiripiri ana, e hāpiapia ana.
He matū ka ahu mai i te tipu, i te kararehe. Ka kitea nuitia i raro tonu iho i te kiri o te kararehe, e kōpaki ana hoki i ētahi whēkau pērā i te tākihi. Ka whakamahia nuitia hei tunu kai, hei kīnaki, hei pani, hei kakara rānei.
He matū ka whakahihiko, ka whakarehurehu rānei i tā te hinengaro, i tā te tinana i rongo ai, tērā anō ka whakakotiti anō i ngā whakaaro ina kainga.
He matū ka whāngaia ki te tinana hei pare atu i te mate.
He matū kei ngā pūtau rauropi e mau ana i ngā āhuatanga tuku iho.
He matū kāore e whakaaetia ana e te ture, ka whakahihiko, ka whakarehurehu rānei i tā te hinengaro, i tā te tinana i rongo ai, tērā anō ka whakakotiti anō i ngā whakaaro ina kainga.
He matū matatini te hanga, koia tētahi wāhanga taketake o ngā mea ora katoa.
He matū nō roto i te whenua, ko te nuinga he mārō, he kānapanapa, ka taea anō te paopao kia rerekē te hanga, te kukume kia oti mai ai he waea angiangi, te whakawera me te tūhono tētahi ki tētahi, he pai anō hei kawe i te mahana, i te hiko.
He matū rehu āhua rite ki te hau takiwā ka makoha noa ki te whakakī i tētahi wāhi wātea.
He matū whakaputa i tētahi aho ngoikore ehara ko te ngingihatanga, ko te wera rānei te pūtake. Ka tino kitea ina pōuri ana.
He matū whero ka ngohe ina wera, ka tere mārō anō ina mātao. I ngā rā o mua i kaha te whakapiria ki te reta, ki te tuhinga kua kōpakina, kua pōkaitia rānei kia noho kati tonu, ā tae rawa ki te tangata māna.
He mau mō te taiaha.
He mau taiaha hei karo i te wiri waewae.
He maungārongo mau tonu.
He mauri hei whakaū i te pai, i te ora o te whare, hei taunga hoki mō te ora, mō ngā mea nōna te whare.
He mauti pā te tupu, 1.5 mita te roa o ngā rau, he whānui tonu ngā rau kōwhai kākāriki, he poto, he makiki ngā tātā kawe i ngā hua mōhinuhinu pango, ka motumotu te kiri i ngā rau o tēnei tipu.
He mauti pā te tupu, 1.5 mita te roa o ngā rau.
He mea e kaha hiahiatia ana, e kaha wawatatia ana e te ngākau.
He mea e kaingākautia ana, he nui rānei te utu, kāore rānei e tino kitea.
He mea e noho mai ana, i tāia rānei ki tētahi mata, e whakaatu ana i tētahi āhuatanga.
He mea e takoto mai ana ki te pae, mai i tētahi taha ki tētahi taha o te tirohanga kanohi.
He mea e teatea ana, e hāmā ana te tae.
He mea e tino kaha ana, e ranea ana te tupu, te hua mai rānei i tētahi wāhi.
He mea e tōtika ana anō kia wātea mai ki a koe, kia āhei rānei koe ki te mahi.
He mea e wehingia ana, nō te ao wairua tōna kaha.
He mea e whakaatu ana pēhea te hanga o tētahi mea, me pēhea rānei te whakamahi i tētahi mea.
He mea e whakaparahakotia ana.
He mea hei hari i te tangata, i tētahi atu mea rānei ki tētahi atu wāhi.
He mea hei puru i ngā kōhao o te waka.
He mea hei whakamaunga atu mā ngā karu, mā te hinengaro, e whakaata ana, e whakatinana ana i tētahi atu hanga, tērā tonu pea he hanga kāore e kitea e te karu.
He mea iti, he wāhanga iti rānei o tētahi mea.
He mea ka hoatu noa e te tangata ki tētahi atu, i runga i tana aroha, i tana whakaaro nui ki a ia.
He mea ka kitea e te karu, ka rangona rānei e te taringa, e waitohu ana i tētahi āhuatanga ka pā, kua pā rānei.

He mātaitai whai kokopi poroāwhio te hanga, neke atu i te 4 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua o tai takoto haere ake, he anga mā, he hāuratea rānei, he pāhiwihiwi tarapī kōpae te hanga kei te anga.
He mātaitai whai kokopi poroāwhio te hanga, paku neke atu i te 4 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua tata mai o tai takoto, he anga rarai mā whai ngutu pūngarungaru tōna.
He mātaitai whai kokopi poroāwhio te hanga.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, 12 henemita te tupu, he piri toka ki taihua, he pukepoto a waho, he pango, he mā rānei a roto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, e 20 henemita te tupu, he piri toka ki tai takoto haere ake, he anga kānapanapa, he ngutu kākāriki.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, e 3 henemita te tupu, he piri toka i ngā paringa a tai aronui, he anga kōratarata, he pango, he pukepoto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, e 30 henemita te tupu, he noho paru ki tai takoto haere ake, he parauri a waho, he pāua a roto, e kapi ana te anga i te tara hākaro.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, e 4 henemita te tupu, he tini te piri toka ki taihua, he anga kōwhai, he ōriwa rānei, e 6 ngā rara kei tētahi pito, 14 kei tētahi, he māwhero a roto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, e 5 henemita te tupu, he mātaitai ore toka ki taihua, he hāurauri a waho, he kahurangi, he waiporoporo a roto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, e 5 henemita te tupu, he piri toka ki tai takoto haere ake, he kiri kōkōwai kei te anga kahotea, he huruhuru kei te pito whānui.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, e 7 henemita te tupu, he piri toka ki tai takoto haere ake, e kapi katoa ana te anga parauri i te tāwakawaka me te huru parauri.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga, e 9 henemita te tupu, he piri toka ki tai takoto, he waiporoporo pango a waho, he hiriwa, he waiporoporo rānei a roto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi rapa te hanga.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, 11 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua o tai takoto, he kiri kōwhai kei te anga kahotea, he kōtingotingo, he tāekaeka kōkōwai ngā whakapaipai o te anga.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, 15 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki waenganui taihua, he kiri kahotea kei te anga mā, tērā kua ura, kua kiwikiwi rānei te anga i te oneone, kei te pito pūhuki te kokopi.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 4 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua tata mai o tai takoto, he anga mā, he papatahi tētahi taha, he tiriwhana tētahi, kei waenganui tonu te kokopi.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 5 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua tata mai o tai takoto, he anga mōhinuhinu, he kōwhai, he waiporoporo a roto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 6 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua tata mai o tai takoto, he tāheke waiporoporo kei te anga mā, he waiporoporo a roto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 6 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua tata mai o tai takoto, he tāheke waiporoporo kei te anga māwhero, he waiporoporo a roto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 6 henimita te tupu, he noho oneone ki waenga taihua, he kiri kōwhai kei te anga mā tērā kua ura, kua pango rānei i te oneone, kei waenganui o te anga te kokopi.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 7 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua tata mai o tai takoto, he anga taumaha, he kahotea, he kiri hāuratea kei te anga.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 7 henemita te tupu, he noho paru ki waenga taihua, he anga mā tērā pea kua pārikoriko i te paru, he mā, he kōwhai rānei a roto.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 8 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua tata mai o tai takoto, he kiri kōwhai kei te anga mā, kei te pito pūhuki te kokopi.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 8 henemita te tupu, he noho paru ki te tāhuna, ki te wahapū, he anga kōwhai tērā pea kua pārikoriko i te paru.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga, e 9 henemita te tupu, he noho oneone ki tua tata mai o tai takoto, he kiri hāuratea kei te anga mā.
He mātaitai whai kokopi tapatoru te hanga.
He mātaitai whai kokopi, tipirori te hanga, e 8 henemita te tupu, he piri toka ki tua tata mai o tai aronui, he hōhonu te taha whakararo o te anga, he papatahi a runga, he anga pūngarungaru tae atu ki ngā tapa.
He mātaitai whai kokopi, tipirori te hanga.
He mātaitai wiri te hanga, e 3 henemita te tupu, he noho one ki tua o tai takoto, he tāwakawaka e heke ana i ngā wehenga o te anga mā.
He mātaitai wiri te hanga, e 3 henemita te tupu, he noho paru ki taikoraha, he tāwakawaka e heke ana i ngā wehenga o te anga parauri.
He mātaitai wiri te hanga, e 3.5 henemita te tupu, he noho one ki tua o tai takoto, he pakini kei te pī whakarunga o te waha, he anga māwhero.
He mātaitai wiri te hanga, e 5 henemita te tupu, he noho kōpūpūtai ki tai hōhonu, he haenga e rere ana i tētahi taha o te anga.
He mātaitai wiri te hanga, e 8.5 henemita te tupu, he noho awa ki tua o tai takoto, he whakaawa tarapī parauri e kōmiro ana i te anga waiporoporo parauri.
He mātauranga e pā ana ki ngā āhuatanga me ngā whakawhitiwhiti o ngā matū me te pūngao, pērā i te hiko, te mārama, te oro me te neke.
He mātauranga hira, he tino whai mana.
He mātauranga pāngarau matua e aro ana ki te tūnga, te rahi me te hanga o ngā āhua i roto i te mokowā.
He mātauranga, he mōhiotanga e noho māori mai ana ki te tangata, e tere mau ai i a ia tētahi mahi, e tino tau ai ia ki taua mahi.
He mōmona, he hanga rānei e rite ana ki te mōmona e tino reka ai te kai, te kōrero rānei.
He mōunu ka tukua ki roto i te wai kia hui mai ai ngā ika.
He mōunu mō te hopu kōura.
He mōunu mō te hopu ngōiro, arā he ika kua raua atu ki tētahi takotoranga kua hangā ki te harakeke.
He mōunu mō te ika.
He nehu kōkōwai (i whakamahia hei pani).
He nehu pahū ka purua ki ngā kariri o te pū i raro i te matā, hei te pahūtanga ka panaia te matā ki waho.
He ngahere e tino mātotoru ana te tipu o te rākau.
He ngahuru e nui ai te huawhenua me te huarākau.
He ngaku harakeke kāore e hāroa, kāore e tāwaia, whakamahia ai hei whakarākei i ngā kahu kōkau; he kahu ka mahia pēneitia.
He ngaku papanga ka rawea atu ki tētahi wāhanga o te tinana kua whara.
He ngaro, ko ia te whakatinanatanga o te wairua o te tangata e mākuturia ana.
He ngaru iti e tāwakawaka ana i te mata o te wai.
He ngaru iti, he karekare ka puta ake ina pā te hoe ki te wai.
He ngaru iti, he karetai rānei.
He ngaru tino nui ka hua ake i te rū. (He mea whakatangata, ā, ka kaha te whai mai o te kupu 'mea'.)
He ngaru tino nui.
He ngaruetanga whenua ka ohorere te puta ake i te nekehanga o te kirinuku.
He ngira pakupaku ka mahia ki te kōiwi, he kōwhao kei tētahi pito.
He ngira tā moko i mahia ki te wheua o te turiwhati.
He ngongo ka takoto hei rerenga mō te wai, te haurehu, te parakaingaki, te aha atu.
He ngākau māia ki te whawhai.
He ngāngara, arā he pepeke noho rākau pirau, ki raro kiri rākau rānei, he tinana pāraharaha tōna, he pango, he pīataata, kāore ōna parirau, kia whakaohongia kua tukua tana haunga tino kino.
He ngāngara, arā he pepeke noho rākau pirau, ki raro kiri rākau rānei.
He ngāngara, arā, he angawaho kaikiko ka kitea i raro i te kiri o te rākau pirau, i raro i te kōhatu, he roroa he pāraharaha te tinana, he maha ngā wāhanga o te tinana, he taurua te noho mai o ngā waewae ki ia wāhanga.
He ngārara ka kitea i ngā whenua mahana, ngā whenua maroke, he kuku kei tana hiku roa hei timo, hei tuku i tana paihana.
He ngārara noho rua, he kiwikiwi, he unahinahi te kiri, he rārangi tarakina kei te tuarā, kāore ōna taringa, e toru ana karu, ko te mea tuatoru kei waenga o te rae, kei raro  unahi e huna ana.
He ngārara noho rua.
He ngārara tinana mohe tino pōturi te haere ka kitea i te māra, i hea atu, ka taea e ia te whakahoki i te katoa ōna ki tana anga tōrino.
He ngārara tino nui kua korehāhā, nō rātou tēnei ao ka hia miriona tau ki mua.
He ngārara tōpuku te tinana, e waru ngā waewae, he hanga māwhaiwhai te nuinga hei hopu kai mā rātou.
He ngārara whakararu i te tangata, he takakino i te kai, i te tupu o te kai, he tuku tahumaero rānei.
He niho e inaki ana i tētahi atu.
He niho hou.
He niho kauoro kei te wāhanga whakamuri o te waha; e ono kei te kauwae runga, e ono anō kei te kauwae raro o te waha pakeke.
He niho koikoi kei te noho tuatoru mai i te rārangi waenga o te pae niho; e rua kei te kauae runga, e rua anō kei te kauwae raro.
He niho kua pirau, te mamae ina pirau te niho.
He niho nui nō te ika moana, nō te poaka, nō te arewhana.
He niho ripi e noho ana ki te wāhi whakamua o te pae niho; e whā kei te kauae runga, e whā anō kei te kauae raro.
He niho tara rua kei muri tonu mai i ngā niho kata i te waha pakeke; e whā kei te kauae runga, e whā anō kei te kauae raro.
He niho tuatahi ka panaia e te niho pakeke ā tōna wā.
He nohoanga i te kei o te waka hei nohoanga mō te tangata whai mana.
He nohoanga āhua roa, he ngohengohe ki te noho i runga, he papa mō te tuarā kei muri, i te nuinga he taunga hoki mō ngā ringa kei ngā taha.
He oko e purua atu ai he kōhatu tino wera hei kōhua i te kai.
He oko ka mahia ki te kiri tōtara hei takotoranga mō te huahua, mō te hinu, mō te aha atu.
He oko ka mahia ki te kiri tōtara hei takotoranga mō te huahua.
He oko ka tapahia mai i te angaanga, i te hue rānei.
He oko paku whai kakau hei inu mā te tangata.
He oko pāpaku ka tapahia mai i te hue.
He oneone haumako, he matarehu te āhua, he paru, he parakiwai me te onepū kua ranua katoatia, he waihotanga iho nā te wai rere, pērā i te awa, me te waipuke.
He oneone i tahuna kia whero, ka konatua ki te hinu hei pani.
He oneone ka ahuahua e te tohunga mō te karakia tira ora. Ko tāna i tohu ai ko te ora, ko te oranga wairua, ko te oranga hinengaro.
He oneone kua pango, kua mōmona, kua pai te pupuri wai, i te nui o te hanga māori o roto kua popo, kua hanehane.
He oneone mākū kua hāpiapia katoa, ki te hōhonu ka tāpokopoko, ka kitea i te whenua ina mutu te ua, i te taikoraha, i te repo, me ērā momo wāhi.
He oneone ngahoro, arā, he onepū, he uku, me te paraumu kua ranua katoatia, engari he nui atu te onepū i te uku me te paraumu.
He oneone ngahoro, he haumako, he onepū, he uku, me te paraumu kua ranua katoatia; e āhua rite ana te nui o te onepū me te paraumu, he iti iho te uku.
He oneone pāpango i te nui o te paraumu, he mōmona.
He oneone whai kirikiri.
He oneone āhua pungapunga nei te āhua, kāore e tino mōmona.
He ope iti ka haere huna, he muru te mahi.
He ope iti ka rere ki mua o te ope matua.
He ope ka haere ki te ngaki i te mate o tētahi kua kōhurutia.
He ope ka haere puku kia kite i te kaha o te hoariri, i te takoto rānei o te whenua.
He ope ka huihui mai ki te kāhaki i tētahi wahine, ki te whakahē rānei i te moenga o tētahi tokorua.
He ope ka whati mai i te taua matua, ka haere ki te tango, ki te tāhae i ngā rawa a te hoariri.
He ope manuhiri.
He ope tango rawa, whānako rawa.
He ope taua ka haere ki te whawhai.
He ope taua ka huna, ka puta ohorere ki te patu i te hoariri.
He ope taua ka pāhoro i te pā.
He ope taua ka whakaeke i te hoariri i a rātou e haere ana i te huarahi.
He ope taua ka whakatūtūngia i runga i te whāwhai i muri tonu mai o tētahi matenga, kia haere tonu iho ki te ngaki i taua matenga.
He ope taua ka āta whakatūtūngia kia haere ki te ngaki i te mate o tētahi.
He ope toa taua, he tau ki te whawhai.
He ope wairua ko te karahiwi, ko te tihi maunga rānei tōna kāinga, he kiritea, he urukehu, he iwi tino tapu. Kia tau mai te kohu, ka rangona e kōrerorero ana, e waiata ana, e whakatangi kōauau ana, e aha ana, ka mutu ki te tūpono atu te tangata ki tōna kāinga, kua rere ki wāhi kē noho ai.
He oro e rite ana ki tētahi mea e wakua ana e tētahi atu mea.
He oro hoihoi.
He oro i tētahi reo ka puta ake i te noho tahi mai o ētahi oropuare e rua.
He oro i tētahi reo, kia whakahuatia, ka katia, ka āhua katia rānei te rere o te hā.
He oro i tētahi reo, kia whakahuatia, ka āhua puare tonu te waha, e rere noa ai te hā.
He oro ka pakō ake, ka tino rangona.
He oro tino kaha, me te mea nei kua pahū tētahi mea, ko te oro tonu rānei ka puta ina pahū tētahi mea.
He oro tīkākā ka rangona ina pūhia te hau ki ngā ngutu, ki tētahi taputapu, ki tētahi puarenga iti rānei.
He otaota kua popo haere, kua noho mai hei whakapaparanga i ngā whenua kōreporepo.
He otaota moroiti, he kōwhai ngā putiputi, ka taea te kai i ngā rau me te tāmore anō hoki.
He otaota tipu noa i waenga pārae, he pāraharaha te tipu o ngā rau, he pua kōwhai tini ōna raupua ka tupu mai i te pū o te tipu, he pia mā kawa ka papī mai ina katohia te tipu nei; he pai ngā wāhanga katoa hei kai.
He otaota tipu noa i waenga pārae.
He otaota tupu ki waenga pārae, he ngita kei ōna wāhi katoa, he pūwhero, he porotea ngā puāwai, he kākano rere ōna.
He otaota tupu ki waenga pārae.
He pae i te waka tere moana hei nōhanga mō te tangata.
He pae kākā, he mutu kākā hoki.
He pae manu whai karu māhanga hei hopu kererū.
He pae manu whai māhanga (mō te hopu manu).
He pae maunga whakapae te tū mai.
He paepae āhua whāiti, he roa tonu, hei pupuri i te wai, i te taonga, i te tūpāpaku, i te aha atu.
He paepae, he pouaka rānei hei pupuri taonga, aha atu rānei.
He pakanga e matemate ai ētahi tāngata o ngā taha e rua.
He pakihi mahi moni mā roto i ngā mahi tauhokohoko.
He pakikau kei te tuarā o te ika.
He pakitaha e hohoko ai te rere o ngā tapawhā rerekē nei te tae.
He pakitaha kei te taha o te kahu.
He pakitaha whakapaipai (o te kahu).
He pakuriki maha e rite ana ki te puehu te āhua.
He panekoti whānui ka mahia ki tētahi papanga mārōrō tonu.
He pani kikorangi ka mahia ki te uku.
He pani mō te kiri hei ārai atu i ngā hihi katikati o te rā.
He pani mō te parāoa, ka mahia ki te huarākau, ki te huawhenua rānei.
He paoa tino mātotoru, he pango.
He papa e toro ake ana i te pito whakarunga o ngā tūwatawata o te pā hei tūnga mō te iwi ki te kurukuru i ngā upoko o te hoariri ki te aha noa iho.
He papa e toro whakawaho ana mai i te pakitara o te whare, he tuanui whakamarumaru tōna.
He papa e tūhono ana i ngā taha o te waka, e oti mai ai te ihu o te waka.
He papa ka hangaia kia toro atu ki te wai, hei taunga mō te poti, mō te kaipuke ina utaina, ina tangohia rānei ngā utanga.
He papa ka kaurori, ka tōia rānei hei whakakapi, hei whakatuwhera hoki i te whatitoka, he hanga pērā rānei kei tētahi atu mea pērā i te motukā.
He papa ka tōia, ka kaurori rānei hei whakakapi i te whatitoka, i te matapihi rānei.
He papa ka whakamaua ki te niao o te waka kia kore ai te wai e uru ki roto.
He papa motuhake kei waho hei kori, hei tākaro mā te tamariki, tērā anō he rawa kei reira pērā i te tārere, i te reti, i te aha atu.
He papa motuhake kei waho, kei rō whare rānei e tākarohia ai tētahi hākinakina.
He papa māmā ka whakamahia hei tipi i te papa mania, i te mata rōnaki rānei.
He papa mātotoru kei te taha whakararo o te whatitoka, ka takahia e te waewae i te kuhunga atu ki rō whare.
He papa pāpango, he papa mā rānei e mau ana ki te pakitara, e tū ana rānei ki ētahi waewae, hei tuhituhi mā te tangata.
He papa rākau ka whakamahia i ngā karakia matakite.
He papa rākau kei muri i te pakoko o te ihuwaka e whakamaua ai ngā pito o ngā rauawa.
He papa rākau, he maitai rānei ka takoto huapae mai ki te whakakaha, ki te whakamārō i tētahi hanga, hei whakamaunga atu rānei mō tētahi atu mea.
He papa whekī ka koropaepaetia ki te rua kūmara.
He papa whānui ka whakatūria kia rere whakapae i mua i te whare, e kōpani ana i te mahau.
He papa, he aha atu ka tūtū mai i waenganui i ngā pou matua o te taiapa.
He papanga haurehu e kōpaki ana i a Papatūānuku me ērā atu aorangi.
He papanga hei muku atu i te para, i te paru, i te puehu, i te aha atu e piri ana ki tētahi mata.
He papanga ka purua ki te weu, ki te huru manu rānei, hei whakamahana i te tangata i a ia e moe ana.
He papanga ka takaia ki te hope, ki waenganui hoki i ngā waewae o te pēpi, hei pupuri i te mimi me te tiko.
He papanga ka whakaarahia ake ki te tokotū o te waka ki te hopu i te hau, e tere ai te waka.
He papanga ka whakairia ki te matapihi, ki hea ake rānei hei rīanga, ka kūmea ake ki ngā taha, ka hūtia ake rānei ki runga.
He papanga kua tāia ki ōna anō tohu hei waitohu i te whenua, i te iwi, i te aha atu. Ko te nuinga ka hūtia ake ki te pou.
He papanga kāore e tuku mai i te wai, he papanga pītongatonga.
He papanga mātotoru hei whakamaroke i te tinana.
He papanga mātotoru ka horahia ki te papa.
He papanga mātotoru, he āhua ngohe anō, ka noho ki waenganui i te tuara me te wahanga, kia kore ai te tuarā e mamae, e pahore.
He papanga nui, he mātotoru hei hora ki te moenga, ki hea atu rānei.
He papanga roa, he whāiti ka noho mai ki raro i te kara o te hāte, ka taponahia ki te korokoro me te waiho i ngā pito kia tautau ki te poho.
He papanga tapawhā nui tonu, he angiangi. Ina horahia te moenga, e rua ka horaina atu, ka whai atu ko ngā paraikete, ko te papangarua rānei.
He papanga whāiti, he rau rākau, he aha atu ka mahia kia tarawhiti te hanga, ka whakamaua ki te upoko hei whakapaipai, hei tohu i te mate, i te aha atu.
He papanga whāiti, he roa, hei whakapaipai i tētahi mea.
He para kōhatu tino ririki e hora ana i te takutai, i te awa me ētahi atu wāhi.
He para ngāwhā kōwhai, he haunga anō. (Tohu pūtaiao: S)
He para uku, he para onepū, he para oneone ka kawea e te waipuke, ka mahue ki te whenua ina heke te waipuke.
He pare mō te rae ka mahia ki te huruhuru manu.
He pare rau rākau mō te upoko ka whakamaua ina tangihia tētahi mate.
He parehua toka mākini kei runga paku atu, kei raro paku atu rānei i te kārewa o te moana e takoto mai ana.
He parepare i hangā ki runga i te pūhara o te pā, hei tiaki i ngā tāngata o runga, arā, hei kaupare atu i ngā rākau a te hunga e whakaeke ana i te pā.
He pareparenga ka mahia ki te raima, ki te oneone, ka hangaia i te whānuitanga o tētahi awa, hei pupuri i ngā wai.
He paru manauri, he takotoranga whakapango mō ētahi mahi o te whare pora.
He paru tāpokopoko, he para waikura kei roto.
He paru tāpokopoko.
He paru, he kongakonga i roto i te wai ehu kua tau iho ki te takere.
He parāoa angiangi ka pania ki te kīnaki tōmato, ka ruiruia ki te tīhi, ki te huawhenua, ki te mīti, ki te aha atu, kātahi ka tunua ki te umu wera.
He pata wai moroiti i te hau takiwā, ka takoto hei pata wai ririki ki te whenua me ētahi atu mata mātao o waho i ngā pō.
He pata wai tino moroiti kei te hau takiwā, kei te mata o tētahi mea, kei roto rānei i tētahi hanga papatipu.
He patu i mahia ki te ōnewa.
He patu ka mahia ki te kōhatu.
He patu ki te taiaha.
He patu tākaro pororapa te hanga hei patu pōro, he aho e rere mārō ana mai i runga ki raro, mai i tētahi taha ki tētahi.
He pauku, he mariao i te korokoro.
He peita whero.
He peka mātauranga pūtaiao whānui e tirohia ai ngā mea ora katoa, tae atu ki tō rātou pūtakenga mai, te tupu, te whakaputa uri, te hanga, me ētahi atu āhuatanga.
He peka ririki, he kōrahirahi, ka tipu mai i ngā peka matua o te rākau.
He pekenga, he rerenga whakamua rānei.
He pepa e whakaatu ana i ngā rawa i hokona, i ngā mahi rānei i mahia, me te utu e tika ana kia utua e te kaihoko mō aua mea.
He pepa he tuhituhi, he pātai rānei e pā ana ki tētahi kaupapa kei runga, he wāhi anō e wātea ana hei whakauru kōrero atu mā te kaipānui.
He pepa, he aha atu rānei hei muku i te tou ina mutu te mimi me te tiko.
He pepa, he hanga maitai iti kua tāia ki ōna anō tohu whaimana, koia e whakamahia ana hei hoko, hei utu i te taonga, i te mahi, i te aha atu rānei.
He pepa, he kāri e tukuna ai te kaipupuri kia uru ki tētahi wāhi, ki tētahi tauwhāinga, kia haere rānei mā runga pahi, mā runga tereina, mā runga waka rererangi.
He pepeke 10 mirimita te roa, kei raro kōhatu i te takutai tana kāinga, he pango, he pīataata te tinana, he kuku kei te tou, kāore ōna parihau.
He pepeke e 20 mirimita te tupu.
He pepeke e 5 mirimita te roa, e rua ōna parihau, he roa ngā waewae, he ngongo toto te uha, ka rangona tōna tangi tīkākā ina tata mai ki te kanohi, ko te wai whakaroau te kāinga o ana punua.
He pepeke e 5 mirimita te roa.
He pepeke kai rau mānuka, he kākāriki te tinana o te nuinga engari arā ētahi he kahurangi, he karaka, he whero, he waiporoporo rānei. I pehua tahitia te pepeke nei me te kōnehu raupō i mua, hei kai.
He pepeke kai rau mānuka.
He pepeke karu putē tapatoru te hanga o te upoko, he kākāriki te tinana hauroa, he ōpure kahurangi, waiporoporo rānei kei ngā waewae o mua, he papatahi te noho mai o ngā parirau i te tuarā, ka whakakopa ngā waewae o mua, me te mea nei e inoi ana.
He pepeke karu pūtenetene tapatoru te hanga o te upoko.
He pepeke kōrahirahi he roa te tinana, he poto te tārāuma, he kōataata ngā parihau e whā, he kikorangi, he pango te tinana o ngā toa, he kākāriki ake te uwha.
He pepeke kōrahirahi he roa te tinana, he poto te tārāuma, he kōataata ngā parihau e whā, he whero, he pango te tinana o ngā toa, he karaka parauri te uwha.
He pepeke kōrahirahi he roa te tinana.
He pepeke manomano te rere i te pō, kei ngā wāhi marumaru, ngā wāhi haukū tana kāinga, he hīnātore kei te tou o te uwha hei whakawai i ngā toa.
He pepeke moroiti e 2 mirimita te roa, e rua ōna parirau, he parauri ki te pango te tae, he ngongo toto ngā uha, he piri toka, he piri tipu ngā hua me ngā punua i te wai rere.
He pepeke moroiti e 2 mirimita te roa.
He pepeke moroiti kai toto, he kaha ki te peke, he parauri, he pango te tae, he mārō te tinana tāpapa.
He pepeke noho ana, noho ngahere, noho wahie i Tāmaki ki te uru, kāore ōna parirau, he tāhei kahotea e huri ana i te tinana manauri, inā te roa o ngā pūhihi me ngā waewae taratara, he taratara kei te tou o te uwha mō te whānau hua.
He pepeke noho pātītī, he tino roa ngā waewae o muri, he pākā, he kiwikiwi, he kākāriki rānei te tae, arā, kei te āhua tonu o tana taiao tōna tae.
He pepeke noho pātītī.
He pepeke noho rākau, noho raro peha rākau rānei, he mōhinuhinu, he pāraharaha te tinana, he tino roa ngā weri, ehara i te pepeke orotā.
He pepeke noho rākau, noho wahie, he tino nui te upoko kōkōwai me te kauae o ngā toa, he kōwhai, he parauri ngā tāhei e huri ana i te tinana, he roa ake ngā pūhihi i te tinana, he nunui ngā tara kei ngā waewae o muri, he tara kei te tou o ngā uwha mō te whānau hua.
He pepeke noho rākau, noho wahie.
He pepeke pango kitā i te pō, he taratara, he roa ngā waewae o muri, he poto he taratara ō mua, he pepeke rere ahiahi i te raumati.
He pepeke parauri ka kitea i ngā takutai one māhorahora, he waewae pakari ōna, he kaha ki te pekepeke, ki te whitiwhiti, he pāraharaha te tinana, ka noho i roto i ngā rimurimu kua pāea ki te ākau, he kakama ki te keri rua.
He pepeke parauri ka kitea i ngā takutai one māhorahora.
He pepeke parirau kore kai toto ka kitea i ngā makawe, i ngā huruhuru rānei o raro.
He pepeke rere ahiahi e 20 mirimita te tupu, he kākāriki te tuarā, he pūwherowhero a raro o te tinana, he poto ngā weri.
He pepeke rere ahiahi e 25 mirimita te tupu, he kākāriki, he mōhinuhinu te tuara, he tāhei kōwhai e rere ana i te tuarā, he pūwhero a raro o te tinana, he poto ngā weri.
He pepeke rere e 25-50 mirimita te roa, he hāurauri te tinana whānui, he tino roa ngā weri, he taratara ngā waewae, he kupenga te tauira e waituhi ana i ngā parihau. Kāore te pepeke nei e kai, ka mutu e rua wiki noa e ora ana, ka mate.
He pepeke rere e 25-50 mirimita te roa.
He pepeke rere he maha noa atu ōna momo, e rua ōna parirau kōataata, he kōpuku ngā karu, ka kitea e rērere haere ana i rō whare, e piri ana rānei ki te tuanui, he iro āna punua waewae kore.
He pepeke rere he maha noa atu ōna momo, kia rere ka tamumu tonu, e rua ōna parirau kōataata, he kōpuku ngā karu, ka kitea i te ngahere, i te whare o te tangata i te raumati, i hea atu rānei, he iro āna punua waewae kore.
He pepeke rere kore rite ki te rārā te hanga, he roa te tinana, he kiwikiwi, he parauri, he pākākā, he kākāriki rānei te tae, he tarakina kei te tinana me ngā waewae o ētahi, he iti ake ngā toa i ngā uwha.
He pepeke rere kore rite ki te rārā te hanga.
He pepeke ririki rere pōkai ka kitea i ngā roto, i ngā wāhi haukū, he rite ki te waeroa engari kāore e timo; ka rua, ka toru tau ngā iro e kai ana i te tipu, i te kiko pirau, kia whai parirau kua kore e kai, ā mate rawa e hia wiki nei i muri.
He pepeke ririki rere pōkai ka kitea i ngā roto, i ngā wāhi haukū.
He pepeke roroa ngā waewae tino roa te ihu, kei te pito o te ihu ngā weri o te toa, kei waenganui ō te uwha kia pai ai tana poka rākau ki te whānau i ana hua.
He pepeke roroa ngā waewae, tino roa te ihu.
He pepeke tinana roa, tinana kōrahirahi, he pango, he kōwhai ngā tāwakawaka e rere ana i te tinana, he whānui te whanga o ngā parirau e whā, he karu nunui ōna.
He pepeke tinana roa, tinana kōrahirahi.
He pepeke tino moroiti 1.5 mirimita te tupu, ka kitea i te taha o te wai, he parauri ki te pango te upoko me te tārāuma, he mā ngā parirau me te puku, he ngongo toto ngā uha.
He pepeke tino nui noho rākau, kāore ōna parirau, he tino roa ngā waewae o muri, he taratara ngā waewae katoa engari he nui ngā tara i ngā waewae o muri, he manauri te tinana, he maru whānui ake i te upoko kei te upoko, he tarapī, he tino roa ngā pūhihi, kia mānukanuka kua whanawhana, kua tānapu mai.
He piere i tētahi toka.
He pihinga nīkau kāore anō kia tīwhera noa.
He pikinga poto, he poupou anō.
He piko i te huarahi, i te awa rānei.
He piko i te tānga moko i te kanohi.
He piko ānau he maha ōna tae ka kitea e tū mai ana i te rangi ina kōuaua, ina ua.
He piri mua ka hono tahi ki ngā tau tahi ki te iwa hei tohu i te rahi ka hua ake ina whakareatia taua tau ki te rua tekau.
He pirihi tūranga nui i ngā hāhi Karaitiana, ka tū hei rangatira mō ngā whare karakia katoa o tētahi rohe nui, māna anō e whakatū, e whakahaere ngā pirihi.
He pirihi whai mana i roto i te hāhi Mihingare ka mahi i raro i te mana o te Pīhopa.
He pito rākau koi hei hika ki te kauahi, e puta ai he ahi.
He pito whenua e karapotia ana e te wai.
He pito whenua kei reira te tupuna whare, ngā kāinga noho, ngā kāuta, ngā mahinga kai, ngā urupā, ngā aha atu e ora ai tētahi whānau, tētahi hapū, tētahi iwi.
He pito whenua kua karia, kua ngakia hei wāhi whakatupu kai, aha atu rānei.
He pito whenua noho mākū tonu, he tāpokopoko, he hōhonu, me te tipuria e te raupō, e te harakeke, e te aha atu.
He pito whenua noho mākū tonu, he tāpokopoko, he pāpaku, ka tipuria e ōna anō momo tipu, e ōna anō rākau.
He pito whenua noho mākū tonu, he tāpokopoko, ka tipuria e ōna anō tipu, e ōna anō rākau.
He pito whenua tapu ka noho hei okiokinga mō te tūpāpaku.
He pito whenua teitei e toro atu ana i te tahatika ki te moana, ki te roto rānei.
He poi kōhatu, he poi maitai rānei ka pūhia mai i te pū.
He poi oneone, he tuapuku oneone.
He pokorua i te pari, i te puke, i raro rānei i te whenua.
He pokorua ka karia ki te whenua hei putunga kai. He pakitara ō ētahi, he tuanui, he tomokanga whāiti anō, ko ētahi he karinga noa iho i te whenua, kāore he pakitara engari he whai tuanui, he tomokanga iti anō kei tētahi pito.
He pona i te kāhikuhiku o te neti.
He pona ka herea hei whakamau i te kūaha o te whare.
He pona ka herea ki tētahi momo tipu i te huarahi hei tohu ki tētahi e whai mai ana i muri.
He pona ka tīponatia ki te kokonga o te kete.
He pononga nā Ihu Karaiti.
He poro rākau hei tāmau i te matapihi o te whare.
He poro rākau ka whakatakotoria ki raro i te hanga taumaha, pērā i te waka, e māmā ai te tō haere i taua hanga nā te hurihuri o ngā poro rākau i raro iho.
He poro rākau ka whakatakotoria ki te ara hei mākutu i te tangata.
He poro rākau poto.
He poro rākau pērā i te kāpara ka tahuna tētahi pito, ka kawea haeretia kia kite pai ai ngā karu i te pōuri.
He poro tapawhā ka mahia ki te uku me te onepū kua tunua, kua whakamarokehia ki te ahi, ki te rā rānei. He pai mō te hanga whare me ētahi atu mea.
He porohita hīnātore e karapoti ana i te marama, i te rā, i tētahi atu aorangi, whetū rānei.
He porohita, he hanga āhua rite rānei ki te porohita, ka mahia mai ki tētahi mea pērā i te taura, i te aho, i te miro rānei.
He porotiti, tētahi atu hanga iti rānei ka tuia atu ki te kākahu, mā te kuhu atu ki tōna anō kōhao e mau pai ai te kākahu.
He poto hāpuku.
He poto kahawai.
He pou angiangi roroa whai teka ka whakamahia hei waewae roa, e teitei ake ai te tangata i a ia e hīkoi ana.
He pou hei māroha, hei whakamārō i tētahi mea pērā i te kōmaru o te waka.
He pou hei pupuri mā te tangata i a ia e noho ana i te heketua.
He pou hei toko ake i tētahi mea.
He pou hei toko i te waka.
He pou hei ā i te kehe.
He pou i te tūāhu hei taunga mō te atua ina karangahia e te tohunga.
He pou i whakamahia i te tūāhu mō ētahi karakia.
He pou ka puritia e te tokomaha ki te uma ina whakawhiti i te awa, kia kore ai tētahi e paheke, e riro.
He pou ka whakatūria ki te tūāhu.
He pou ka whakatūria mō te tūā pā.
He pou kua whakairohia a runga, ka whakamahia i ētahi karakia.
He pou māpou ka whakatūria mō te pure i te māra tapu.
He pou mō ngā whakaritenga tapu.
He pou roroa tūtika hei whakairinga mō ngā kōmaru o te waka.
He pou whakairo kei ngā tīwatawata o te pā.
He pou whakairo nō te pā tūwatawata, he rite ki te tangata te āhua.
He pou, he tokotoko rānei e kawea ai tētahi hanga taumaha i waenganui i tētahi tokorua; ka kawe (i tētahi hanga) ki tēnei taputapu.
He pou, tētahi atu mea rānei ka whakatūria mō ngā mahi mākutu.
He pou; he maha noa atu ngā mahi mō te pou nei pērā i te noho hei puritanga ringa i te heketua, hei kauwhata, hei pupuri mā te wahine whakawhānau, hei whakanoho mai i te mōkaikai, hei toko ake i te tāhū o te pewa, hei turu mō te māhanga, hei mahi toemi, hei aha atu, hei aha atu.
He pouaka hei nehu, hei tahu rānei i te tūpāpaku.
He pouaka i te poutāpeta e puritia ai ngā reta mā te tangata nōna te ingoa o runga, hei tiki māna ā tōna wā; he pouaka i tētahi wāhi tūmatanui e tukuna atu ai ngā reta ki tangata kē.
He pouaka iti whai taupoki kua kopia ki te aho; he nohoanga atua nā te tohunga.
He pouaka whakairo hei putunga rau huia, hei putunga taonga rānei.
He pounamu kōataata, he ōriwa ki te kahurangi kākāriki te tae.
He pounamu kōmā te āhua.
He pounamu kōtea te āhua.
He pounamu pērā i te kawakawa engari he kōtingotingo whero, he tāekaeka whero e rere ana i roto.
He pounamu uriuri tonu te tae.
He pounamu whakatīaho, he karera te tae, kāore ōna koha, ōna aha, paruhi kau ana.
He pounamu, he tāingo teatea, he tāekaeka teatea e rere ana i roto.
He poupou te hoa (o te tuanui).
He pua tāhune roroa ka tautau mai i ētahi rākau pērā i te whiro.
He puehu pango, he mahuetanga iho nō te rākau nui te kāpia kua tahuna. Ka whakataerangitia te puehu nei ki te wai o ētahi rākau hei pani ki te kiri kua haehaea e te uhi tā moko.
He puka whaimana ka tukua e te kāwanatanga e whakatūturu ana i te tuakiri o te kaipupuri, e whakaatu ana nō hea ia, e tuku ana i a ia kia toro atu i whenua kē.
He pukapuka e rārangi mai ana ētahi huinga kupu taurite.
He pukapuka e rārangi ā-pū mai ana ētahi kupu o tētahi reo, tae atu ki ngā tikanga me ngā whakamārama o aua kupu.
He pukapuka kawe kōrero, kawe whakaahua ka puta ia wiki, ia marama, i te takanga rānei o tētahi wā kua whakaritea.
He pukapuka whai wāhanga mō ia rā o te tau, e tuhia ai ngā hui, ngā aha noa iho kua whakaritea; he pukapuka hei tuhi i ngā āhuatanga ka pā, ngā mahi ka mahia, me ngā whakaaro ka whakaarohia ia rā.
He puke me te awa i te māra, he rārangi rānei i te māra; he wāhi motuhake i te māra.
He puke oneone iti noa i hangā e te ringa tangata ka whakamahia i roto i ētahi karakia.
He puke oneone, he wāhi tokatoka rānei kei te moana, kei te awa, ka kitea ina mimiti te wai.
He puke onepū.
He puke, he maunga whai pakohu, whai putanga, i puta mai ai, e puta mai ai rānei te rangitoto, te kongakonga toka, te koromāhu me te hau.
He puku e tipu ana i te kahiwi o te rākau, e uhi ana i te pūpeka pihi kore.
He puku i te kiri e kī ana i te wai ka kitea ina wera te kiri, ki te roa rawa rānei te kiri e hikaia ana ki tētahi mea.
He puku iti kei te pito whakamua o te tara o te wahine.
He puku ka puta ki te kiri, ka tupu rānei i roto o te tinana nā tētahi mate, nā te whara rānei.
He puku kei mua o te kakī, kia kōrero, kia horomi ka piki, ka heke; ka tino kitea i te kakī o ētahi tāne.
He puku tetere kei raro i te hiako.
He puna o tētahi matū, o tētahi atu mea rānei he painga ōna mō te tangata, e taea ana te whakapau, te whakamahi rānei ina hiahiatia.
He puna wai ka pupū ake i te manawa o te whenua, e kore e mimiti.
He punga tōpuku e puku mai ana i tētahi mata.
He punua ika.
He punua kuaka.
He punua manu whenua kei te kōhanga tonu.
He punua pāua.
He punua tuna rite ki te kōata te hanga ka piki haere i ngā awa i te kōanga.
He puoto kōata rango te hanga, he papatahi te tou, he ngutu kei te niao e taea ai te riringi mea, whakamahia ai i roto i te taiwhanga pūtaiao.
He pupuhitanga iti ka puta ki te kiri, i ētahi wā he pirau anō kei roto.
He puru e kīia ana kei roto i te ihu o te pēpē kātahi tonu ka whānau mai.
He puru kei te takere o te waka.
He puta i te pakitara, i te tuanui rānei o te whare, i ngā taha rānei o te waka, kua kuhuna atu he hanga whai kōata ki roto kia uru ai te mārama, te hau, kia taea ai rānei a waho te kite atu.
He putanga auahi i te pakitara o mua o te whare, i raro tonu o te tāhuhu.
He putunga ngako i te ruahuru (o te kiri tangata), he āhua kōwhai te tae i te tīmatanga, ka mangu haere i te takanga o te wā. Ka kitea nuitia i te kanohi.
He putunga rīwai.
He pāpaka iti, he mōunu mō te mangō.
He pātai e mōhio tonutia ana te whakautu e te kaipātai.
He pātai e ui ana i te pono, i te tika o tētahi kōrero kātahi tonu ka puta, i te ohorere, i te mīharo o te kaiwhakarongo ki taua kōrero.
He pātai mārama tonu ka hāngai tonu ki te tangata, kāore e taiāwhio i te kaupapa.
He pātaka iti ka noho mai ki runga pou kotahi.
He pātaka kua hoatu he papa ki runga o ia pou hei ārai atu i te kiore.
He pātītī pā te tupu i ngā whenua haukū, i rō tāwhao rānei, e 45-90 henemita te tupu, he papatahi, he kākāriki ngā rau runga tātā whero, he mangaeka ngā pua. Kia maroke haere ngā rau kua rangona tōna kakara.
He pātītī pū te tupu ka kitea i waenga pārae, he pāraharaha, he kikorangi kiwikiwi ngā rau.
He pātītī wai tai e 20-50 henemita te tupu, he rau ōriwa, he whakatīaho, ka tipu ki uta paku mai o tai takoto, haere ake ki tua paku atu o tai takoto; koinei anahe te tipu whai pua o Aotearoa ka tipu ki wai tai.
He pātītī wai tai.
He pātū ka mahia ki te oneone, ki te aha atu hei whakangungu i ngā toa i ngā maioro.
He pātū ka mahia ki te tini manga rākau kua poua ki te whenua.
He pātū uaua kei waenganui i ngā pūkahukahu me te puku.
He pātū, he waonga ka mahia ki te pou, ki te wāwā.
He pēke iti e raua atu ai ngā moni me ērā atu taonga whaiaro iti a te tangata; ka waiho mā te ringa tonu e pupuri, mā te pakihiwi rānei e tākawe.
He pēpē ka whānau tōmua mai.
He pēpē papatahi, he keke papatahi rānei ka mahia ki te aruhe, he kai.
He pīkari kiwi.
He pītau, he pihinga hou (o te huruwhenua, o tētahi atu tipu rānei).
He pōkai tupeka kua takaia ki te pepa, ka tahuna kia momia ai te auahi.
He pōro kōmāmā, he tau tōna, ka piua e te ringa, i te nuinga o te wā hei hoa mō tētahi waiata.
He pōtaka koi ngā pito e rua.
He pōtaka porotaka te tinana, he koi tētahi pito, he pāraharaha te tumuaki, ka kōture mai he pihi i te tumuaki, ka takaia he miro ki te pihi kia huhū ai ina tāia.
He pōtaka porotaka te tinana, he koi tētahi pito, he pāraharaha te tumuaki, kia tāia ki te tā kua hurihuri.
He pū e rua ōna ara matā.
He pū hune toroa hei whakarākei i te tinana.
He pū iti, pērā i ērā ka whai mai i te pū tuatahi o ngā rerenga kōrero me ngā ingoa.
He pū ka pupuhi tonu ki te mau tonu te keunga o te keu.
He pū ka pūhia mai i te pakihiwi, he roa te aramatā, he kōwakawaka tōrino a roto kia tāwhirowhiro ai te matā, e tawhiti ai te rere tōtika.
He pū ka whakawhana i te matā ki te hau pineke.
He pū makawe ka whakamahia i ētahi karakia.
He pū makawe.
He pū poto te ara matā, he pū ka puritia ki te ringa kotahi.
He pū rahi ka noho tuatahi mai ki te kupu tuatahi o te rerenga kōrero, me te ingoa.
He pū tino nui, he taimaha, he whai wīra ētahi, ko ētahi ka whakanōhia ki tōna anō tūāpapa.
He pū, ka whāngaia te waha ki te paura me te matā i te wā kotahi, he kōpaki paura iti kei te wāhi e tau ai te hama kia pahū ai, ka tahuna te paura e rere ai te matā.
He pū, ka whāngaia te waha ki te paura me te matā.
He pū, tētahi atu momo tānga rānei hei whakaatu i tētahi āhuatanga motuhake i roto i ngā mahi pāngarau, pūtaiao, puoro, me ētahi atu wāhi.
He pūeru nō te wahine ka heke atu i te hope ki ngā turi.
He pūhā rau māeneene, he ngohe ngā pūtiotio o ngā rau, he roa, he ngohe anō ngā tātā.
He pūhā rau māeneene.
He pūhā rau taratara.
He pūhā taratara, he tino koi, he tino roa ngā pūtiotio i ngā rau, he mōhinuhinu anō ngā rau.
He pūkohu e iri kōpurepure mai ana ki te rangi.
He pūkohu ngohe hei hopu, hei pupuri i ngā toto i te wā o te mate wahine (i ngā rā o mua); ngā hanga o ēnei rā koinei tāna mahi.
He pūkohu wai tai nui ka tipu i tahatai, i te moana, i runga toka rānei i tua atu o tai aronui.
He pūkoro angiangi ka hangaia ki te rapa, ka whakamaua ki te ure ina ai te tāne, hei ārai hapūtanga, hei ārai mate paipai.
He pūkoro kei te korokoro o te manu hei pupuri i ana kai, ka paku nakunakua i reira i mua o te hekenga ki te puku.
He pūkoro, he uhi rānei (mō te huruhuru whakarākei).
He pūmotu ka kitea i roto i ngā matū pararopi. (Tohu pūtaiao: C)
He pūmotu konganuku kore, he kiwikiwi te tae, he pīataata, he tioata te hanga, ka taea e ia te kawe hiko kia iti nei. (Tohu pūtaiao: Si)
He pūnaha ine ko te tekau te pūtake, ka whakamahia hei whakatau i te roa, i te taumaha, i te rōrahi.
He pūnaha, he tānga rānei e whakaatu ana i te taka o ngā rā, o ngā marama o te tau.
He pūngāwerewere māori 10 mirimita te tipu o te uwha, e 3 mirimita te toa, he pango, he mōhinuhinu, he puku kōpio, he waewae roroa, he tohu whero kei te tuarā.
He pūngāwerewere pākākā nui tonu, he mātotoru, he huruhuru ngā waewae, he huruhuru anō te puku, he rei tapahi whakarunga, whakararo ōna; ka keria he rua hei kāinga mōna, ka whatua he hiraka kia kapi katoa a roto, he hiraka anō te kūaha ki tōna rua.
He pūngāwerewere pākākā, he kunekune te puku, he tarakina kei ngā waewae kōrahirahi, ko tāna he whatu whare tukutuku rite ki te te wīra pahikara te āhua hei hopu pepeke rere.
He pūrei whetū rongonui, e whitu ngā whetū ririki ka hikohiko i ngā rā whakamutunga o Haratua i ia tau.  Ka rewa ake i te rua i te tahatū o te rangi, i mua tata tonu i te aonga ake o te rā.  Ka tīmata ngā whakanuitanga o te tau hou i te kitenga o te kōhiti i te marama i muri tonu mai i te putanga ake o tēnei tātai whetū.
He pūrere haere whenua, he whai pūkaha, e whā ngā wīra, he kawe i te tokoiti tāna mahi.
He pūrere hiko hei whāwhā mā te tangata takitahi, e māmā ai ngā mahi pērā i te tuhi kōrero, te kohikohi me te tātari raraunga, te toro i te Ipurangi, me te kawe i ngā mahi kaute.
He pūrere hiko iti whakamahia ai hei whakaoti i ngā momo tātaitanga katoa, mā te pēpēhi i ngā tau me ngā tohu e tika ana.
He pūrere ka huri i te pūngao kia neke ai te waka, kia mahi ai rānei tētahi atu momo mīhini i tāna mahi e tika ana.
He pūrere tuku mahana.
He pūrerehua rere ahiahi tino nui, he kākāriki, he parauri nga ōpurepure i ngā parirau o mua, he pākākā ngā mea o muri, he hanga iti iho te toa i te uwha, he kōtingotingo kei ngā parirau karera whānui.
He pūrerehua rere pō āhua rahi tonu, he mātotoru ngā pūhihi, he tino roa te arero, he roa, he whāiti ngā parirau pākā kōrito o mua, he poto, he whāiti ō muri, he tāekaeka pango e huri ana i te tinana hauroa, e rua ngā kōiraira whero kei te tinana.
He pūrerehua rere pō āhua rahi tonu.
He pūrori ka tāraia ki te pito runga o te pou i te tūwatawata.
He pūrākau ka tuhia hei whakatinana mā ētahi kaiwhakaari, ka whakaaturia ki te atamira, ka pāhotia rānei ki te reo irirangi, ki te pouaka whakaata, ka mahia rānei hei kiriata.
He pūtake kōekoeko tipu torotika ki roto i te oneone, koia nei te pū e tipu ai ngā piakaaka.
He pūtea iti hei pupuri i te hinu whakakakara.
He pūtoi huruhuru manu hei whakapaipai i ētahi mea pērā i te waka.
He pūtoi huruhuru manu kei te rapa o te waka.
He pūtoi kaka, he paparanga kaka rānei i te kiko e taea ana te kukuti kia oreore ai, kia mārō ai rānei tētahi wāhi o te tinana.
He pūweru hei kākahu i te pito whakararo, i te wāhanga whakararo rānei o ngā waewae; he pūweru mō ngā waewae o te wahine ka kiri rua te piri ki ana waewae.
He raenga e koutu mai ana i te hiwi, i te maunga.
He rahinga, he āhuatanga rānei kāore e pūmau te nui - ka rerekē haere, ka taea rānei te whakarerekē.
He rama ka mahia ki te kāpara.
He rangi kore kapua.
He ranunga haurehu e kitea ana i te kirinuku o Papatūānuku, he māmā te tahu kia kā mai.
He rarauhe ka tupu mai anō i muri i te paunga i te ahi.
He raruraru iti, he kinonga iti.
He rau harakeke.
He rau hei takai i te kai ka taona ki te umu.
He rau iti e rere ana i te tātā rau o ētahi tipu pērā i te huruwhenua, he wāhanga nō te rau matua.
He rau maitai ka whakamaua ki tētahi kakau hei haehae, hei tapahi.
He rau maroke, he otaota pērā i ērā ka pāea e te waipuke.
He rau ponga, he rākau rānei ka whakamahia i roto i ngā karakia hei rāhui, hei tā rānei i te kawa mō te whare hou.
He rau raupō, he whā harakeke, he rau aha atu ka whakamaroketia, ka herepūngia hei tuanui, hei pakitara mō te whare.
He raukura mā (nō te toroa, nō te kōtuku rānei).
He raupapa mahi, he takahanga rānei e tutuki ai tētahi whāinga.
He rawa ka waihangatia e te ringa tangata, he kaha, he māmā, he nui ōna whakamahinga.
He reo e tauhou ana ngā oro, kāore e mārama ana te tikanga o ngā kupu.
He reo ka rangona e waiata ana i te pō i raro i te awe o tētahi wairua. Ahakoa reo wairua rānei, ahakoa tira haere rānei, he tohu aituā tahi.
He reo wairua ka rangona i te pō, i te takutai moana.
He reo wairua ka rangona i te wai e rere ana.
He reo wairua, he tohu kino.
He reo, he oro kāore e tino mārama te rangona atu.
He rere whakamua ki te whawhai ki te hoariri.
He rerenga aho ka whiti mai i te rā, i te whetū, i tētahi atu hanga rānei.
He rerenga aho mahana ka whiti mai i te rā.
He rerenga aho.
He rerenga kōrero poto e mōhio nuitia ana, he kupu pono, he tohutohu rānei kei roto.
He rerenga kōrero roa ka whakahuahuatia e te tamariki i te hā kotahi.
He rerenga toto ka pakaru mai i te ia toto kua pahū.
He rerenga wai iti ka karia e te tangata.
He rerenga wai ka maringi iho i tētahi wāhi poupou, tētahi wāhi tiketike tonu.
He rerenga wai ka whati mai i te awa matua me te whai i ara kē.
He rerenga wai kua maroke.
He rerenga wai māori e whai ana i tōna ara whānui tonu, hōhonu tonu, ko tōna otinga atu ko tētahi roto, ko te moana rānei.
He rerenga wai māori iti e rere ana ki te awa, ki te roto, ki te moana rānei.
He rerenga wai māori tino iti e rere ana ki te awa, ki te kōawa, ki te roto, ki te moana rānei.
He rerenga wai tere tonu te āmiomio, he au kukume tōna e romia ai ngā mea ka tūpono atu ki roto i a ia.
He rerenga wai, ahakoa nui, ahakoa iti, ahakoa māori, ahakoa karia rānei e te tangata.
He rimurimu mōhinuhinu ka tipu runga toka, he waiporoporo kiwikiwi, he kākāriki rānei te tae, he kai.
He rimurimu piri toka i kō paku atu o tai takoto, i ngā tahatika e ākina ana e te tai, he whānui, he roroa, he pāraharaha ngā rau tokorera, he parauri, he koura rānei te tae.
He rimurimu piri toka i kō paku atu o tai takoto.
He ringaringa, he waewae rānei e ngoikore ana te tupu o ngā uaua.
He ripa i te whakairo e wehe ana i ngā rārangi pākati.
He ripa, he kopa rānei kei te mata o tētahi mea māeneene pērā i te kiri.
He riri hauwarea noa iho.
He riri i waenga i ētahi iwi mō te wahine, mō te whenua me ētahi take pēnei.
He riri i waenganui i ētahi iwi e rua.
He riri i waenganui i ētahi tāngata nō te iwi kotahi.
He riri i waenganui i ētahi wehenga o te hapū, o te iwi, o te motu rānei.
He riri ka mutu ina mate katoa tētahi taha.
He rite ki te 'ko tēnei', ki te 'ko ēnei', ki te 'ko tēnei te take' rānei.
He rite ki te 'ko tēnā', ki te 'ko ēnā', ki te 'ko tēnā te take' rānei.
He rite ki te 'ko tērā', ki te 'ko ērā', ki te 'ko tērā te take' rānei.
He riwha, he wāhanga kino i te papa, i te kōhatu, i te aha atu.
He roherohenga whenua i te pāmu.
He rongo pūmau.
He rongo āhua kino ki te ihu.
He rongoā ka mahia kia mārō, kia iti te hanga, kia taea ai te horopuku.
He rourou mō te kūmara ka whakamahia i te kawa pure; he tapawhā te hanga, he mea raranga ki te harakeke, he kāwai i ōna tapa, he mea ruruku ngā taha ki te aho kua tuia i ngā kāwai.
He rua hei hopu kiore.
He rua hōhonu i tētahi awa, i te takutai moana rānei, he rua wai hōhonu i te whenua rānei pērā i te puna.
He rua hōhonu tonu.
He rua hōhonu.
He rua i keria i te whenua hei tohu i te wāhi i hinga ai tētahi rangatira.
He rua i keria ki te whenua mō ngā wairua o te hoariri ka poapoaina mai e te tohunga, ki reira patua ai ki te karakia.
He rua i raua atu ai te rīwai me te onepū, ka takatakahia kia pahore mai ai te peha.
He rua i te ihonui o te whare kua whakatakotoria atu he kōhatu ki roto, hei pae ahi.
He rua i te whenua ka nohoia e te manu.
He rua i te whenua, i te rākau, he hanga tamomo rānei ka hangaia e te manu hei whānau i ana hua, hei kāinga mō ana pīpī; he wāhi i te whenua ka whakapaipaitia e te kararehe pērā i te poaka, hei kāinga mō ana punua.
He rua ka karia ki te whenua (mō te whakatō taro, mō te rau atu rānei i ngā tuna kua mau ki te matire, mō te aha atu).
He rua ka karia ki te whenua kia taea ai ngā wai kei raro i te whenua; he kōpua māori e piki mai ai te wai o te whenua ki te mata o te whenua.
He rua ka keria hei wāhi tao kai ki te kōhatu wera.
He rua kai kua koropaepaetia ki te tīrongo.
He rua kūmara.
He rua taewa.
He ruku poto kāore i pai te mahinga mai.
He rā e whitu, he pō e whitu.
He rākau 10 mita te tipu, he rau pinerua niho roa manawa te hanga, he whero te kakau o ngā rau, he whero, he pango rānei ngā hua i ngā rākau wahine; te hua o te makomako.
He rākau 10 mita te tipu.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he hohoko ngā rau, he mā, he ririki ngā kōtingotingo kei ngā rau, he niho ririki kei te kāmata, he pua mā whai kōtingotingo waiporoporo ōna, he waiporoporo ngā hua.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he nawe kōpae e rere ana i te kahiwi, he kōpuku kei te take o ngā rau tino roa, he pua māwhero, he hua whero pū roa te tupu ka tautau mai i raro i te kōpuku; te rau o te nīkau; te hua o te nīkau.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko kakau roa,  e 8 ki te 12 ngā tawheraiti o ngā rau, he niho roa, he more rānei ngā tapa, he pua whero pūhui roa te tupu, he hua whero, he pango te kākano; te hua tītoki.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko niho ririki, he pua karera ka tipu i ngā peka, he hua waiporoporo ririki i ngā rākau wahine; te hua o te māhoe.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko whai niho tōpuku, he pua mā, whetū te hanga.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko, he kakara, he kōratarata, he kōwhai te karawhā, he pūngarungaru ngā tapa, he ririki, he kākāriki ngā pua, he pango ngā hua.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko, he kōratarata, he whāiti, he niho roa tonu kei ngā rau, he mā ngā pua whetū te hanga.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko, he tuawhiti, he niho tāwhitiwhiti kei ngā tapa, he kahotea, he ririki ngā pua, he kakara, he pango ngā hua ririki kei ngā rākau wahine; te hua o te kaikōmako.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau kāwitiwiti roa pū te tupu i te kāmata o ngā peka, he niho ririki kei ngā tapa o ngā rau, he koikoi te kāmata, he pūhui roa te tupu mai o ngā pua whero i te rito.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau kōwhai parauri whai tāingoingo whero, he kahurangi kākāriki te angamate, he pua kahotea kakara rite ki te whetū te āhua, he hua pango pōī te tupu.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau ririki whai tāingoingo kōwhai, he angiangi ngā rau whai niho koi, he pua kakara pōī te tupu, he hua pango.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he rau tipitaha ōna, he tuawhiti, he kōratarata te taha whakarunga, he pua kākāriki pūhui roa te tupu, he waiporoporo pango ngā hua i ngā rākau wahine.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he toro whakarunga ngā peka me ngā rau, e kapi katoa ana te angamate o ngā rau i te huruhuru mā, he koinga kei te kāmata o ngā rau, he pua karera whai huruhuru mā, he pōī te tupu.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu, he whānui, he tautau te tipu o ngā peka, he pinerua, he ririki he tōpuku ngā rau, he tautau, he poto, he pūhui roa te tipu o ngā pua kōwhai, he parauri, he pukupuku ngā pākākano; te pua o te kōwhai.
He rākau 10 mita te tupu.
He rākau 12 mita te tipu, he rau pinerua, he tāwhitiwhiti ngā niho ririki  i ngā tapa, he pua karera, he hua karaka pū te tipu i ngā rākau wahine; te hua o tēnei rākau.
He rākau 12 mita te tipu.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he hohoko, he whāiti ngā rau whai niho pūhuki, he kahotea ngā pua pūhui roa te tipu, he pere tautau te hanga, he waiporoporo ngā hua; te hua o te hīnau.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he kārikiuri ngā rau, he horotea te angamate, he huruhuru ngā iaia, he rau ngahoro i te takurua, he pua whero tautau ōna, he hua waiporoporo; te hua o te kōtukutuku.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he kōratarata, he kakara ngā rau, he pūngarungaru ngā tapa, he kahotea te tuaka me te kakau, he whetū te hanga o ngā pua kahotea pōī te tupu, he parauri ngā hua.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he pinerua, he whāiti, he roa ngā rau, he kōwhai, he roa, he pūhui roa te tipu o ngā pua, he pukupuku, he parauri te pākākano; te pua o te kōwhai.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he rahirahi, he roroa, he pū te tipu o ngā rau makiki, he koi te kāmata o ngā rau, he mā, he pere te hanga o ngā pua pūhui roa te tupu mai i te rito.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko koi te kāmata, he whāiti anō hoki, he roa, he pua kōwhai kakara pūhui roa te tupu, he huruhuru kōkōwai kei ngā kakau, he ponguru mā ngā hua.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko whai niho koi roa, he mā, he kakara ngā pua, i ōna wā anō ka ngahoro te nuinga o ngā rau.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he rau nunui pinerua te tupu o ngā tawheraiti, he tawheraiti nui tonu kei te kāmata, he niho ririki kei ngā tapa, he taratara, he pūhui roa te tupu o ngā pua, he whero ngā hua.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he rau tapa niho pūhuki, he pua mā kakau roa te tipu, he ponguru whero ngā hua, he tarawai rite ki te miraka tō tēnei rākau.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he rau tōpuku ririki whai niho tōpuku, he mā ngā pua kakau roa te tupu, he ponguru whero ngā hua, he tarawai rite ki te miraka tō tēnei rākau.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu, he rau whānui whai tapa pūngarungaru, he pūhuki te kāmata, he kahotea, he kakara ngā pua, he hua waiporoporo e rere ana i ngā rārā.
He rākau 12 mita te tupu.
He rākau 12-20 mita te tipu, he torotika te kahiwi, he roa, he whāiti ngā rau pū te tipu i te kāmata o ngā peka, he mā he kakara ngā pua pūhui roa te tipu, he mā ngā hua, he kōtingotingo kahurangi kei runga.
He rākau 12-20 mita te tipu.
He rākau 15 mita te tipu, he rau pinerua, he more ngā tapa, he tiwha kei te kāmata, he poi taratara te tipu o ngā pua whero; te pua o tēnei rākau.
He rākau 15 mita te tupu, he hohoko, he pinerua anō te tupu o ngā rau, he kaitara ngā rau, he huruhuru te angamate, he niho ririki kei ngā tapa, he karera ngā pua, he whero ngā hua tino reka. He rākau tēnei i āta whakatipuria e te Māori i mua.
He rākau 15 mita te tupu, he kārikiuri, he kōratarata ngā rau, he pua karera pūhui roa te tupu, he karaka, he nui ngā hua.
He rākau 15 mita te tupu, he pinerua, he kōratarata ngā rau, he tātā roa whai pua mā ka tipu mai i te kahiwi me ngā peka, he kākāriki te hua, he whero ngā kākano ina kōihi te hua o te kohekohe.
He rākau 15 mita te tupu, he rau hohoko kakau roa te tupu, e 8 ki te 12 ngā tawheraiti i ngā rau, he hanga matakahi ngā tawheraiti, he koroī ngā hua, he pōī te tupu.
