He rākau e 8 mita te tupu, he rau whāiti roa tonu, he pua māwhero ka tipu mai i ngā kaupeka, he hua whero, he kōwhai ngā wana; ngā hua o tēnei rākau.
He rākau e 8 mita te tupu, he tuawhiti, he tino nui ngā rau, he kōratarata a runga, he horotea te angamate, he pua karera tātā tūtika te tupu, he hua pango.
He rākau e 8 mita te tupu, he tōpuku, he ririki ngā rau, he kōtingotingo kei raro, he pua karera, he hua parauri pōī te tupu, he pango ngā kākano, he kakara ngā rau o tēnei rākau.
He rākau e 8 mita te tupu, kotahi ki te toru ngā mati o ngā rau hohoko, he niho ririki kei waenganui o ngā tapa ki te kāmata, he ririki, he kākāriki ngā pua, he pango ngā hua pūhui roa te tupu.
He rākau e 8 mita te tupu.
He rākau e 9 mita te tupu, he hohoko te tipu o ngā rau, he kōratarata a runga, he horotea te angamate, he kurauri, he kakara ngā pua, he pango, he hāpiapia ngā kākano, he poi iti te pākākano.
He rākau e 9 mita te tupu, he rau karera kōratarata, he pūngarungaru ngā tapa, he pua kurauri, he pango rānei, he pango, he hāpiapia ngā kākano, he poi iti te pākākano; ngā rau whakakakara o te kohuhu; te pia whakakakara o te kohuhu.
He rākau e 9 mita te tupu, he rau whāiti roroa whai tāingoingo whero, he tapa pūngarungaru, he pua mā pūhui roa te tupu, he hua parauri ririki.
He rākau e 9 mita te tupu.
He rākau e herea atu ai te whakahope.
He rākau e kā ana tētahi pito, ka purihia ki te ringa hei tūrama i te pōuri, hei aha atu.
He rākau e takoto whakapae ana i te mutu, ka herea ki ētahi peka rākau e rua hei tauranga mō te manu.
He rākau hei kai mā te ahi.
He rākau hei nekeneke, hei kōrori rānei.
He rākau hei patu manu.
He rākau hei patu tuna.
He rākau hei tango mātaitai i ngā toka.
He rākau hei torotoro i te ahi.
He rākau hei wero i te hoariri, kei tōna 2 mita nei te roa.
He rākau hei whakapuare tonu i te waha o te kupenga hopu kōkopu.
He rākau hei ārahi i te kurī, ko tētehi pito e mau ana ki te kara.
He rākau hei āwhina i te tangata i a ia e hīkoi ana, he reke, he piko rānei kei te pito whakarunga.
He rākau iti (pērā i te mānuka) e mātotoru ana te tupu tahi.
He rākau iti 1 mita te tupu, he kōratarata te taha whakarunga o ngā rau, he huruhuru mā kei raro, he niho roa tonu kei ngā tapa, he mā, he waiporoporo ngā pua nunui tonu.
He rākau iti 1-2 mita te tupu ki runga i tētahi atu rākau nui.
He rākau iti 1-2 mita te tupu, he pounamu ngā rau taiāwhio te tupu i ngā peka, he koi te kāmata o ngā rau, he pua whero ririki, he piko whakamuri ngā raupua; kia tipu māori mai te rākau nei ka tipu i runga i tētahi atu rākau, kāore ngā paiaka e tae ake ki te whenua.
He rākau iti e 2 ki te 5 mita te tupu, he rau pinerua torutoru noa, he rārā papatahi whai kōwakawaka, he pūkanohi e rere ana i ngā rārā, ranea ana te tupu o ngā pua, he pākākano roa tonu.
He rākau iti e 2 ki te 5 mita te tupu.
He rākau iti e 2 mita te tupu, he niho pūhuki kei te tapa o ngā rau iti, he rite te hanga o ngā pua mā ki te pere, he māwhero, he whero ngā hua.
He rākau iti e 2 mita te tupu, he whīwhiwhi te tupu o ngā tātā, he rau tino ririki, he mā ngā pua ririki, he hua parauri ririki e rere ana i ngā tātā.
He rākau iti e 2 mita te tupu.
He rākau iti e 2-5 mita te tupu.
He rākau iti e 3 mita te tupu, he whīwhiwhi te tupu o ngā peka, he rau kārikiuri, he rauwhero rānei, he pua kōwhai rite ki te whetū te āhua, he hua whero.
He rākau iti e 3 mita te tupu.
He rākau iti e 90 henemita te tupu, he pinerua te tupu o ngā rau kārikiuri, he pūhui roa te tupu o ngā pua mā.
He rākau iti e 90 henemita te tupu.
He rākau iti ka whiua e te matakite ki te papa, kei te āhua tonu o te tau atu o ngā rākau e mōhio ai ia he aha ngā āhuatanga ka pā.
He rākau iti nō te whānau karaka.
He rākau iti tipu ki te māheuheu, ki te tāhuna rānei, he rau pinerua ririki torutoru noa, he rārā papatahi whai kōwakawaka, he pua māwhero ranea te tupu, he pākākano roa tonu, he whero ngā kākano.
He rākau iti tipu ki te rei, 1 mita te tupu, he roa ngā rau, he niho pūhuki maha kei ngā tapa, he mā, he māwhero, he waiporoporo ngā pua, he pua nunui tonu.
He rākau iti, he rākau hūtoitoi e manomano ana, e apiapi ana te tupu tahi.
He rākau ka herea he pūpū noke, he pūpū huhu rānei ki tētahi pito, ka toua atu ki te wai ki te toitoi tuna, ki te toitoi kōkopu.
He rākau ka kawea e te ia o te wai, ka rukea mai rānei ki uta.
He rākau ka nohoia e te kererū.
He rākau ka nohoia e te manu ina kaha haere te mōmona.
He rākau ka takoto whakapae hei whakapakari ake, hei taunaki i te waka.
He rākau ka tukua e te taputapu e kīia nei he kōpere.
He rākau ka whakamahia i ngā karakia pure.
He rākau ka whakamaua atu ki te pito whakarunga o te tumu, o te tuke kia pai ai te whakairi i te taputapu hopu manu nei ki te rākau.
He rākau ka whakatakotoria ki runga i te tuanui o te whare hei pupuri i ngā kākaho, i ngā toetoe kua tīrepatia atu.
He rākau kei waenga i te 50 henemita me te 15 mita te  tupu i ngā paenga wai tai, he rau tuawhiti kōratarata a runga, he huruhuru te angamate, he hua kākāriki pōī te tupu, ka kitea ngā paiaka o te rākau nei e pihi ake ana i te paru ina takoto te tai.
He rākau ki reira hopukina ai te manu ki te mutu.
He rākau koi hei titi atu, hei wero atu i te kai, ka whāngai ai ki te waha.
He rākau koi roa ka titia ki te kiko o te manu, o te aha, kia pai ai te tunutunu ki te ahi.
He rākau kotahi tuke pea te roa, ka whiua e tētahi ki tētahi i te kēmu tī rākau.
He rākau kāore ōna whakapaipai, ōna aha, ka whakamahia hei rākau whawhai.
He rākau maunga 10 mita te tupu, he rau kāwitiwiti roa pū te tupu i te kāmata o ngā peka, he māeneene ngā tapa, he pua whero kei runga tātā torotika ka tupu mai i te rito.
He rākau nō Te Moana-nui-a-Kiwa, he porotaka, he kākāriki, he kākano kore ngā hua; ngā hua o te rākau nei. Kia tunutunua ki te ahi hei kai, he rite ki te parāoa.
He rākau nō te whānau karaka engari kāore i rite ki te karaka te teitei o te tupu. He rākau ka kitea i Pātea.
He rākau pirau.
He rākau popo ka whakamahia hei tahu ahi.
He rākau popoto te tupu, he maha ngā peka o te nuinga, e pihi mai ana ngā peka i te whenua tonu, i runga paku ake rānei.
He rākau poto mō te patu mangō.
He rākau poutū kua herea atu he rākau huapae poto ake ki te takiwā whakarunga, e nērahia atu ai, e herea atu ai te tangata, hei whakamate i a ia; he tohu e pēnei ana te hanga e waitohu ana i te whakapono Karaitiana, he tohu whakamaumahara ki te matenga o Ihu Karaiti.
He rākau pīngore roa ka whakamaua atu he aho, he maihea, he matau hei hī ika.
He rākau pūhou, e pakari ana te tupu engari kāore anō i pakeke noa, i nunui.
He rākau rere hauroki i te tapa whakararo o te kōmaru o te waka.
He rākau rite ki te tī kōuka engari 1 mita noa iho te tupu, he roa ngā rau kōekoeko pū te tupu, he mā, he kakara ngā pua pūhui roa te tupu.
He rākau rite ki te tī kōuka engari 1 mita noa iho te tupu.
He rākau roa hei tautoko i te aho ina hī ika mai i te waka, hei hī tuna rānei.
He rākau roroa ka whakamaua atu he pae ki runga, ka tautau mai he tohe i te pae, ka tākirihia te tohe ki te aho e mau ai he manu.
He rākau roroa whai pae, whai karu māhanga, whai aho ka kawea haerehia hei hopu kākā.
He rākau taha tai e 20 mita te tipu.
He rākau taha tai e 20 mita te tupu, he kahiwi kōraparapa tōna, he rau pinerua, he horotea te taha whakararo o ngā rau, he poi taratara te tipu o ngā pua whero; te pua o tēnei rākau.
He rākau taha tai e 20 mita te tupu.
He rākau taha tai e 8 mita te tupu, he tū toka, he tūtika, he taitakoto rānei, he rau tuawhiti piko whakararo, he kōratarata, he karaka ngā hua pōī te tupu; te hua o tēnei rākau.
He rākau taha tai e 8 mita te tupu.
He rākau taitakoto te tupu, he tuawhiti ngā rau ririki, he tuawhiti te tuaka, he hua whero whai kākano kākāriki i ngā rākau wahine, he pōī te tupu o ngā hua.
He rākau takoto huapae e tautoko ana i te raho o te waka.
He rākau taratara e 6 mita te tupu, he rau kōratarata tuawhiti pū te tupu i raro iho i ngā taratara, kei reira anō ngā pua mā, he parauri ngā hua.
He rākau taratara e 6 mita te tupu.
He rākau tokomanga hei tunutunu kai ki te ahi.
He rākau tokomanga mō te hopu tuna.
He rākau tokomanga roa hei hīrau i tētahi mea; i āta tapahia te peka rākau i te torohanga tonu kia tokomanga te hanga, ka hurihia te pito kia whīwhiwhi ai ki ngā rau o te mea e hīrautia ana.
He rākau tīwhana kei te anga o te mahau o te waka haere i te au o te moana.
He rākau wero tuna, kotahi tōna pito koi.
He rākau whai aho hei maka pere.
He rākau whai tongari hei āwhina i te tangata e tātai whakapapa ana.
He rākau whakamate whai arahāmoa e pūhia atu ai te matā me te kariri.
He rākau wharemoa, he rua rānei i tētahi rākau, ka noho hei kōhanga mō te kākā.
He rākau whawhai e rite ana ki te taiaha; i hangā te nuinga ki te maire.
He rākau whawhai e whitu ki te waru putu te roa, he koi ngā pito e rua.
He rākau whawhai i hangā ki te iwi parāoa, he poto, he pāraharaha.
He rākau whawhai i hangā ki te kōhatu, i whakamaua atu anō he taura kia pai ai te whiu ka kukume mai anō.
He rākau whawhai i hangā ki te maitai.
He rākau whawhai i hangā ki te rākau.
He rākau whawhai i mahia ki te rara parāoa, kei tōna 1.5 mita pea te roa, he ānau te āhua, he kāwitiwiti te pito ki te rau, ka herea he taura ki te puare i te poro, ko tētahi pito ka herea ki te maro o te toa, kia mau tonu ai i a ia. He rākau tuku whakarere tēnei.
He rākau whawhai ka hangā ki te kahikātoa.
He rākau whawhai ka hangā ki te maitai, he koi tētahi mata o te rau, ngā mata e rua rānei, he koi te pito o te rau, he kakau whai ārai kei tērā atu pito. Ka hāpaingia ki te wero, ki te hahau, ki te tapahi rānei i te hoariri.
He rākau whawhai ka hangā ki tēnei rākau.
He rākau whawhai ka tukuna ki tētahi iwi noho tata hei tono i a rātou kia uru mai ki tētahi ope tauā.
He rākau whawhai kei tōna 1.5 mita pea te roa, he pāraharaha te pito ki te rau, ka tāraia he upoko me te arero whātero ki tērā atu pito, ka tauria a runga ake i te upoko ki te huru manu, ki te awe. He rākau tēnei e  werohia ai, e hāua ai rānei te hoariri.
He rākau whawhai kei tōna rua mārō nei te roa, he koi tētahi pito, he pūreke kei tētahi.
He rākau whawhai nō nehe.
He rākau whawhai poto i hangā ki te kōhatu mō te whawhai kanohi ki te kanohi, he tōpuku a runga, ka kāwetoweto haere ki te reke o te kakau.
He rākau whawhai poto i hangā ki te parāoa, ki te rākau rānei, he rite te rau ki te tākihi tangata.
He rākau whawhai poto i hangā ki te rākau, ki te poroiwi rānei, he whakapakoko kei tētahi taha o te rau, he waha kei tētahi.
He rākau whawhai poto ka whiua ki te hoariri ina tata mai.
He rākau whawhai poto mō te whawhai kanohi ki te kanohi, ka hangā ki te parāoa, ki te koiki rānei, e rua ngā waha huaki i ngā taha, he whawhati rākau te mahi, he tīkaro hoki.
He rākau whawhai poto, he rite ki te mere pounamu engari i mahia ki te kāpara.
He rākau whawhai poto, he taputapu rānei ka waihangatia ki te pounamu.
He rākau whawhai poto, ka kawea i te tātua.
He rākau whawhai poto.
He rākau whawhai rite ki te kani te āhua, he niho mangō kua houhia ki te rākau.
He rākau whawhai roa, he koi ngā pito e rua, kei tōna 4 ki te 5 mita te roa.
He rākau whawhai tapu i tāraia ki te pounamu, whakamahia ai hei patu i te ika o te pakanga.
He rākau whawhai whai taura, ka piua.
He rākau whawhai āhua rite ki te taiaha engari kāore he arero whakairo, he pito koi kē tōna; he upoko whakairo tō ētahi, engari he iti.
He rākau whawhai, he haehae te mahi.
He rākau whawhai, he pūreke kei tētahi pito, he koi tētahi taha.
He rākau whawhai, he rākau hei tohutohu i te taua, i hangā ētahi ki te parāoa, kei te roa o te tangata tōna roa, he upoko hau tōna, he whānui, he pāraharaha, ka puhipuhia te tākakī ki te huruhuru manu.
He rākau whawhai, i hangā ki te pakiaka o te rākau.
He rākau whawhai, i hangā ki te rara o te parāoa.
He rākau whawhai.
He rākau, he aha atu kua rukea mai e te tai ki uta.
He rākau, he aha atu rānei kua mau ki tētahi wāhi o te awa, o te roto, o te whanga, ka whakararu i te haere mā reira.
He rākau, he maitai, he aha atu ka rere hauroki, ka rere hāngai rānei ki tētahi hanga, i waenga rānei i tētahi anga, ko tāna he tautoko, he whakapakari i te tū a taua hanga.
He rākau, he maitai, he aha atu ka rere hāngai ki tētahi hanga, i waenga rānei i tētahi anga, ko tāna he tautoko, he whakapakari i te tū a taua hanga.
He rākau, he papa, he aha atu, ka rere tītaha hei taunaki, hei whakapakari, hei whakatina i tētahi mea.
He rākau, he wāhanga rānei o te ngahere ka nohoia, ka hokia e te manu.
He rāpoi pua e noho mai ai tēnā me tēnā pua ki tētahi tātā poto, ko ēnei ka rere i tētahi tātā matua. Ka pua tuatahi mai ko ngā pua e tata ana ki te tātā matua, haere ake ki tōna kāmata.
He rārangi e whakaatu ana āhea tū ai, āhea rānei mahia ai ētahi kaupapa ngā wāhanga rānei o tētahi kaupapa.
He rārangi huruhuru e tipu ana i te tapa o te paerunga me te paeraro.
He rārangi iti ka noho mai i runga tata ake i te oropuare, e tohu ana he roa tōna whakahuatanga.
He rārangi ka tāia kia awhe i te hope o te wahine.
He rārangi kāreti e tūhono ana tētahi ki tētahi, ka kumea haeretia e te waka whai pūkaha o mua, e tētahi atu momo pūkaha rānei.
He rārangi pohewa e wehe ana i te haurua whakarunga me te haurua whakararo o te ao.
He rārangi pou ka poua ki raro i te wai hei whakararu i ngā waka o te hoariri.
He rārangi puke matua.
He rārangi puke, he roa, he papatairite te kahiwi.
He rārangi rere poupou i te mahere whenua mai i te pito raki ki te pito tonga o te ao, koia e tohu ana kei hea ake o te ao tētahi whenua, tētahi wāhi.
He rārangi rere whakapae i te mahere whenua, ko ētahi kei te raki, ko ētahi kei te tonga o te weheruatanga o te ao, koia e tohu ana kei hea ake o te ao tētahi whenua, tētahi wāhi.
He rārangi torotika ka rere i tētahi taha o te porohita ki tētahi, me te haukoti anō i te pū.
He rārangi tānga moko.
He rārangi tōrino i te tānga moko.
He rārangi wai ka pupuke ake i te mata o te moana i te kukume o te tai, i te pupuhi rānei o te hau.
He rārangi whakarara i te mahi whakairo.
He rārangi, he mahere rānei e tohu ana i te wā, i te wāhi anō pea, e haere ai tētahi mahi.
He rārangi, he tapa, he mata, tētahi atu hanga rānei kāore e rere torotika, engari ka kopa haere mai i tētahi pito ki tētahi, pērā i te āniwaniwa.
He rārangi, he tohu rānei ka noho mai ina whētuia, ina pēhia, ina kopenutia rānei tētahi mea.
He rārangi, he tohu, he aha atu rānei e wehe ana i tētahi mea i tētahi atu.
He rārā maroke.
He rīwai kua nui haere engari kei te angiangi tonu te kiri, arā kāore anō i pakari.
He rīwai, he kūmara, he huawhenua pēnei rānei, ka wehea mai hei whakatipu e puta ai he tipu hou, he huawhenua hou.
He rōnakitanga poupou (pērā i te tahataha o te hiwi).
He rōpū he mea kōwhiri ngā tāngata o runga hei whakahaere i tētahi mea, hei tāpae whakaaro rānei.
He rōpū ka tohua e te kāwanatanga hei āta tirotiro, hei āta whewhera i tētahi mea whai take.
He rōpū ka waiata tahi.
He rōpū ka whakatūria e ngā kaimahi hei tiaki i ā rātou tikanga me ngā mea e tika ana kia whakawhiwhia ki a rātou i roto i tā rātou mahi.
He rōpū ka whakatūria hei hāpai kaupapa, hei whakatutuki whāinga.
He rōpū ka āta whakaakona ki te tū ki te haka, ki te poi, ki te waiata ā-ringa, ki te waiata mōteatea, e whakataetae ai, e whakangahau ai rātou.
He rōpū kaimahi kāore e kimi utu mō tā rātou i mahi ai.
He rōpū kaimahi, he rōpū pononga rānei.
He rōpū kaitākaro ko rātou tētahi taha o tētahi whakataetae, o tētahi tākaro, o tētahi hākinakina.
He rōpū kua āta whakaritea kia waiata tahi.
He rōpū rangatira, he kaumātua rānei ka noho ki te whakahaere i ngā take a te iwi.
He rōpū tokoiti ka whakatangitangi taonga puoro, ka waiata, ki te whakangahau, ki te whakakanikani i tētahi whakaminenga.
He rōpū tāngata kua whakakotahi i runga i tētahi kaupapa motuhake pērā i te hākinakina, i te hauora, i te aha atu rānei.
He rōpū whaimana ka noho ka whiriwhiri, ka whakatau i ngā take matua o tētahi whakahaere.
He rōpū whāiti ka kōwhiria e tētahi hunga nui ake hei āta whiriwhiri, hei āta whewhera i tētahi take, hei tāpae pūrongo rānei mō tētahi take.
He rōpū ākonga ka noho tahi, ka ako tahi.
He rūma e ako ai te ākonga i ngā mātauranga ka whāngaihia atu e te kaiako.
He rūma, he kāpata rānei e waihotia ai ngā kai, tae atu pea ki ētahi utauta kai.
He rūma, he whare, he whakaruruhau rānei ki reira tunua ai te kai.
He rūnanga nui mō ngā minita, ngā rangatira me ngā kanohi o te hunga whakapono o tētahi hāhi.
He taewa ka tupu noa mai.
He taewa kua kino, kua kupango te kiri i te rā.
He tahua kai nui ka horaina e te tangata whenua kia ngata ai ana manuhiri, he tohu manaaki, he tohu mana; he tahua kai nui hei whakanui i tētahi kaupapa; he kai hei whakatutuki i ngā mahi tapu o tētahi kaupapa pērā i te tangihanga, te pure, te huamata, te whakamānu waka, te aha atu, te aha atu.
He tahā kua tapahia mai te pito iti hei taupoki.
He tahā kōpio.
He tahā rahi.
He tahā waha whāiti.
He tai iti noa te paringa mai ki uta, iti noa te hokinga whakawaho, ka pā i muri mai i te Ahotu me te Okoro.
He tai ka heke ki tawhiti noa atu, pērā i te heke o te tai ina pā te tai toko i te wā ki a Ōturu me Whitireia.
He tai teka tino nui ka pā i muri tonu mai o Ōturu me Whitireia, hei konei kitea ai te tai rere.
He taiaha ko te awe o te upoko kua herea ki te aute.
He taiapa e toro ana i te whāroa o te awa, he pūrangi, he hīnaki kei te ngutu o ngā paihau, hei hopu tuna, aha atu rānei,
He taiapa, he awamate, he oneone kua whakapukea ki waho o te pā hei kaupare atu i te hoariri, kia kaha ake ai te pā.
He taiapa, he pātū, he aha atu hei pare atu i te hoariri.
He taiapa, he pātū, he aha atu, hei ārai atu, hei pare atu i ngā āki mai a te hoariri, a tētahi atu mea rānei.
He taiepa hakahaka e pātata ana ki te waha o te pā, kei tētahi mahinga rānei hei ārai atu i te poaka, i te kararehe.
He taio makawe ka waiho kia roa i tētahi taha o te upoko ahakoa tapahia atu ētahi kia poto, hei tohu i te taurere, i te hiahia rapu utu rānei; kei te taha katau o te upoko mehemea he uri tata te tūpāpaku.
He taio makawe ka whakamahia i ngā karakia i te tūāhu me ētahi atu wāhi hoki.
He taio makawe kei te wāhi whakamua o te māhunga kua waiho kia roa te tipu, ka tapahi atu ai i te toenga kia poto.
He taitama kātahi anō ka puta i tana whawhai tuatahi.
He taiwhanga, he huinga taiwhanga, he whare rānei e whakahaeretia ai ngā mahi noho tou o te pakihi.
He takiwā pō kerekere e tata ana ki Māhutonga, me te mea nei he angotanga i Te Mangōroa.
He takiwā pōkerekere o te rangi e tata ana ki Te Taki-o-Autahi.
He takotoranga mō te tūpāpaku, he tapawhā te hanga, he taupoki rauwhare kei runga.
He takotoranga oneone rahi nō tētahi iwi, he kāwanatanga, he mana whakahaere motuhake tōna.
He takotoranga wai hei titiro mā te tangata i tōna āhua.
He takotoranga wai ka kitea i te onepū ina timu te tai.
He takotoranga wai māori, he marino, he iti, kāore i pērā rawa te hōhonu.
He takotoranga wai tai, nā te matatāhuna, nā te pūkawa rānei i noho wehe ai i te moana.
He takotoranga whenua roroa, he whāiti, he puke e rārangi ana i ngā taha e rua, tērā tonu pea he awa e rere ana i waenganui.
He takotoranga whenua whāiti ka takahia e te waewae, ka haerea rānei e te waka, e tae atu ai te tangata, te aha atu ki wāhi kē.
He takutai me uaua ka ūngia e te waka.
He tama rongonui nā Ranginui rāua ko Papatūānuku, he atua; ko ia te kiko me ngā wheua o tōna whaea, ko tōna whakatinanatanga ko te aruhe me ngā kai tupu noa.
He tama rongonui nā Ranginui rāua ko Papatūānuku, he atua; ko ngā hau tōna whakatinanatanga.
He tama rongonui nā Ranginui rāua ko Papatūānuku, he atua; ko ngā ika tōna whakatinanatanga; he maha atu ōna ingoa hei tohu i ōna rohenga mana.
He tama rongonui nā Ranginui rāua ko Papatūānuku, he atua; ko tōna whakatinanatanga ko ngā mahi kino a te tangata ki te tangata pera i te kai tangata, te kōrero teka, te whānako me ngā mahi o tērā hanga; arā atu anō ōna ingoa e tohu ana i ōna rohenga mana.
He tama rongonui nā Ranginui rāua ko Papatūānuku, he atua; nāna ka puta te āio ki te whenua, ko te rongomau ki waenga i te tāngata; he maha atu ōna ingoa hei tohu i ōna rohenga mana.
He tama rongonui nā Ranginui rāua ko Papatūānuku, he atua; nāna ko te tutū o te puehu, ko te heke o te toto; he maha atu ōna ingoa hei tohu i ōna rohenga mana.
He tamaiti ahakoa tāne, ahakoa wahine rānei, ka whai muri iho i te mātāmua.
He tamaiti i ōna tau tuatahi ki tēnei ao, he tamaiti tino nohinohi.
He tamaiti ka whakatipungia e tētahi atu i tua atu i ōna mātua ake.
He tamaiti ko ia anake ka whānau mai i te whānautanga kotahi.
He tamaiti ko ia anake te hua a ōna mātua - kāore ōna tuākana, tēina, tungāne, tuāhine rānei.
He tamaiti kua mate ngā mātua.
He tamaiti kāore e tipu ki te rahi e tika ana, he iti te hanga, tērā anō pea he ngoikore.
He tamaiti, he tangata rānei e whai ana i te mātauranga i tētahi whare ako.
He tangata atu i te taraiwa, i te kaiurungi, ka haere i runga waka.
He tangata e arahina ana e tētahi atua, ka noho ia hei matakite, hei māngai mō taua atua, e pai ai tana ārahi, tana tohutohu i āna pononga.
He tangata e aroha nuitia ana, e tōreretia ana.
He tangata e hake ana te tuarā.
He tangata e hono ana ā-toto ki tētahi atu.
He tangata e kore e tini ngā ika ka mau i a ia.
He tangata e mōhio ana ki te kauhoe.
He tangata e mōhio pai ana koe, e tino rata ana koe, ā, ko ia e whakaaro pērā ana mōu (hāunga pea te hoa moe).
He tangata e noho ana i te taha o te moana.
He tangata e noho ana ko ia anake, ko tōna kotahi.
He tangata e noho wātea ana i te atua, i te wairua rānei, nāna ia i kōwhiri hei huarahi, hei reo, hei ringaringa, hei tinana mōna.
He tangata e ora ana i te aroha o ētahi atu, engari kāore ōna whakaaro ki te hunga aroha ki a ia.
He tangata e patupatua ana, e tūkinotia ana, kua murua rānei ana taonga, tana kāinga.
He tangata e reka ana, e ātaahua ana tana reo waiata, tana reo kōrero rānei.
He tangata e rua ōna pākanga, arā e heke mai ana ōna tātai i ngā tūpuna e rua; e taea ana te whakaheke mai i ōna whakapapa i ngā tūpuna e rua he iwi kē, he iwi kē.
He tangata e rua, neke atu rānei ngā iwi nō reira mai ōna tātai whakapapa.
He tangata e tauhou ana ki tētahi whenua, ki tētahi marae, ki tētahi wāhi rānei.
He tangata e tohunga ana ki te mahi i tētahi mahi ki ana ringaringa, he tere, he tau ki te mahi.
He tangata e whakapono ana, e whakaae ana, e tautoko ana i ngā whakaakoranga a tētahi atu.
He tangata eke hōiho, ko tāna mahi he ā haere, he tiaki i ngā kāhui kau.
He tangata haere noa, maewa noa ki hea, ki hea, kāore he kāinga tūturu.
He tangata haere noa, maewa noa ki hea, ki hea, kāore ōna kāinga tūturu, kāore e mahi ana, kāore rānei e hiahia ki te mahi.
He tangata hara kore; te hoa tauaro o te kupu 'whiro'.
He tangata he maha atu i te rua ōna pākanga, ōna tātai whakaheke; arā e taea ana te whakaheke mai i ngā mātua, tūpuna tokomaha; he tangata tuarā whānui i roto i te hapori, i te hapū, i te iwi.
He tangata he pūmanawa whakaharahara ōna ki tētahi kaupapa, ki ētahi kaupapa.
He tangata he ure tōna, māna rawa e hapū ai te wahine.
He tangata hīanga, he tangata whakatoi.
He tangata i noho i Iharaira e rua mano tau ki muri; te tama a te Atua ki te whakapono Karaitiana, nāna te whakapono Karaitiana i tīmata.
He tangata i roto i te pakiwaitara, i te whakaari, i te kiriata rānei.
He tangata i āta ākona ki ngā kōrero o te whare wānanga.
He tangata ka eke ki te tūranga o tētahi kua whakawātea i taua tūranga, ka ngaro rānei i taua tūranga mō tētahi wā.
He tangata ka hoko rawa, ka hoko ratonga rānei mai i te whare hoko, i te pakihi rānei.
He tangata ka hopukina, ka puritia e ōna hoariri i te wā o te pakanga.
He tangata ka karo, ka oma rānei i tētahi āhuatanga wehi, i tētahi mahi uaua rānei, i te mea he mataku, he māia kore.
He tangata ka mahi i runga i te aroha ki te tangata, ki te kaupapa rānei.
He tangata ka mate i tētahi āhuatanga, ka patua rānei kia mate.
He tangata ka mauheretia e te ture he mahi kino nōna, e whakapaetia ana rānei kua mahi kino.
He tangata ka noho hei karere i waenga i te tokorua e whaiāipo ana.
He tangata ka noho tahi ki te rangatira ki te āwhina i a ia, hei whakawhirinakitanga rānei mōna; he tangata noho tahi ki tētahi atu, ka utua kia mahi i ngā mahi o te kāinga.
He tangata ka patapatai ā-waha i tētahi atu e riro mai ai ngā tūmomo kōrero e whāia ana, e hiahiatia ana.
He tangata ka patua hei whakarata i a Tangaroa.
He tangata ka patua kia whai mana ai te tānga o ngā ngutu o te wahine.
He tangata ka pīkau i ngā mahi a tētahi e ngaro ana i te mahi; tētahi atu hanga rānei koinei tana āhua.
He tangata ka riro māna e kōrero, e kōkiri tētahi kaupapa mā tētahi rōpū.
He tangata ka taea e ia te whānau uri; he rākau ka whai kākano. Arā te kupu tauaro, ko te 'tāne'.
He tangata ka taumaha te takahi o te waewae ina haere mā raro.
He tangata ka tiaki i ngā tuhinga kōrero, i ngā kaute o te tari, me te mahi anō pea i ētahi atu mahi o te tari e pērā ana te āhua.
He tangata ka tohutohu, ka tāpae whakaaro ki te aroaro o tētahi atu, hei ārahi, hei āwhina i a ia.
He tangata ka tonoa hei āta kawe i ngā kōrero whai tikanga i waenga i ētahi tāngata, i ētahi rōpū.
He tangata ka tukuna ki whenua kē ki te kauhau i te whakapono, e tahuri ai ngā tāngata o reira ki taua whakapono.
He tangata ka tunu kai, ka taka kai mā ētahi atu.
He tangata ka tū i waenganui i tētahi tokorua, i ētahi taha e rua rānei ki te kimi huarahi e tatū pai ai tētahi tautohetohe.
He tangata ka tū ki te kōrero i tētahi huihuinga nui pērā i te tangihanga, he tohunga ki te tārai kupu, he hōhonu, he ngahau rānei ana kōrero.
He tangata ka tū ki te kōrero, ki te whaikōrero, i tētahi huihuinga tāngata.
He tangata ka utua e tētahi atu ki te whakapai whare, ki te tunu kai, ki te horoi kākahu me ērā tūmomo mahi.
He tangata ka utua ki te mahi i ētahi mahi o te tari pērā i te tiaki i te kiripaepae, te whakautu waea, te patopato reta, te whakarite hui, te tuhi i ngā kōrero o ngā hui, te aha atu, te aha atu.
He tangata ka utua ki te mahi i ētahi mahi.
He tangata ka whakaaraara i te pā, ko ia ngā kanohi o te iwi, waihoki he tangata ka haere ki te titiro i te kaha o te hoariri.
He tangata ka whakanohongia hei kaiwhakahaere mō tētahi whenua kei raro i te mana whakahaere o whenua kē.
He tangata ka whakawhiti mai i tētahi ope ki tētahi, i tētahi rōpū ki tētahi, he kawe kōrero te mahi.
He tangata ka āta romiromi, ka āta mirimiri, ka āta kukume rānei i ngā wāhanga o te tinana e mate ana, e mamae ana, kia pai ake ai.
He tangata ka āta tautoko, ka āwhina i te hoariri i roto i te pakanga, he tangata rānei kāore e tautoko, e āwhina i āna ake.
He tangata ka āwhina i tētahi atu, i tētahi kaupapa rānei.
He tangata karo mahi, he māngere.
He tangata kawe i te kōrero kino kia heke ai te mana o te tangata, o te kaupapa, he kaha ki te whakahāwea i tētahi atu.
He tangata kei a ia te mana ki te whakatau mehemea e ū ana ngā kaitākaro o tētahi tākaro ki ngā ture o taua tākaro.
He tangata kei a ia ētahi pūkenga, ētahi mātauranga hōhonu e pā ana ki tētahi kaupapa.

He tangata ko te kai tōna atua, arā, ahakoa pēhea te kai, kāore rawa e ngata te hiahia.
He tangata ko tāna mahi he hanga whare, he whakatikatika rānei i te hanga o te whare.
He tangata ko tāna mahi he rūri i te whenua.
He tangata ko tāna mahi he taka, he tohatoha, he hoko rongoā ki te iwi tūmatanui; te wāhi e hokona ai ēnei rongoā.
He tangata ko tāna mahi, he āta whāngai i te ākonga ki te mātauranga.
He tangata kore mana ka mauheretia hei kaimahi mā tētahi atu.

He tangata kua hono atu, kua uru atu ki tētahi rōpū.

He tangata kua ngoikore, kua hauā rānei i tētahi mate, i tētahi aituā, tērā pea e riro ana mā tētahi atu e tiaki.
He tangata kua oti te whakaako, kua āta whakatapua hei whakahaere i ngā mahi tapu me ngā karakia a ngā hāhi Karaitiana.
He tangata kua piki ake i te taumata ki te tāura, tērā pea ka noho ia hei kaiāwhina mō te tohunga tūāhu, mō te tohunga taua rānei.
He tangata kua piki ki te whai i te taumata tuarua o ngā āhuatanga o te kauae runga, e whakaakona ana e te tohunga.

He tangata kua tāia katoatia te mata.
He tangata kua tū i te rākau whawhai, i te kariri rānei.
He tangata kua whai i ngā akoranga e tika ana hei whakahaere karakia i ngā hāhi Karaitiana, hāunga anō te Hāhi Katorika ki ētahi; ka kawe i ngā mahi a tēnei tangata.
He tangata kua whai i te tohu mātauranga e rite ana mō te rongoā i te kararehe e mate ana, kua whara rānei.
He tangata kua whai i te tohu mātauranga e rite ana mō te rongoā i te tangata.
He tangata kua whai i te tohu mātauranga e rite ana mō te tiaki me te whakatikatika niho.
He tangata kua whiwhi i te tohu mātauranga tiketike rawa o tētahi whare wānanga.
He tangata kua āta tohua māna e tiaki tētahi wāhi, tētahi mea rānei, māna rānei e ārahi te tutukinga pai o tētahi kaupapa.
He tangata kua āta whakaakona ki te tiaki i te tūroro, i te hunga tārutu.
He tangata kua āta whakaakona ki te tiaki, ki te āwhina i te wahine whakawhānau.
He tangata kāore e aro ake, e whakarongo ki ngā whakaaro, ki ngā tohutohu a tētahi atu, ka ū tonu ki tāna ahakoa pēhea.
He tangata kāore e mōhio ki te kauhoe.
He tangata kāore e mōhiotia ana, he tangata rānei kua tatū mai i whenua kē, i iwi kē, he rāwaho.
He tangata kāore e pai ki te titiro atu, i te kore e pai o te āhua.
He tangata kāore e paingia e tāna e whai ana hei wahine, hei tāne rānei māna.
He tangata kāore e taunga ana ki te taiao kua uru atu a ia.
He tangata kāore e tātāwhi i ana whakaaro, kāore e aro ki te hā o tētahi atu.
He tangata kāore e whakaaro, kāore rānei e mātau ki te mahi tika.
He tangata kāore i heke mai i ngā kāwai rangatira.
He tangata kāore i mana te moe a ōna mātua i tōna whānautanga mai.
He tangata kāore i tika te tupu, kāore i pai te tupu, kua kore e eke ki te rahi e tika ana.
He tangata kāore ōna toto Māori, nō iwi kē, nō whenua kē.
He tangata kātahi tonu ka tīmata te ako i ngā āhuatanga o te kauwae runga, e whakaakohia ana e te tohunga.
He tangata kōrero parau, kōrero rūkahu.
He tangata mahi kino.
He tangata matapiko.
He tangata me pātai rawa ko wai ōna tūpuna, i te mea kāore ia e mōhiotia ana, kāore ōna mana.

He tangata māngere.
He tangata mātau ki ētahi āhuatanga, ko tāna mahi he āwhina i te kaiwhakawā kia tika ai tāna whakatau.
He tangata mātau, otirā he nanakia, he rauhanga.
He tangata mōhio, he tangata whai pūkenga ahurei ki tētahi āhuatanga.
He tangata nui te mana, he tangata whakahirahira.
He tangata nō ngā iwi e rua ka whawhai mō tētahi o aua iwi, kātahi ka whawhai mō tērā atu iwi.
He tangata nō ngā iwi e rua, arā nō ngā iwi e rua ōna whakapapa.
He tangata nō waho atu o te iwi, o te whenua, o te whakahaere, o te aha rānei.
He tangata nō wāhi kē e haere rēhia ana i tētahi whenua ki te tirotiro noa.

He tangata patipati, he tangata nukarau, kāore i pono.

He tangata pūmanawa nui, he rehe, he tangata rānei kua puta tōna rongo.
He tangata rahi ngā taringa.
He tangata tahanga.
He tangata tiaki hipi.
He tangata tino kaha ki te kōrero me te whakaputa mōhio hoki.

He tangata toha kai, toha inu, āwhina hoki i ngā pāhihi i runga waka rererangi, waka moana rānei.
He tangata whai tohu mātauranga ture, ko tāna he tohutohu i te tangata ki te ture, he tū anō hei waha kōrero mō te tangata i roto i ngā whakawākanga.
He tangata whai tūranga i roto i tētahi rōpū, pēnei i te kāwanatanga, i te ope hōia, i tētahi kamupene rānei.
He tangata whakakatakata, whakangahau i te whakaminenga, tērā ka kuhuna e ia he kākahu rerekē me te pani i tana kanohi.
He tangata whakaora i ngā momo māuiui o te wairua o te tangata, he kawe anō hoki i ngā mahi e whakaatungia ana ki a ia e te taha wairua.
He tangata whakauru atu i tōna ihu ki ngā take a ētahi atu, ki reira whakaputa mōhio ai, whakararu ai.
He tangata whawhai ki uta nō te ope taua nui tonu o tētahi iwi, o tētahi whenua rānei.
He tangata whenua nō Aotearoa, tērā tonu ka hoki ōna whakapapa ki tētahi o ngā tūpuna o runga i ngā waka i heke mai i te hekenga nui.
He tangata whenua nō Rēkohu, ka hoki ōna whakapapa ki tētahi o ngā tūpuna o te hekenga ki ērā moutere.
He tangata whānako.
He tangata, he aha atu ko ia te huarahi, te reo, te ringaringa, te tinana rānei o tētahi wairua, o tētahi atua.
He tangata, he aha atu kua tapaina ki tētahi atu, e rite ana rānei ngā ingoa.
He tangata, he aha atu rānei e toheriri ana ki tētahi atu, ko te hiahia ia kia hinga, kia mate atu rānei i a ia.
He tangata, he aha atu rānei ko ia te huarahi o tētahi atua.
He tangata, he hanga rānei e kai kino ana te aroha mōna.
He tangata, he huinga tāngata rānei ka whawhai tahi me tētahi atu, ka tautoko rānei i tētahi atu.
He tangata, he kararehe rānei e iti noa ake ana tana tupu i tērā e tika ana.
He tangata, he kararehe rānei e mā ana te kiri, ngā makawe, ngā huruhuru, me te māwhero anō pea o ngā karu; he āhuatanga whakaheke.
He tangata, he kararehe, he aha atu rānei ka heke mai i tētahi tupuna.
He tangata, he mahi koia te aronga o te kohimu, o te heitara.
He tangata, he mea rānei e tohu tōmua ana i te taenga mai, i te ekenga rānei o tētahi atu mea.
He tangata, he mea rānei ko ia e whakatauira ana i tētahi karangatanga, ko ia te whakatinanatanga o tētahi karangatanga.
He tangata, he mea, he āhuatanga rānei ka whakahōhā, ka whakararu i te wairua, i te ngākau.
He tangata, he rōpū rānei ka āta toro i tētahi atu, ka noho ki raro i ngā manaakitanga a tāna e toro rā.
He tangata, he tikanga, he aha atu ka whāia, ka tāwhaitia e te tangata.
He tangata, he tāngata ka kōhuru i te pō.
He tangata, he tāngata rānei ko rātou anahe ngā kanohi ora o tētahi iwi, o tētahi whakatupuranga, o tētahi pakanga, o tētahi atu karangatanga rānei.
He tangata, he tāngata rānei ko rātou te whakamutunga o tētahi whakatupuranga e ora tonu ana.
He tangata, he wāhi, he mea rānei kua whakatauiratia tōna pai, tōna mana ki te pepeha.
He tangata, he ārai, he aha atu hei tiaki, hei whakamarumaru i tētahi mea.
He taniwha horo waka kei te aumoana tōna rua, mā te tohunga rawa e whakaoho, e whakarata, e whakatau.
He taniwha weriweri, he taniwha whakamataku, he taniwha kai tangata, he auau pērā i te kurī, he noho wai engari he haere anō i raro i te whenua.
He taniwha weriweri, he taniwha whakamataku, he taniwha whakatūpato.
He tao ka whiua ki te hoariri e whakatata mai ana, he wero, he tohu hoki.
He tao ka whiua ki te ringa.
He tao kāore anō i oti te hanga.
He tao maha e rere tahi ana.
He tao poto, he koi ngā pito e rua.
He tao whawhai e 5 ki te 8 mita te roa, he koi a mua, he pūreke ka pūtoia ki te waero kei muri, kia whawhai i te pā ka taea e te tangata kotahi te kōkiri, kia whawhai ki waho, kia rua rawa. Ko te pae ki mua, ko te kaikōkiri ki muri. He rākau tēnei e werohia ai te hoariri.
He tao whawhai e taea ana tōna mata te tango mai.
He taonga ka puritia hei whakamaharatanga ki te tangata nāna i hoatu ki a koe, nāna ake rānei te taonga.
He taonga ka tukua, he kōrero ka whakapuakina, he waiata rānei ka waiatatia hei tohu ki ngā iwi e rata mai ana, e kimihia ana he āwhina i a rātou mō te haere ki tētahi pakanga.
He taonga ka tāraia ki te pounamu.
He taonga matakite i mahia ki te tā toetoe, ki tētahi tipu pērā rānei, ka rākaitia ki te rau rangiora, kātahi ka whiua mai i tētahi wāhi teitei ki te whakaatu mai i ōna tohu.
He taonga niho whāiti hei whakamatara, hei whakapaipai i ngā makawe.
He taonga papatahi iti ka hangaia ki te maitai, he kupu he whakairo rānei kei runga, hei tohu i te toa o te tangata ki tētahi mahi, hei whakanui rānei i tētahi āhuatanga kua pā.
He taonga pounamu e rite ana tētahi pito ki te pito o te whao.
He taonga puoro e ono, tekau mā rua rānei ngā aho, he kakī roa tōna, ka tākirikiritia, ka pākia tahitia rānei ngā aho e puta ai he oro.
He taonga puoro e whā ngā aho, he tinana hahao whai hope tōna, he puare oro kei ia taha o te tinana he 'f' te āhua, ka mukua ngā aho ki tētahi momo rākau kia tangi ai.
He taonga puoro he whānui te pito whakarunga, he whāiti te pito whakararo, kotahi te wenewene kei waenganui tonu o tōna whāroa. He reo wahine tōna, he reo tāne tōna. E tangi ai tōna reo wahine ka pūhia te pito whakarunga mai i te taha, ka pūhia rānei me te noho mai o tōna ngutu ki te kauae. Ko tōna reo tāne ka rangona ina pūhia pērā i te pūkaea.
He taonga puoro hei whakaaraara i te iwi, e toru ki te ono putu te roa, he whara nui, arā he waha nui tōna, i hangā ki te tōtara ki te mataī rānei, he tohe kei te whara.
He taonga puoro ka hangaia ki te hue iti, ka pūhia ki te pongāihu; ka tapahia atu te kakī o te hue, e rua ngā wenewene ka mahia ki ngā wāhi o te taonga e pai ai mō ngā mati o te kaipupuhi.
He taonga puoro ka hangā ki te rākau, ki te wheua, ki te anga rānei, e rua ka tukia tahitia kia mau ai te manawataki o te waiata.
He taonga puoro ka hangā ki te tātara, ka mahia anō he ngutu rākau ki ētahi.
He taonga puoro ka kumea whakawahotia, ka pēhia whakarototia me te pēpēhi anō i ngā pātene o tētahi taha, o tētahi taha kia tangi ai.
He taonga puoro ka mahia ki te anga, ko te tuki roa ka whakairohia ki rākau.
He taonga puoro ka mahia ki te pūtātara, he tuki whakairo anō tōna.
He taonga puoro ka purua, ka taupokina rānei tētahi pito, kotahi te wenewene pupuhi kei te pito whakarunga, e toru ngā wenewene hei pokipoki kei te pito whakararo.
He taonga puoro ka whakatangihia mā te pupuhi whakaroto, whakapae rānei i te ngutu, me te āta pokipoki anō ngā wenewene.
He taonga puoro kotahi te aho, ka paopaongia te aho ki te rākau e tangi ai.
He taonga puoro rite ki te kōauau roa engari kei te pito whakararo ngā wenewene.
He taonga puoro, arā he maramara rākau whāiti, he pāraharaha, ka tākirihia kia tōiri ai.
He taonga puoro, he momo pū, ka hangaia ki te wheua, ki te rākau, ki te kōhatu, ki te rimurimu rānei, e toru, e rima rānei ngā wenewene, he taonga tēnei ka pūhia ki te waha.
He taonga rite ki te oko ka hangā ki te hiriwa, ki te kōura rānei, kotahi tōna waewae, tērā pea he kakau kei ia taha, he taonga ka whakawhiwhia ki te toa o tētahi whakataetae, o tētahi āhuatanga rānei.
He taonga tākaro e herea ai ētahi taura ki tētahi takaore kei runga i tētahi pou, ka mau te tangata ki te taura, kātahi ka oma kia rere ai ki te takiwā.
He taonga tākaro hanga rite ki te neti ka whakaripihia ki te papa.
He taonga tākaro i mahia nuitia ki te kākaka, ka takaia tētahi pito ki te harakeke kia noho mai ai he pōike, koinei te pito whakamua; ka ahuahua he puke ki tētahi wāhi, kātahi ka whiua te taonga nei mai i tawhiti kia ripi atu ai i te puke, kia rere anō ki te rangi, kia tau atu ki tawhiti.
He taonga tākaro ka hangā ki te rākau, he whāiti he pāraharaha, he pororapa te rau, ka whakamaua he here ki tētahi pito, ka herea atu he kakau ki tērā. Ka mau te ringa ki te kakau, kātahi ka piua haeretia ki runga ake i te upoko, ka kaha ake te piu, ka kaha ake te rorohū o te taonga nei.
He taonga tākaro nā te tamariki. Ka mahia he porotiti tipirori ki te rākau, kātahi ka pokaina ētahi kōhao e rua ki waenganui. Ka kauia he aho ki ngā kōhao, ka herea. Ka kuhuna atu ngā kōnui tētahi ki tētahi pito o te aho, tētahi ki tētahi, ka hurihuri, ka kukume kia tāwhirowhiro ai te porotiti, kia hū, kia wheowheo.
He taonga tākaro porohita te hanga ka mahia ki te aka, ki te kareao hei patu mā tētahi ki tētahi atu.
He taonga tākaro porotaka, he iti tonu, he māeneene, ka hangaia ki te karaehe, ka perea ki ngā matimati.
He taonga tākaro rite ki te manu te hanga, he whai anga māmā ka uhia ki te raupō, ki te pepa, ki te aha atu, he aho roa tōna ka mau tētahi pito ki te ringa, ka tukua kia rere rā runga hau.
He taonga tākaro rite ki te tangata te hanga, i mahia ki te rākau, he kakau kei raro iho i ngā waewae hei puritanga, ko ngā ringa i mahia motuhaketia, ka honoa atu i ngā pakihiwi ki te aho, ka herea ngā aho ki muri i te hope; he taonga tākaro ka whakakorihia ētahi wāhanga o te tinana hei whakaari kōrero.
He taonga tākaro, arā he taura whai pona, whai nohoanga ka iri mai i te rākau, i hea ake, e rere ai te kaieke ki mua, ki muri, ki mua, ki muri.
He taonga tākaro, he taonga matakite rānei i mahia ki te rau o te whārangi me te tā otaota pērā i te kāretu; ka werohia te tā o te kāretu ki te tātā o te rau o te whārangi, ka tukua kia rere mai i tētahi wāhi teitei.
He taonga whakapaipai ka tāheia ki te kakī.
He taonga whakapaipai ka whakamaua ki te taringa.
He taonga whakapaipai mō te taringa.
He taonga, he tangata, he aha atu rānei ko ia e kaha tautoko ana, e whakakaha ana i tētahi atu mea, ko ia tōna oranga.
He taonga, he āhuatanga, he aha atu rānei kei tēnei ao e mōhio nei tātou; koia anō te kupu ka whakamahia hei tohu i tērā kāore e taea ana e te kaikōrero te āta whakaingoa, hei aha noa iho rānei te whakaingoa.
He taotū ā-kiko noa nei.
He tapawhā e whā ōna koki hāngai.
He tapawhā he ōrite te roa o ōna tapa e whā, e whā anō ōna koki hāngai.
He tapawhā rite he whāiti ētahi o ōna koki tauaro e rua, he whānui ētahi.
He taputapu ahuwhenua hei wāwāhi paioneone.
He taputapu ahuwhenua whai mata koi ka kumea haerehia ki te tapahi, ki te huripoki i te whenua, kia rite ai mō te whakatō purapura.
He taputapu e kitea ai ngā mea tino moroiti nei te hanga.
He taputapu e māmā ake ai te kite i ngā mea noho tawhiti, pēnei i te whetū.
He taputapu e mōhio ai koe e ahu pēhea ana koe, he ngira autō tōna ka tohu tonu ki te raki.
He taputapu haehae i mahia ki te niho mangō, ki te pāra matā rānei i herea ki tētahi kakau.
He taputapu hei hopu i te āhua o tētahi mea e puta ai he whakaahua, he kiriata, he ataata rānei.
He taputapu hei hopu kiore, hei hopu manu rere kore pērā i te weka rānei.
He taputapu hei hopu kāhu.
He taputapu hei hopu manu iti pērā i te koreke, i te karuwai, i te miromiro. Ka mahia ki te kareao me te rākau, ko te mata ka mahia ki te harakeke, he aho roa anō tōna. Ka whakatūria te taputapu nei ki te ara manu, ka hoatu he poa ki mua, ina kainga te poa e te manu, kua kumea te aho, kua taupokina te manu, kua mau.
He taputapu hei hopu manu rere kore, arā he tāwhiti e whā, ka tapawhā te whakanoho mai ki te whenua.
He taputapu hei hopu tuna.
He taputapu hei kari aruhe, hei tāmata hoki i te oneone.
He taputapu hei kawe i te tangata, i te tūroro, i te tūpāpaku, i tētahi atu mea rānei.
He taputapu hei kawe i te tangata.
He taputapu hei kawe kākahu, aha atu rānei, he whai kīwei, tērā tonu he taupoki whai kauhuri tōna, he waha nui rānei e taea ana kati.
He taputapu hei keri i te māra.
He taputapu hei kohi tuangi.
He taputapu hei koko i te oneone, he āhua rite ki te tīheru te hanga.
He taputapu hei kōutu i te wai i te riu o te waka.
He taputapu hei mahi kōhao ki tētahi mea pērā i te pounamu.
He taputapu hei paopao ka puritia ki te ringa.
He taputapu hei pupuri wai, hei pupuri aha atu.
He taputapu hei pāpako i te oneone i mahia ki te rākau tokorera, ko tētahi taha hei pupuri mā ngā ringa, ko tētahi taha he pāraharaha, he rau.
He taputapu hei tapahi mai i ngā huruhuru o te kanohi, o tētahi wāhi rānei o te tinana.
He taputapu hei tapahi rākau, wahie, aha atu, arā, he upoko koi, he taumaha anō, kua whakamaua ki te kakau.
He taputapu hei titi ake i te kai, hei kawe i te kai ki te waha.
He taputapu hei tākiri ake i te pere, arā, he rākau kua herea atu he taura ki tētahi pito.
He taputapu hei tāmata i te māra.
He taputapu hei tārai rākau, arā, he mata kōhatu, he mata anga mātaitai rānei kua herea ki te kakau.
He taputapu hei whakaatu i te takanga o ngā hāora o te rā, ka iri mai ki te pakitara, ka tū motuhake rānei ki tētahi wāhi.
He taputapu hei whakaatu i te takanga o ngā hāora o te rā, ka whakamaua ki te kawititanga o te ringa.
He taputapu hei whakahaere, hei kati atu rānei i te rere o te wai, o te haurehu rānei ka puta i tētahi pū.
He taputapu hei whakapā atu ki te tangata kia pai ai te kōrero ki a ia mai i tawhiti; te hononga e taea ai tēnei mahi.
He taputapu hopu ika, he taputapu rānei hei rau atu i te ika.
He taputapu hopu ika, ka whatua tōna raumata ki ōna momo aho anō; he taputapu whai raumata hei hopu i te manu, i te aha atu.
He taputapu hopu kiore i mahia ki te ara kiore, e whā ōna māhanga.
He taputapu hopu kiore i whakatakotoria ki ngā wāhi ngahoro ai te hīnau, te miro, te tawai, te patatē, me ētahi atu hua i kainga e te kiore.
He taputapu hopu kiore.
He taputapu hopu manu ka horahia ki waenganui i ētahi rākau.
He taputapu hopu tuna hanga kōrere te āhua, ka hoatu he mōunu ki roto ki te poapoa mai i ngā tuna.
He taputapu hākinakina taumaha porohita te hanga, ko te whāinga a te kaitākaro he maka ki tawhiti.
He taputapu i hangā ki te kōhatu hei paopao muka kia ngāwari ai.
He taputapu i mahia ki te kareao, ki te aha atu, hei kaupare i te weronga mai a te tao i te whakatatanga atu ki ngā maioro o te pā.
He taputapu i mahia ki te kōhatu, ki te rākau rānei ka paoa hei whakaara i te iwi i ngā wā o te pakanga.
He taputapu iti motuhake tōna āhua ka hangā ki tētahi momo maitai, ka kuhuna atu ki tōna anō raka, ka hurihia kia huaki mai, kia raka rānei tētahi mea, kia haruru mai, kia weto rānei tētahi mea, kia haere tonu ai rānei tētahi mea. Arā atu anō āna mahi.
He taputapu ka hangaia hei pae noho mō te tou o te tangata.
He taputapu ka hangaia ki te rino.
He taputapu ka mahia ki te rākau, he poroharore tētahi pito, he taputapu hei paopao aruhe, hei paopao aha atu.
He taputapu ka puritia ki te ringa, he mata rino, he mata papatahi tōna ka whakawerangia hei whakaene, hei whakakore i ngā kopakopa i te kākahu, i te aha atu.
He taputapu ka riro mā te pūhiko rawa e puta ai tōna aho, ka kawea haeretia kia kite pai ai ngā karu i te pōuri.
He taputapu ka whakamahia i te whawhai, i te riri.
He taputapu kakau roa hei kari, hei ope i tētahi mea, he whānui te mata, he piko whakarunga ngā taha.
He taputapu kakau roa hei keri, hei ahu whenua, hei koko rānei; he whānui tonu te mata, he hakoko, ka koeko haere te pito.
He taputapu kirihou he porohita te hanga, he tino angiangi, 12 henimita iti ake rānei te whitianga, whakamahia ai hei pupuri i te puoro, i te kōrero, i te whakaahua, i te aha atu rānei hei whakatangi, hei whakaata ā tōna wā.
He taputapu maitai e taea ai te peru o tētahi pine te huri, te whakatangatanga, te whakakikī rānei.
He taputapu māra he kakau roa tōna, he maitai koi kei tētahi pito hei heu ake i ngā taru.
He taputapu mō te pere kōhatu. Ko te taputapu nei he rākau ka poua ki te whenua, he aho kei te pito hei kukume whakamuri mā tētahi o ngā tāngata e pere kōhatu ana. Ka pupurihia te kōhatu e tana hoa ki te rākau, kātahi ka tukua te aho, rere ana te kōhatu ki tawhiti.
He taputapu mō te tapahi mea pērā i te papanga, i te pepa, i te makawe, e rua ōna rau ka kaurori i waenganui, e whakamahia ai, ka kuhuna atu te kōnui ki te mōwhiti kei te pito o tētahi o ngā rau, ko te kōroa ki te mōwhiti i tētahi atu.
He taputapu ngaki māra, he rite ki te hoe pakupaku, he āhua koi te pito hei pāpako i te oneone, hei hauhake rānei i te kūmara, i te taewa.
He taputapu paopao, he pane taumaha tōna ka mahia nuitia ki te maitai.
He taputapu porohita te hanga i mahia ki te kareao, ki te mānuka rānei, hei hopu kōura.
He taputapu pouaka te hanga hei rokiroki i te kai, ka noho rawa te pāmahana o roto ki raro i te pae whakatoka.
He taputapu pouaka te hanga hei whakamātao i te kai, i te inu, mā te hiko rawa e noho mātao tonu ai a roto.
He taputapu pouaka te hanga hei whakamātao i te kai.
He taputapu pupuri wai, pupuri kai rānei ka tāraia ki te rākau, he porowhita te hanga, he nui atu te waha i te tou.
He taputapu rau maitai angiangi whai niho, hei tapahi rākau me ētahi atu hanga mārō tonu.
He taputapu rite ki te pona e hono ana i ētahi wāhanga e rua, e taea ai tētahi mea (pērā i te kūwaha, i te taupoki) te huaki, te kati; he hanga pēnei e hono ana i ngā wāhanga e rua o ētahi mātaitai pērā i te pipi, i te tuangi.
He taputapu roa hei wāwāhi i te oneone, he koi te pito ngau ki te oneone, he hamaruru hei takahi atu mā te waewae kei runga paku atu i te koinga; he rākau whawhai anō hoki i ōna wā.
He taputapu tahu kai ka whakawerahia ki te hiko, ki te kapuni, ki te waro, ki te wahie rānei.
He taputapu tā moko ka mahia ki te kōiwi toroa.
He taputapu tākaro, he teitei tētahi pito, he māeneene, he rōnaki te mata hei rerenga iho mā te tamariki.
He taputapu whai kakau roa hei keri, hei ahu whenua, he papatahi te mata; i ngā rā o mua i mahia ki te rākau, i ēnei rā ka mahia ki te maitai.
He taputapu whai kakau roa hei tahitahi i te papa, kua whakamaua atu he hanga pērā i te tā, i te rārā tipu kua paiheretia ki te pito, he hanga mārō rānei kua titia ki te wanawana.
He taputapu whai kakau, he arearenga pāpaku kei te pito, he taputapu hei whāngai kai ki te waha, hei tohatoha, hei kōrorirori kai, hei aha atu, hei aha atu.
He taputapu whai kakau, he kakau tonu rānei kua whakamaua atu ētahi hanga pērā i te huruhuru, i te wanawana, i te waea, hei peita, hei ūkui paru, hei whakapai makawe, hei aha atu.
He taputapu whai kakau, he rau maitai tōna, he whāiti te pito hei huri i te kōwiri.
He taputapu whai koromāhanga hei hopu kererū.
He taputapu whai koromāhanga hei hopu manu.
He taputapu whai rau roa he hema te pito ngau, ka patokia ki te kuru e whakairohia ai te rākau, te kōhatu, te kōiwi, te aha atu.
He taputapu whai wāhanga nekeneke ka whakaharurutia, ka whakahaeretia rānei ki te mahi i tētahi mahi.
He taputapu whakaputa oro tīkā hei tuku tohu ki te tangata, ki te kararehe rānei.
He taputapu whāiti ka hangaia ki te rākau ki te maitai rānei, hei hiki, hei neke rānei i tētahi mea. Ka poua atu tētahi pito ki raro i te mea e nekehia ana, ka pēhia whakararotia kia neke ai.
He taputapu, arā, he rākau tokomanga whai reke ka whakawiria kia kikī ai ngā aukaha o te waka.
He taputapu, he mīhini rānei ka hurihuri te mata ki te  mahi kōhao.
He taputapu, he rākau whawhai rānei i hangā ki te pakohe.
He tara koi ka hoki paku ake i te koinga o te matau, o te tao, o te aha atu e uaua ai te tango mai ina titi ki tētahi mea.
He tarawhiti māna e puare ai te waha o te kupenga ā-ringa, o te aha atu rānei.
He tau e taea ana te wehe pū ki te rua, arā, kāore he toenga.
He tau kāore e nui te hua, te kai.
He tau kāore e taea te wehe pū ki te rua, arā, ahakoa pēhea, he 1 ka toe mai.
He tau nui, e rite ana ki ngā rau tekau, ko te 1,000 tōna tohutau.
He tau nui, tekau ngā tekau, ko te 100 tōna tohutau.
He tau tino nui, ko te 1,000,000 tōna tohutau.
He tau, he tapeke, he tātaitanga tāpiri rānei.
He taua kua āta whakarārangi mai i a rātou kia rite ai mō te whawhai.
He taua whakaeke.
He tauhou, he tangata nō whenua kē.
He tauihu kua whakairoa ki te pītau.
He tauihu whakairo, ko ngā ringa o te whakapakoko ka toro whakamuri.
He tauira e ako ana i ngā āhuatanga o te kauwae runga.
He tauira e koki haere ai he rārangi, he tāhei rānei ki matau, ki mauī, ki matau, ki mauī.
He tauira e rite ana ki te pātiki ka mahia ki ngā mahi raranga, ki te tukutuku, ki te kōwhaiwhai me ētahi atu wāhi.
He tauira e whai ana i te pākati kōpikopiko o te whakairo, hei whakarākei i te raranga, i te whatu, i te tukutuku.
He tauira i te mahi whakairo.
He tauira i te tukutuku, i te kōwhaiwhai, i te aha atu e whakatauira ana i te āhua o te rara, o te kēkē.
He tauira kāniwha i ngā mahi whakairo, ka takoto i waenga patapata.
He tauira kōwhaiwhai e rite ana te āhua ki te ngaru, he tohu nō te toa, nō tōna tere.
He tauira kōwhaiwhai e whakaahua ana i ngā rau o te tawa.
He tauira kōwhaiwhai e whakaahua ana i te upoko o te mangō pare.
He tauira kōwhaiwhai ka peitatia atu ki ngā heke o te wharenui.
He tauira kōwhaiwhai.
He tauira mō te raranga, te whatu, te tāniko me te tukutuku.
He tauira pākati e whakaahua ana i ngā huruhuru ka tū mai i te tuarā o te kurī.
He tauira pūmau ka tāia ki te kiri.
He tauira raranga ka hoatu ki te whāriki, te kete me te tātua.
He tauira raranga whāriki.
He tauira raranga, he tauira whatu, he tauira tukutuku, he pātikitiki te hanga.
He tauira tongi ka tuhia ki te kanohi.
He tauira tukutuku e rite ana ki te taimana te āhua, e whakaahua ana i te pātiki.
He tauira tukutuku e whakaahua ana i te au mārō o te toa i taotū ki te takiwā o tana pito.
He tauira tukutuku e whakaahua ana i te tini whetū.
He tauira tukutuku he rite te āhua ki te tauira purapura whetū, ki te pūkanohi rānei.
He tauira tukutuku mō ngā whakapaipai o roto i te whare, e tohu ana i ngā roimata o te toroa.
He tauira tukutuku rite ki te koinga o te pere te āhua.
He tauira tukutuku, he tauira whakairo e whakaahua ana i te tapuwae o te pūkeko.
He tauira tukutuku, raranga whāriki, he arawhata nei te āhua.
He tauira tānga moko onamata i āhua rite ki te mahi raranga ki te titiro atu, he mea mahi kia kapi katoa te tinana.
He tauira whai he rite te āhua ki te waka.
He tauira whai rite ki te whare.
He tauira whai, e rua ngā kaikori, 12 ngā whiringa ka hua ake i waenganui ko te ara e piki ai a Tāwhaki ki te rangi, e waru atu ngā tauira ka hua mai i tēnei.
He tauira whai, e whā ngā taimana, ko ngā taimana e rua o waenganui he whāiti.
He tauira whakairo e noho mai ai he rārangi pākati.
He tauira whakairo e noho tāpua mai ana ngā taka; he pākati rānei e hohoko tahi ana ki te haehae.
He tauira whakairo e rite ana ki te māwhaiwhai o te pūngāwerewere.

He tauira whakairo hei whakapaipai i ngā tokotoko o te tatau o te whare.

He tauira whakairo ka kīia ko te pākati kōpikopiko, kitea nuitia ai i ngā whakairo o te pātaka.

He tauārai ka whakatūria hei karapoti i ētahi mea, hei roherohe rānei i te whenua. Ka hangā te nuinga ki ētahi pou maha kua honoa ki te papa, ki te waea rānei.
He tauārai ka whakatūria hei karapoti i ētahi mea, hei wehe rānei i tētahi wāhanga o te whenua i tētahi atu. Ka hangaia te nuinga ki te kōhatu, ki te porokere, ki tētahi atu rawa papatipu rānei.

He tikanga e hopukia ai, e tāruatia ai, e pāhotia ai rānei he raupapa āhua nekeneke ki te rīpene, mai i te rīpene rānei; he kiriata, ētahi atu kōrero rānei e mau ana ki tēnei momo rīpene.
He tikanga e kore ai e taea ētahi āhuatanga te mahi.

He tinana kore māhunga.

He tipu 1 mita te tupu, he hūmekemeke, he nui tonu ngā rau, he pūtaratara ngā tapa, he niho roa tonu kei ngā tapa, he kahurangi ngā pua, he pukepoto ngā hua.
He tipu 1 mita te tupu, he pinerua te tupu o ngā rau, he kaitara, he rauwhero, he kākāriki, he hūmekemeke anō, he pūtaratara ngā tapa, tipu ai i ngā wāhi tāmaru i te kōawaawa.
He tipu 1 mita te tupu.
He tipu e 2 mita te tupu, ka kitea i te taha o te roto, i te repo, i te waikeri rānei, he roroa, he whāiti ngā rau, he hāurauri, he ure te hanga o te puku kākano rere tātā roa te tupu.
He tipu e 2 mita te tupu.
He tipu e 2.5 mita te tupu, he kaitara, he roroa ngā rau, he pua ura tautau tātā roa te tupu, ka motumotu te kiri i tēnei tipu.
He tipu e 45 henemita te tupu, he rau hohoko piko te kāmata, he roroa, he whāiti, he pua kākāriki tāwakawaka whai pōtae.
He tipu e 50 henemita te tupu, he pinerua, he roa tonu, he kārikiuri, he kōratarata ngā rau, he niho tāwhitiwhiti kei ngā tapa o ngā rau, he mā ngā pua pōī te tupu.
He tipu e 50 henemita te tupu, he rau tōpuku whāiti ōna, he tāingoingo whero kei ngā rau, he whero, he kōwhai rānei ngā pua, he whero ngā hua.
He tipu e 50 henemita te tupu.
He tipu e 60 henemita te tupu, he huruhuru te tātā, he rau mati toru tapatoru te āhua, he pūtaratara ngā tapa o ngā rau, he pua kahotea ura te korokoro.
He tipu e 60 henemita te tupu, he rau kororā makiki roroa pā te āhua o te tupu, he tara kei te kāmata o ngā rau, he pua kōwhai tātā tūtika roa te tupu, he tara roroa e rere ana i te tātā pua.
He tipu e 60 henemita te tupu.
He tipu e 65 henemita te tupu, he poto ngā rau, he koi te kāmata, he mā ngā pua pūhui roa te tupu.
He tipu e 65 henemita te tupu.
He tipu e 70 henemita te tupu torotika mai i te whenua, he whāiti, he koi, he whai awa ngā rau, e 2-12 ngā pua e rere ana i tōna tātā kotahi.
He tipu e 70 henemita te tupu torotika mai i te whenua.
He tipu e 80 henemita te tupu, he rau kāwitiwiti roa pā te tupu, he rau tuawhiti, he pua taratara whero tātā roroa te tupu.
He tipu ka kitea i ngā wairepo, i ngā whenua mākū, 1.6 mita te tupu, he mātotoru ngā tātā kahurangi-kākāriki, he parauri ngā pua.
He tipu ka kitea i ngā wairepo, i ngā whenua mākū.
He tipu ka kitea i waenga pārae, i te ngakinga rānei, he pūtiotio ngā rau, ko ētahi momo he ririki, he ngohe ngā pūtiotio, ko ētahi he roa tonu, he koi, whakakopa atu ai te pū o ngā rau ki te tātā, he kōwhai ngā pua, he tino kai te tipu nei i mua i te puāwaitanga, i te pakaritanga.
He tipu ka kitea noatia e uwhi ana i te whenua, he whāiti he kōekoeko ngā rau kākāriki.
He tipu ka tupu ake i te akakōare, he rau kororā whāiti, he roa, he apiapi te tupu o ngā rau i te kāmata o ngā tātā, he pua whero.
He tipu ka tupu ake i te akakōare.
He tipu ka tupu i ngā tāhuna ki tahatai, e 60-90 henemita te tupu, he makiki, he paku kōrino nei ngā rau kōwhai kākāriki; kia maroke ngā rau ka karaka, ka kōwhai muramura te tae, he pai mō te raranga kete, me te tukutuku.
He tipu ka tupu i ngā tāhuna ki tahatai.
He tipu ka tupu ki runga rākau, he kāwitiwiti ngā rau tātā te tupu, he pua mā tātā roa te tupu, he kōwhai te pokapū, he tino kakara te pua.
He tipu ka tupu noa i te wai māori, ka kainga matatia, ka kōhuatia rānei hei kai.
He tipu ka āta whakatupuria e te tangata, whakamahia ai ōna pata hei mahi pāreti, hei mahi parāoa, hei kai anō mā te hōiho, mā te aha atu; ngā pata tonu o te tipu nei.
He tipu kotahi mita te tupu torotika mai i te whenua, he parauri, he pango, he kākāriki rānei tōna tātā kotahi, kei te pito whakarunga ngā pua pōngarengare e rere ana, he unahi te āhua o ngā rau, he tōpuku, he tuawhiti tōna pū, he kai.
He tipu kotahi mita te tupu torotika mai i te whenua.
He tipu kāore e paingia ka tupu noa i te māra, i hea atu, ka tāmi i ngā kai, i ngā aha kua āta whakatōkia atu.
He tipu kāore e whai pua, he huru manu te hanga o ngā rau, he tihenga atua kei te angamate o ngā rau.
He tipu kōekoeko te hanga o ngā whā roa tonu, me he kōwhiuwhiu te tūtū mai o ngā whā i roto i te pā, 1.5 ki te 4 mita te roa o ngā kōrari, he kōkōwai ngā pua, he tūmatohi ngā pākākano.
He tipu kōekoeko te hanga o ngā whā roa tonu.
He tipu nō Rēkohu e 40-60 henemita te tupu, he rau tōpuku nunui, he kārikiuri, he hūmekemeke, he tuawhiti, he kōratarata, he kahurangi, he mā rānei ngā pua, he pōī nunui te tupu runga tātā roa.
He tipu nō Rēkohu e 40-60 henemita te tupu.

He tipu toro nuku i āta waiho ngā hua kia nunui, kia pakari, i whakamaroketia hei oko, hei kawe wai, hei rau atu i te huahua, hei pōito, hei aha atu, hei aha atu, i kainga anō ngā hua ririki i te raumati.

He tipu toro nuku.
He tipu toro toka, toro pari tahataha i te ākau, he rau tuawhiti kākāriki, he ura rānei, he ura ngā tātā, he māwhero ngā pua, he tuawhiti, he ura ngā hua tōpuku te hanga.
He tipu toro toka, toro pari tahataha i te ākau.

He toa; he toa ka hinga i te pakanga.
He toenga maramara rākau pango ka mahue mai ki te ahi mātao.
He tohu (i te pukapuka, i te tuhinga) e whakaatu ana nō hea mai tētahi o ngā kōrero, ngā whakaaro o roto, arā, me toro ki hea ki te kimi i te kōrero ake.
He tohu (pērā i te 1, i te 2), he kupu rānei (pērā i te 'tahi', i te 'rua') ka whakamahia hei tatau i ētahi mea.
He tohu aituā, he tohu kino e pā ana ki ngā moemoeā e tohu ana i tēnei tūāhua.
He tohu atua ka kawea i runga i te waka ina haere i te aumoana.
He tohu atua ka mauria e te tohunga o te ope taua hei whakararu i te hoariri.
He tohu e whakaatu ana i tētahi tau, ka whakamahia hei tatau i ētahi mea.
He tohu e whakaatu ana i tētahi āhuatanga kino kāore anō kia puta.
He tohu e whakaatu ana ka toa i te pakanga.
He tohu hei whakaatu i te tīmatanga, i te mutunga hoki o tētahi rohe whenua.
He tohu hei whakatūpato i te iwi kia kaua e poka noa ki tētahi wāhi, e takahi rānei i te tapu o tētahi wāhi.
He tohu i te wā e hī hāpuku ana, e hī tarakihi ana; ki te pā te ika ki te waka, e kore ētahi atu ika e mau i taua wāhi.
He tohu iti pērā i te tongi, i te porohita iti rānei e mau mai ana ki tētahi mata.
He tohu iti, he whakaaro rehurehu ka takoto hei ārahi i te tangata kia kite i te whakautu tika ki tētahi pātai, ki tētahi panga.
He tohu ka hoatu, he ingoa rānei ka uhia e te Karauna ki te tangata, e ingoatia ai ia mō tana māia, mō te nui rānei o tana whakapau kaha ki tētahi kaupapa.
He tohu ka mahue mai ki te kiri ina mahu te hakihaki, te tūnga, te motunga, tētahi wāhi rānei i wera.
He tohu ka puta hei whakaatu i tētahi āhuatanga pai, āhuatanga kino rānei kāore anō kia puta.
He tohu ka tuhia hei whakaatu i tētahi oro o tētahi reo.
He tohu kino i ngā mahi raranga, i ngā mahi whatu kākahu.
He tohu kino ka tohua e te manu ka pahuhu i te tao.
He tohu kino.
He tohu mō roto i ngā tānga kōrero, he whetū iti te hanga, e tohu ana kei wāhi kē o te whārangi tētahi whakamārama e hāngai ana ki te kōrero i te wāhi i tāia ai te tohu, me ētahi atu āhuatanga. Ko te '*' tōna whakatinanatanga.
He tohu nō te ngākau aroha ka whakapuakina e te tangata.
He tohu nō tētahi atua ka whakatakotoria ki te ara e takahia mai ana e te hoariri, hei whakararu i a ia.
He tohu parauri, he tohu pango rānei pēnei i te tongi, ka puta mai, ka puku mai rānei i te kiri.
He tohu pepa iti, ka whakapiria hei tohu utu i ngā hanga e tonoa ana ki wāhi kē mā te huarahi tuku mēra.
He tohu rite ki te tongi te hanga ka noho mai ki te mutunga o te rerenga kōrero.
He tohu roa, he whāiti, ka tāia ki tētahi mata pēnei i te pepa, i te papa rānei.
He tohu takirua ka karapoti i ētahi kupu motuhake, i ētahi pārongo motuhake i te rerenga kōrero, i te tuhinga rānei, he whakamārama, he tāpiritanga whakaaro te mea o roto. Ko te '(. . .)' tōna whakatinanatanga.
He tohu tino iti, he porohita te hanga.
He tohu tuhituhi ka kuhuna atu ki te kupu pūhui hei hono i ngā wāhanga motuhake o te kupu, ka kuhuna rānei hei tohu i te poronga o tētahi kupu kua taka atu tētahi wāhanga ōna ki te rārangi o raro iho.
He tohu tuhituhi ka kuhuna atu ki te rerenga kōrero hei whakaatu i te hikinga o te whakaaro, ka kuhuna anō ki ngā rārangi hei wehewehe i tēnā, i tēnā o ngā mea i te rārangi. Ko te ',' tōna whakatinanatanga.
He tohu whakamaharatanga ka whakatūria ki te upoko o te rua tūpāpaku kei tōna kotahi tau nei i muri mai i te matenga o te tangata, ka tāraia atu anō he kōrero mōna ki runga.
He tohu, he tau rānei e whakaatu ana i te tapeke i taea mō ētahi mahi i whakaritea e te kaiwhakahaere, e te kaiwhakaako.
He tohu, he ture, he wī, he tohu whenua rānei hei ārai atu, hei kati atu i te rāwaho.
He tohunga ka whakahaere i ētahi āhuatanga motuhake e pā ana ki te māra kūmara.
He tohunga matua.
He tohutohu whai mana e whakatakoto ana he aha ka taea, he aha rānei kāore e taea i tētahi wāhi, i tētahi mahi, i tētahi tākaro.
He toka e tawhiti ana i ētahi atu, e tū motuhake ana i ētahi atu.
He toka iti, he aha atu rānei ka rere mai i tuarangi, kia kuhu mai i te kōhauhau o te ao kua mumura, he hihi aho tōna rite ki te titiro atu.
He toka kei te poho o Papatūānuku, kua rewa i te kaha o te wera i te papanga whakararo o te kirinuku o te ao.
He toka kua rewa i te kaha wera o raro i te whenua, kua puhaina mai, kua tere noa mai rānei i te puia, i tētahi piere rānei.
He toka kāhuarau kōmā, kitea ai i Te Puku-o-Ōtākou. Ko te hōanga te rite ki te titiro atu, engari he mārō ake, he moremore ake, he pīataata ake.
He toka kākāriki tino mārō, he tino taonga nui ki te iwi Māori.
He toka pango nō te poho o Papatūānuku ka hukea hei whāngai i te ahi.
He toka papatahi.
He toka parataiao matanui, he nui te kiripaka o roto. He mōhinuhinu kore, he parauri, he kiwikiwi, he pūmā rānei te tae. Whakamahia nuitia ai hei kauoro, hei tārai toka e oti mai ai he taputapu, he taonga whakapaipai rānei.
He toka puia kahotea, he pōareare, he māmā. Ka hua ake i ngā hū pākaha, e mau ai ngā mirumiru hau ki te tokarewa i te tuhanga mai, toka tonu atu i reira.
He toka puia matarehu he uriuri te tae, he āhua rite ki te ōnewa.
He toka puia matarehu, he mārō, he uriuri te tae, whakamahia nuitia ai hei hanga patu, hei hanga toki me ētahi atu tino taputapu o mua.
He toka puia pango, he mōhinuhinu, he mārō, whakamahia nuitia ai i ngā rā o mua hei tapahi, hei ripiripi.
He toka tino mārō, he toka māeneene.
He tokarewa kua tuhaina rikirikitia mai i te puia, he āhua taratara, he kōputaputa anō.
He toki hei tua rākau.
He toki hei whakaoti haere i te waka.
He toki i hangā ki te uri.
He toki iti hei whakapaipai i ngā taonga pērā i te hoe me te tao.
He toki iti i mauria mai e te Pākehā.
He toki iti, he mea hanga ki te kōhatu; mā te ringa kotahi e hiki.
He toki ka mauria e te ariki hei tohu i tōna mana.
He toki kōhatu e hāngai ana te takoto o te mata ki te kakau.
He toki kōhatu nui.
He toki maitai he rite te hanga o te mata ki te kapu o te ringa o te tangata.
He toki maitai.
He toki pounamu whai mana, he rākau whawhai hoki i hāpaingia e te tangata whai mana.
He toki rino.
He toko ka whakamaua atu ki tētahi hanga hei whakamārō, hei whakapakari, hei whakatorotika i a ia.
He toko kua whakapaipaingia ki te raukura ka toro mai i te ihu o te waka.
He toko rere whakapae ka whakamaua ki ngā pou o te taiapa, hei piringa mō ngā wana.
He tongi e tohu ana i te takotoranga o tētahi mea (i ngā mahi pāngarau).
He toronga roroa e tipu mai ana i te kahiwi o te rākau.
He torongū e kainga ana e te āwhato engari kāore anō i mate, i maroke.
He torongū pango, he whero, he purepure te tupu o ngā huruhuru e rere ana i te tinana, i te āhua tonu o ana kai, he paihana te torongū nei ki te ngārara me te nuinga atu o ngā manu.
He torongū rahi he mā te tae, tērā tonu ko te huhu, he kai tāna i te kahikatea me ētahi atu rākau.
He tote kei roto (o te wai māori).
He toto, he aha atu kua kukū, kua kōpā, kua noho hei pōkurukuru ngohe.
He tuangi kua tangohia mai i te kota.
He tuangi, he kuku, he pipi, he aha atu ka tangohia i ngā anga, ka waiho kia moī i mua i te tunuhanga.
He tuanui poupou te rōnaki.
He tuna 120 henemita te tipu o ngā uwha, e 60 henemita ngā toa, he kōura ōriwa, he ōriwa rānei a runga, he mā, he kiwikiwi, he hiriwa rānei a raro, kia heke ki te moana kua pango a runga, kua hiriwa a raro, kua karapotia ngā karu e te kahurangi.
He tuna 120 henemita te tipu o ngā uwha, e 60 henemita ngā toa.
He tuna e 200 henemita te tipu o ngā uwha, e 70 henemita ngā toa, he parauri pakohe a runga, he kōwhai kiwikiwi a raro, kia heke ki te moana kua pango a runga, kua hiriwa a raro, e taiāwhiotia ana ngā karu e te kahurangi, he tuapuku kei te upoko o ngā uwha pakeke.
He tuna e 200 henemita te tipu o ngā uwha, e 70 henemita ngā toa.
He tuna e heke atu ana i ngā awa ki te au o te moana ki te whānau hua.
He tuna tai e 100-120 henemita te tipu, he kiwikiwi, he pakohe, he pango, he pukepoto rānei te tinana, he nui ngā karu, ka tīmata te urutira i runga ake i ngā pakipaki.
He tuna tai e 100-120 henemita te tipu.
He tuna tai e 75-80 henemita te roa, he kōwhai, he kākāriki rānei tana kiri kōratarata, he upoko nui, kāore he pakipaki, he pakihawa rānei.
He tuna tai e 75-80 henemita te roa.
He tupu whai uhitea, whakatōkia ai e ngā tūpuna i ngā rā o nehe, he rite ki te kūmara te mahinga hei kai.
He tā karamū ka whakamahia hei whakamāmā, hei whakakore atu rānei i ngā taumahatanga o te tapu i runga i te taua.
He tā kāramuramu ka whakamahia i ngā karakia matakite, hei tohu mō ngā iwi, mō ngā hapū rānei e whakarite ana i a rātau mō te pakanga.
He tā rimurimu ka taona i te umu, ka karakiatia, ka kawea i roto i te ihu o te waka i ngā haerenga.
He tā rākau hei whakawhiti atu i te mana o te tangata kua mate, kia pai ai te kawe i taua mana ki āna piki tūranga.
He tā rākau ka poua ki te whenua hei tohu i te tangata e mākuturia ana.
He tā rākau, he māhuri rānei ka hūtia ake i te whenua ka puritia i te ringa i ētahi karakia.
He tāhei huruhuru poto e tipu ana i runga ake i te karu.
He tāhei ka mahia ki te harakeke, ki te aha atu, ka whakamaua ki te hope.
He tāhei ka mahia ki te kirikau, ki te aha atu, hei pupuri, hei whakapaipai noa rānei i te kākahu, hei pupuri rānei i te pū.
He tāhei kei te tapa o te kahu, he rerekē te āhua i tō te roanga atu o te kahu, ko te nuinga hei whakapaipai.
He tāhei pounamu torotika te tinana, e piko ana te pito whakararo.
He tāhei whāiti, he roa.
He tāhoata kua pakaru ririki, e rite ana ki te onepū, ki te kirikiri rānei te rahi.
He tākai, he pouaka rānei mō te tūpāpaku.
He tākaro e noho ai tētahi tokorua me te anga tētahi ki tētahi, ko tā tētahi he whai i te whiu o ngā ringa me ngā mati o te hoa, me te whai anō i ngā kupu ka whakahuatia e ia.
He tākaro e noho tauaro ai tētahi kaitākaro i tētahi, ka tū tētahi o ō rāua ringa me te totoro o ngā mati. Ko tā tētahi he kati i ana karu, ka taki i tana pepeha, ka pana whakamua i tōna ringa me te whai kia noho mai ana mati ki waenganui i ngā mati o tana hoa.
He tākaro e tākiritia ai te ringa, kei pākia e te rākau ka hāua mai e tētahi atu.
He tākaro e whakamahia ai ētahi rākau māmā kua whakataumahatia tētahi pito, kia mārangaranga i te wai.
He tākaro e whakapekea ai te kōhatu pāraharaha i te mata o te wai.
He tākaro e whiua ai he maramara kiri rākau porohita ki te takiwā; he tākaro tēnei ka tākarotia i te taha o tētahi rākau, kia kitea ai nā wai te maramara rākau ka teitei rawa te rere. Ko te tamaiti nāna, ko ia ka toa.
He tākaro mā te tokorua e whakamātau ai tētahi ki te pīhere i te mati o tētahi, ki te pōtari kei te pito o tētahi aho ka mahia ki te tuaka o te whā tī kōuka.
He tākaro mā te tokorua, te tokowhā rānei, e patupatua ai tētahi pōro ki te rākete mai i tētahi taha ki tētahi, kia whiti rawa i tētahi kupenga.
He tākaro nā te tamariki e huna ai ētahi, kia kimihia e tētahi atu, e ētahi atu.
He tākaro nā te tamariki e kapu ai ngā ringa, engari ka waiho te kōroa kia toro tonu. Kua tāpatupatu ngā ringa o te katoa, kua waiata. Ina whakahuatia te 'tara koekoeā' o te ruri, kua mahi katoa kia pā te takoroa ki te ringa o tētahi atu, ka whakahoki ai ki muri o te tuarā. Ki te pā te takoroa o tētahi ki tōu ringa, kua hinga koe.
He tākaro nā te tamariki e pōkaia ai te rau o te tī kouka kia peke atu ai i te matimati.
He tākaro nā te tamariki e tuhia ai he porowhita ki te whenua, ko te wī tēnei. Kua tūtū mai ngā tamariki ki waho o te porowhita, kua tatau tangata te katoa, ā kōwhiria rawatia he kaitiaki mō te wī. Ina kitea, kua tū mai te kaitiaki ki te porowhita, ko tā ētahi atu he whakamātau ki te kuhu atu, me te kore e pākia e te kaitiaki. Ki te pākia, kua noho ia hei hoa mō te kaitiaki o te wī.
He tākaro nā te tamariki e tū tāwhitiwhiti mai ai rātou, ka kōwhiria tētahi hei whai haere i tētahi atu ka kīia ko te kiore. Me mātua whai te kaiwhai i ngā takahanga a te kiore, ā pā rawa tana ringa ki a ia. Inā pā atu te ringa, kua piro te kiore, kua taka atu ki waho, kua noho kiore mai ko tētahi atu tamaiti.
He tākaro tuhi kupu huna ki ētahi tapawhā mā, he rere huapae ētahi, he rere poutū ētahi, he tīwhiri anō ka takoto ki te taha e mōhiotia ai ngā kupu hei kuhu atu.
He tākaro ā-ringa mā te tokorua, he kaikaranga tētahi, he kaiwhai tētahi. Ka whiua tahitia e rāua ō rāua ringa, me te whai a te kaikaranga kia mau tana hoa e whiu tahi ana i ōna ringa ki tāna i whiu ai.
He tākohu i te kōhauhau ka huri hei hukapapa kōmāmā, he whā mā te hanga i te takanga iho ki te whenua.
He tākohu kua pā atu ki tētahi mata makariri, kua huri hei pata wai.
He tāmure e paku tonu ana, ehara i te poto engari kāore i nunui.
He tāmure e paku tonu ana.
He tāmure e pīpī tonu ana.
He tāne e rite ana ngā mātua, tētahi rānei o ngā mātua ki ō tētahi wahine kua tohua; he tāne nō te whānau nui tonu kei te whakapaparanga o tētahi wahine kua tohua.
He tāne e tamariki tonu ana.
He tāne ka moe i tō whaea i muri i te mahuetanga tūturu o rāua ko tō pāpā tupu, i muri i te matenga rānei o tō pāpā tupu.
He tāne ka noho tupuna ki a koe.
He tāne moe tāne, he wahine moe wahine rānei.
He tāne noho takakau, e noho tahi ana rānei ki tētahi whānau.
He tāne pakeke ake i tētahi atu tāne e rite tahi ana ō rāua mātua, tētahi rānei o ngā mātua.
He tāne taiohi.
He tāne taipakeke kua roa ngā rā ki te ao.
He tāne tamariki ake i tētahi atu tāne e rite tahi ana ō rāua mātua, tētahi rānei o ngā mātua.
He tāne, ahakoa te pakeke.
He tāne, he taitama rānei.
He tāne, he wahine kua mate tana hoa rangatira, ka mutu kāore anō kia whai hoa rangatira hou.
He tāne, he wahine rānei ko ia e āta whakatipu ana i te tamaiti a tētahi atu.
He tāne, he wahine rānei kua neke atu ōna tau i ō te tamariki, i ō te taiohi, engari kāore anō kia koroua rawa, kia kuia rawa.
He tāne, he wahine rānei kua taipakeke, kua roa ngā rā ki te ao.
He tāne, he wahine rānei.
He tānga e whakaatu ana i a Papatūānuku, i tētahi wāhanga rānei ōna, e tohu ana kei whea ngā huarahi, ngā tāone, ngā awa, ngā maunga, ngā aha atu.
He tānga kupu whaimana e whakatūturu ana i te ekenga ki tētahi taumata, i te ū ki tētahi ture, i te pono rānei o tētahi āhuatanga.
He tānga moko e tata atu ana ki ngā taringa.
He tānga moko i ngā pāpāringa, kei runga ake i te pūtaringa me te paepae.
He tānga moko i ngā taha o te ihu.
He tānga moko i ngā taha o te waha.
He tānga moko i raro i ngā karu.
He tānga moko i raro i ngā tukemata.
He tānga moko i te kauae o te wahine.
He tānga moko i te kikowhiti.
He tānga moko i te kumu, kei waenganui i te rape.
He tānga moko i te kūhā.
He tānga moko i te pokapū o te rae.
He tānga moko i te pāpāringa.
He tānga moko i te rae.
He tānga moko i te taha o te ihu.
He tānga moko i te takapū o te waewae.
He tānga moko ka huri i te kawititanga o te ringa.
He tānga moko ka rere i ngā pongāihu, ka huri i ngā pī o te waha ki ngā taha e rua o te kauae.
He tānga moko kei ngā pī o te waha o te wahine.

He tānga moko kei runga ake i ngā tukemata.
He tānga moko kei runga ake i te pokapū o te rae.
He tānga moko kei te kauwae.
He tānga moko kei te kūhā, kei te ringa rānei, e rite ana ki te tūātea o te moana.
He tānga moko kei te ngutu o runga.
He tānga moko kei te pito o te ihu, kei te ngutu o runga rānei.
He tānga moko kei te rae o te wahine.
He tānga moko kei te tiki, arā, te wāhanga whakararo o te tuarā.
He tānga moko kei waenga i ngā tukemata.
He tānga moko roa kei te ringa.
He tānga māmā e whakaatu ana i te hanga, i te takoto rānei o tētahi mea.
He tānga nui, he whakaahua, he kupu, he tohu anō pea kei runga, hei whakatairanga i tētahi mea, hei whakarākei anō.
He tānga o te āhua o tētahi mea, he mea hopu ki te kāmera.
He tānga o te āhua o tētahi whare kāore anō i hangaia, e whakaatu ana i ōna āhuatanga matua.
He tānga whakaahua kotahi, hei whakakata, hei whakatoi, hei whakaoho kōrero, ka whakaputaina i ngā nūpepa, i ngā moheni rānei; he raupapa whakaahua e whakaata pūrākau ana.
He tānga whārangi nui tonu ko te nuinga ka puta ia rangi, ia wiki rānei, ka noho tangatanga tonu ngā whārangi kua pōkaihia ki waenganui, he tānga hei whakaputa i ngā rongo kōrero o te wā, i te pānui, i te aha atu.
He tānga, he tae kei tētahi mata, ka mahia ki te kōkōwai, ki te aha atu.
He tānga, he āhua e tohu ana i tētahi kamupene, i tētahi whakahaere, i tētahi rōpū, e whakaatu ana ko wai rātou.
He tāngata e tū matatira mai ana.
He tāngata ka huihui tahi ki te karakia.
He tāngata tokomaha ka whakawhāiti mai ki tētahi wāhi mō tētahi kaupapa kua whakaritea.
He tāngata tokomaha tonu, engari kāore e mōhiotia ana tokohia rawa.
He tāniko ka tuia atu ki te kākahu, ki te ipu rānei.
He tāone tino nui.
He tāpaenga kai tapu.
He tāpaenga ki ngā atua e pā ana ki te waka hou.
He tāpaetanga ki tētahi atua.
He tārawa whakanikoniko i te reke o te mere.
He tāruatanga o tētahi tānga kōrero, whakaahua rānei ka hurihia hei karere hiko, kātahi ka tukuna ā-waea ki wāhi kē; te mīhini ka tuku i tēnei hanga.
He tātai whetū e rite ana ki te waka te hanga, ko Rehua tētahi o ngā whetū rongonui o roto. Ki ētahi ko tēnei kāhui te tauihu o Te Waka-o-Tamarēreti.
He tātai whetū e rite ana ki tētahi waka rahi te hanga.
He tātai whetū e rite ana ki tētahi waka rahi te hanga. Ko Māhutonga te punga, ko Te Waka-o-Mairerangi te tauihu, ko Tautoru te taurapa.
He tātai whetū nui ki te tonga e rite ana te āhua ki te rīpeka.
He tātai whetū.
He tātai whetū. E toru ngā whetū e rārangi mai ana i raro i a Puanga, i te taurapa o Te-Waka-o-Tamarēreti, ā, he rārangi whetū anō i te taha. Koinei te 'kakau,' te 'tuke' rānei kei ētahi o ōna ingoa.
He tātua e mau ai ngā pūkohu nei i ngā rā o mua.
He tātua nō te tohunga ka whītikiria mō ētahi o āna mahi.
He tātua roa ka mahia ki te harakeke, he ringa pea te whānui, ka tāpekatia ki te tinana hei whakapuru rākau whawhai.
He tātā mātotoru huapae te tupu i te whenua, ka wana ake te tipu hou i ngā pūkanohi.
He tāwhiti hei hopu kāhu, arā, he rākau tokorera ka poua ki te whenua, ka herea he koromāhanga ki runga; te koromāhanga o te taputapu nei.
He tāwhiti hopu kāhu, arā he rākau tokorera ka poua ki te whenua, ka herea he koromāhanga ki runga.
He tēpa kua tāia ki ōna anō waeine hei ine i tētahi mea.
He tīmatanga kōrero e tohu ana e hē ana, kāore rānei e pono ana te kōrero ka whai i muri tonu mai.
He tīpare; he momo tīpare ka whiria ki te whītau hei whakamau atu i te huruhuru manu, i te huruhuru kurī rānei ki te upoko o te taiaha, hei whakapaipai; ka here (i tētahi mea) ki tēnei hanga.
He tōiriiritanga ka rere i te hau takiwā, i tētahi atu hanga rānei, ka rangona e te taringa; he mea ka rangona e te taringa.
He tōpana e kumea whakarotohia ai tētahi hanga whai papatipu ki te pūtahi o Papatūānuku, ki te pūtahi rānei o tētahi atu ao tuarangi.
He tōtara tāne.
He tōtara wahine.
He tūingoa e tohu ana i tētahi wā.
He tūingoa e tohu ana i tētahi wāhi.
He tūmahi e whakaahua ana i tētahi mahi kua mahia, ka mahia rānei, i tētahi āhuatanga kua eke, ka eke rānei.
He tūmahi ka noho hāngū tonu i roto i te rerenga kōrero, e kore rawa e makere mai tōna pīmuri hāngū.
He tūmahi ka noho motuhake mai te mahi e kōrerotia ana ki te mea nāna te mahi, kāore e whiti rawa, e pā rawa ki tētahi atu hanga.
He tūmahi ka whiti rawa, ka pā rawa te mahi e kōrerotia ana ki tētahi atu hanga, kāore e noho motuhake mai ki te mea nāna te mahi.
He tūmomo whakairo e rite ana te āhua ki tēnei momo taniwha.
He tūnga, he takotoranga rānei e anga ana ki tētahi ahunga.
He tūpāpaku kua whakamaroketia, kua rongoāhia i mua i te whakanohoia mai ki tōna rua, ki tōna ana.
He tūranga i te whare pāremata, i te kaunihera, i tētahi atu rōpū rānei ka pōtihia e te tokomaha.
He tūtakinga nā ētahi ope taua e rua, neke atu, e whawhai ai tētahi taha ki tētahi.
He tūwiri e rua ōna aho hei kukume ki tētahi taha, ki tētahi taha, kia huri ai.
He tūāpapa hakahaka e tīraha mai ai te tūpāpaku.
He tūāpapa tārewa e tū mai ai te tāngata ki te kawe i ngā mahi a rēhia.
He ua e ākina ana e te hau.
He ua ka rere iho i te ata tū.
He ua ka rukea iho i ngā kapua, he kōpatapata mano tini āhua nui tonu.
He ua ka āta rere ā-kōpatapata moroiti nei.
He ua kei roto anō he haupapa, he hukarere e rewa haere ana i te rerenga mai ki te whenua.
He ua kua totoka ka rere iho i ngā kapua pērā i te ua.
He ua kōehuehu e ākina ana e te hau.
He ua kōpatapata moroiti ka āta rere iho i ngā kapua.
He ua kōpatapata moroiti māmā te rere iho, he wā poto kua mao anō.
He ua kōpatapata moroiti māmā te rere iho, ka mao, ka rere iho, ka mao, ka rere iho.
He ua kōpatapata nunui ka rukea iho i ngā kapua.
He ua māmā te rere iho i ngā rā o te raumati.
He ua nehu auroa.
He ua rere tika iho i te kore e pupuhi o te hau.
He ua āta rere rehu mai i ngā kapua ki te whenua.
He uaua rahi kei mua o te wāhi whakarunga o te ringa, māna e piko ai te ringa i te tuke.
He uaua rahi kei mua o te wāhi whakarunga o te waewae, māna e toro ai te waewae.
He uaua rahi kei muri o te wāhi whakarunga o te ringa, māna e toro ai te ringa.
He uhi mō tētahi mea (pērā i te pouaka, i te kōhua) ka taea te tango iho, te hiki ake rānei.
He uira kei tawhiti.
He uku teatea.

He whare tūmatanui, he whare huihui mā te hapori.
He whare whai maihi i te mataihi.
